### [1] [MultiRef-Compass: Towards Comprehensive Evaluation of Multi-Reference-to-Audio-Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14189)
*Xiaohan Zhang,Yuqing Wen,Junlin Chen,Yuqi Tang,Yiting He,Lizhuo Shao,Weiming Zhu,Tengfei Liu,Yang Shi,Jialu Chen,Yuanxing Zhang,Huaxiong Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MultiRef-Compass，一个针对多参考音频视频生成的统一基准，涵盖多视角主体保留、多实体绑定和人-物-场景组合，包含350个精心构建的样本，并定义了四个评估维度（基础质量、参考一致性、音视频一致性、指令遵循）及14个子指标，结合自动评估与MLLM作为裁判的可审计评估框架，揭示现有系统在多个维度仍有巨大提升空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准主要关注文本驱动生成、单参考主体保持或孤立音视频对齐，未充分探索多参考到音视频生成（MR2AV）这一新兴领域，而该任务需模型在生成同步视听内容时联合推理多个参考信息，忠实保留每个参考并正确组合多个参考实体形成连贯视听事件。

Method: 构建可扩展且可控的资产组合流水线，生成350个高质量样本；设计包含四个维度（基础质量、参考一致性、音视频一致性、指令遵循）的评估协议，结合自动指标与增强重评的MLLM-as-a-Judge框架，实现可审计的评估。

Result: 在8个代表性MR2AV系统上进行的广泛实验表明，各系统在多个评估维度上均存在显著改进空间，验证了新基准的有效性与必要性，确立了MultiRef-Compass作为未来MR2AV研究的基础。

Conclusion: MultiRef-Compass为多参考音视频生成提供了首个统一、可解释、可扩展的评估基准，推动该领域从单一任务向复杂多参考协同生成演进，为后续研究奠定坚实基础。

Abstract: Multi-reference-to-audio-video (MR2AV) generation aims to generate coherent audio-video content conditioned on multiple references and textual instructions. Existing benchmarks mainly focus on text-driven generation, single-reference subject preservation, or isolated audio-video alignment, leaving the emerging MR2AV setting largely unexplored. Compared with these settings, MR2AV requires models to jointly reason over multiple references while generating synchronized visual and audio content. Models must not only preserve each reference faithfully but also correctly bind and compose multiple referenced entities into coherent audio-visual events. To address this gap, we introduce MultiRef-Compass, a unified benchmark for MR2AV generation. It comprises $350$ carefully curated samples constructed through a scalable and controllable asset-composition pipeline, covering multi-view subject preservation, multi-entity binding, and human-object-scene composition. To provide interpretable assessment, MultiRef-Compass defines an evaluation protocol with four dimensions: Basic Quality, Reference Consistency, Audio-Visual Consistency, and Instruction Following, using 14 sub-metrics. MultiRef-Compass integrates automatic metrics with a rejudging-enhanced MLLM-as-a-Judge framework, enabling scalable and auditable evaluation of both perceptual fidelity and reference-conditioned composition. Extensive experiments on eight representative MR2AV systems reveal substantial room for improvement across multiple evaluation dimensions, underscoring the need for a comprehensive benchmark and positioning MultiRef-Compass as a foundation for future MR2AV research.

</details>


### [2] [Inference-Time Concept Suppression and Video-Centric Evaluation for Text-to-Video Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14194)
*Wenxuan Chen,Wenjie Feng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SIRUS是一种无需训练的推理时框架，用于文本到视频生成中的概念级去学习，能够有效移除目标概念同时保留非目标内容和视频时序结构。通过定位并抑制目标相关提示信息，在不更新模型参数的情况下实现概念擦除。引入了面向视频的评估体系，综合衡量遗忘效果、非目标保留、视频质量、抗规避能力和效率。在CogVideoX上，SIRUS在平均遗忘成功率（70.4%）和帧残留率（25.7%）方面优于VideoEraser，且视频质量下降更小（VBench从-0.043降至-0.016），表现出最优的遗忘-质量权衡。在Wan2.2上的迁移实验表明其可泛化至多种主流视频生成模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到视频生成模型难以可控地移除特定概念，尤其当目标概念在多帧中持续存在时，需在不破坏非目标内容与时间连贯性的前提下实现精准擦除。传统方法在遗忘效果与视频质量之间难以平衡，亟需一种高效、通用且无需训练的去学习框架。

Method: SIRUS采用推理时干预策略，基于目标概念的文本别名定位其在生成过程中的提示证据，并在采样阶段动态抑制目标表达；不修改文本编码器或去噪网络，保持原模型不变。结合视频级失败标准、帧级残留统计、成对保留分析、VBench质量评估及部署开销测量，构建全面评估体系。

Result: 在五个安全、物体和风格概念上，SIRUS在CogVideoX上达到70.4%平均遗忘成功率与25.7%平均帧命中率，显著优于VideoEraser（44.4%/47.2%）；VBench质量下降由-0.043减少至-0.016，实现最佳遗忘-质量平衡。跨模型迁移实验显示其在Wan2.2上具有强泛化能力。

Conclusion: SIRUS为文本到视频生成提供了高效的无训练概念去学习方案，兼具高遗忘效果、强非目标保留能力与良好视频质量，且具备跨模型泛化潜力，推动了可控视频生成的发展。

Abstract: Text-to-video (T2V) generators can synthesize realistic and temporally coherent videos, but controllably removing a target concept from a generator remains difficult.
  Unlike text-to-image concept erasure, T2V unlearning must suppress a target concept that may persist across frames while preserving non-target subjects, actions, scenes, and temporal structure.
  We propose \textbf{SIRUS}, a training-free inference-time framework for concept-level T2V unlearning.
  Given textual aliases of a target concept, SIRUS localizes target-related prompt evidence and suppresses target expression during sampling, without updating the text encoder or denoising network.
  We further introduce a video-oriented evaluation framework for T2V unlearning that separately measures target forgetting, non-target preservation, video quality, jailbreak robustness, and efficiency, using video-level failure criteria, frame-level residue statistics, paired preservation analysis, VBench-based quality diagnostics, and deployment overhead measurement.
  Across five safety, object, and style concepts on CogVideoX, SIRUS reaches 70.4\% average forgetting success and 25.7\% average frame hit, compared with 44.4\% / 47.2\% for VideoEraser, while reducing the average VBench quality drop from -0.043 to -0.016, yielding the strongest forgetting-quality trade-off among fully evaluated baselines.
  Transfer experiments on Wan2.2 further suggest that SIRUS generalizes across modern T2V backbones.

</details>


### [3] [KeyFrame-Compass: Towards Comprehensive Evaluation of Keyframe-Conditioned Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14202)
*Yuqi Tang,Tengfei Liu,Yizheng Lai,Yuran Wang,Yang Shi,Wanshun Su,Zhuoran Zhang,Qixun Wang,Xiaohan Zhang,Xinlei Yu,Xuehai Bai,Xuanyu Zhu,Bohan Zeng,Bozhou Li,Shujie Li,Yifan Dai,Yujie Wei,Shixuan Liu,Haotian Wang,Jialu Chen,Yuanxing Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出首个针对关键帧条件视频生成的综合性基准KeyFrame-Compass，涵盖386个精心设计的样本，覆盖多种应用领域、视频结构、提示粒度、条件格式和关键帧密度。引入自动化评估框架，分解关键帧执行为六个指标（存在性、保真度、时间顺序、定位、持续性和唯一性），并结合基于证据的多模态大模型判断与专用感知模型评估整体视频质量。实验发现当前模型在忠实再现关键帧与自然视频合成间存在明显权衡，且随着关键帧密度增加性能下降，多数开源模型无法正确理解时间有序的关键帧序列输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关键帧条件视频生成模型在忠实再现指定关键帧方面表现不明确，缺乏系统性评估工具，亟需一个全面的基准来揭示其能力边界与局限性。

Method: 构建包含多维度变量的基准数据集，设计自动化评估框架，分解关键帧执行为六项具体指标，并结合多模态大模型与专用感知模型进行综合评价。

Result: 九个代表性视频生成系统在测试中暴露出显著缺陷：在关键帧忠实度与视频自然性之间存在权衡；高密度关键帧条件下性能下降；多数开源模型无法正确解析时间有序的关键帧网格输入。

Conclusion: 当前关键帧条件视频生成技术仍面临核心挑战，需在模型设计上兼顾精确控制与生成流畅性，未来工作应聚焦于提升对复杂关键帧序列的理解与执行能力。

Abstract: Video generation increasingly relies on keyframe-based workflows, where creators specify a sequence of reference images to guide generation. Although recent models support multi-keyframe conditioning, it remains unclear whether they can faithfully reproduce the prescribed keyframes while maintaining overall video quality. We present KeyFrame-Compass, the first comprehensive benchmark for evaluating keyframe-conditioned video generation. The benchmark contains 386 carefully curated samples spanning three application domains, two video structures, two prompt granularities, two conditioning formats, and four keyframe densities, enabling controlled analysis under diverse generation settings. We further introduce an automated evaluation framework that jointly measures keyframe execution and overall video quality. Specifically, we decompose keyframe execution into six complementary metrics covering presence, fidelity, temporal ordering, localization, persistence, and uniqueness, while assessing overall video quality through evidence-grounded MLLM judgments augmented with specialized perception models. Experiments on nine representative video generation systems reveal several fundamental limitations. Current models exhibit a clear trade-off between faithful keyframe execution and natural video synthesis. Their performance further degrades as keyframe constraints become denser and most open-source models also fail to interpret storyboard-grid inputs as temporally ordered keyframe sequences.

</details>


### [4] [SeeSE3: Emergence of 3D Space in Vision Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14228)
*Caroline Chen,Sayna Ebrahimi,Fedor Kitashov,Ming-Hsuan Yang,Leonidas Guibas,Viorica Pătrăucean,Maks Ovsjanikov*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文探讨视觉基础模型是否构建了反映三维欧几里得空间内在性质的表征。不同于以往通过回归图像中心量（如深度或法向）来探测视觉特征的3D感知，本文从拓扑和几何角度评估视觉特征空间与欧几里得变换群SE(3)之间的关系。提出两种探测方法：互邻域度量以衡量特征邻域与空间拓扑的一致性，以及Poincaré Adapter用于测试相机运动几何在静态场景中潜在位移的线性可访问性。结果表明，即使未接受直接3D监督或主动代理训练的自监督视觉模型，其潜在子空间也与三维欧几里得空间存在强烈相关性。基于此发现，提出一类新的‘潜在空间导航’技术，可在潜在空间内实现视觉里程计和定位，无需显式三维重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究视觉基础模型是否隐含对三维欧几里得空间结构的理解，突破传统依赖图像中心量回归的3D感知评估方式，寻找更本质的空间表征证据。

Method: 提出互邻域度量和Poincaré Adapter两种探测方法，分别从拓扑一致性与几何线性可访问性角度评估视觉特征空间与SE(3)群的关系。

Result: 自监督视觉模型的潜在子空间与三维欧几里得空间具有显著相关性，表明其具备内在的3D空间理解能力。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了自监督视觉模型在潜在空间中蕴含丰富的3D结构信息，为无需显式3D重建的视觉导航提供了新范式，推动了对视觉表征本质的理解。

Abstract: In this paper, we ask whether vision foundation models construct representations that reflect the intrinsic properties of 3D Euclidean space. Unlike previous works that probe 3D awareness of vision features by regressing image-centric quantities such as depth or normals, we investigate the relation between the structure of the space of visual features and the group of Euclidean transformations $SE(3)$. We propose a set of probes to evaluate this relation from both topological and geometric perspectives: a mutual neighborhood metric that measures the alignment between feature neighborhoods and spatial topology, and a Poincaré Adapter to test the linear accessibility of the geometry of camera motion from latent displacements in static scenes. We show that self-supervised vision models, which, in principle, have not been trained with direct 3D supervision or active agency, possess latent subspaces that are remarkably strongly correlated with three-dimensional Euclidean space, when probed correctly. Building on this insight we propose a new class of "Latent-Space Navigation" techniques that perform visual odometry and localization purely in the latent space, bypassing the need for explicit 3D reconstruction.

</details>


### [5] [3D Lane Detection with Odometry for High-Speed Vehicle Racing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14248)
*Omoruyi Atekha,John Subosits,Marcus Greiff*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于赛车场景下3D车道线检测的新数据集，包含超过25万张来自多摄像头和惯性测量的数据图像，旨在解决高速、极端道路几何条件下的车道检测问题。研究对比了多种3D车道检测方法，并提出改进方案，实现接近300Hz的处理速度，同时保持高精度。通过融合惯性测量与多摄像头集成预测，显著提升性能：F1分数提高3个百分点，近车区域平均绝对误差（MAE）降低30%以上。实际车辆部署中，F1分数超过0.9，横向MAE低于0.18米。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有车道检测研究主要集中在常规驾驶场景，而赛车场景因高速行驶和复杂道路几何，对车道检测提出了更高要求，但相关研究较少。因此，亟需针对赛车场景构建专门的数据集并开发高效、高精度的3D车道检测方法。

Method: 引入一个包含多摄像头图像与惯性测量数据的新数据集；设计可支持近300Hz处理速度的3D车道检测框架；采用多摄像头集成策略；利用惯性测量数据进行预积分，联合回归时空上的道路几何结构。

Result: 相比BevLaneDet等方法，所提方法在F1分数上提升3个百分点，近车区域平均绝对误差降低30%以上；车辆实测中达到F1分数>0.9，横向误差<0.18m。

Conclusion: 本研究通过构建专用数据集与优化算法，实现了赛车场景下高效、高精度的3D车道检测，验证了多模态感知与集成预测的有效性，为高速自动驾驶系统提供了可靠的技术支持。

Abstract: Lane boundary detection is a critical component in autonomous driving systems and has been rigorously studied in regular driving scenarios. However, it is less explored in vehicle racing, where the car moves at higher speeds across more extreme road geometries. To study this problem, we introduce a new dataset for 3D lane detection in racing, featuring >$250$k images from multiple camera feeds and inertial measurements taken with a Lexus LC 500 driving on a closed circuit. With this dataset, we compare various approaches to 3D lane detection and propose modifications that permit frames to be processed at rates of almost 300Hz while retaining high predictive performance in the racing application. This facilitates a multi-camera ensemble approach that is validated on hardware. We show that sensing modalities such as inertial measurements can be leveraged for pre-integration to regress road geometries over both cameras and time, yielding improvements in key metrics. Compared to methods such as BevLaneDet, adding odometry and ensemble predictions improves the F1 score by 3 points and reduces near-vehicle mean absolute errors (MAEs) by $>30 \%$. We show F1 scores $>$0.9 and lateral MAEs of $<$0.18m in vehicle deployments.

</details>


### [6] [MonteRET: AI Agent Enhancing Multimodal LLMs with Multi-granularity Knowledge Retrieval for Chest CT Report Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14264)
*Yi Lin,Yihao Ding,Elana Benishay,Elefterios Trikantzopoulos,David Nauheim,Hanley Ong,Jiang Bian,Hua Xu,Yuzhe Yang,George Shih,Yifan Peng*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MonteRET 是一种区域感知的检索增强框架，用于生成胸部CT报告中的发现部分。它结合了全局CT特征与局部解剖表示，通过预测的医学状况和区域级视觉-语言对齐来检索临床相关知识，并通过知识引导的报告重写代理改进初始报告。在包含24,128个CT扫描的公开数据集上训练，并在公开和外部测试集上评估，结果显示其在报告质量、语义相似性和临床有效性方面优于基线和其他先进方法，尤其在召回率上提升显著，表明更少遗漏发现。放射科住院医师的人工评估也支持该模型的优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胸部CT报告生成面临挑战，因为临床准确的报告需要对整个体积的理解以及对局部解剖发现的精确描述。现有方法在捕捉局部细节和临床相关性方面存在不足。

Method: MonteRET 结合全局CT特征与区域级解剖表示，利用预测的医学条件和区域级视觉-语言对齐进行临床知识检索，并通过知识引导的报告重写代理优化报告输出。

Result: 在公开和外部测试集上，MonteRET 在报告质量、语义相似性和临床有效性方面均优于基线和当前最先进方法，特别是在召回率上表现突出，人类专家评估也显示其优势。

Conclusion: MonteRET 有效提升了胸部CT报告生成的质量与临床实用性，尤其在减少遗漏发现方面表现出色，具有良好的应用前景。

Abstract: Automated chest CT report generation remains challenging because clinically faithful reporting requires both whole-volume understanding and accurate description of localized anatomical findings. Here we developed and retrospectively evaluated MonteRET, a region-aware retrieval-enhanced framework for generating chest CT findings sections. MonteRET integrates global CT features with region-level anatomical representations, retrieves clinically relevant knowledge using predicted medical conditions and region-level vision-language alignment, and refines initial reports through a knowledge-guided report rewriting agent. We trained our model on a public cohort with 24,128 CT scans from RadGenome-ChestCT. We evaluated MonteRET on the public RadGenome-ChestCT test set of 1,564 CT scans and an external cohort of 82 CT scans from NewYork-Presbyterian/Weill Cornell Medical Center. MonteRET improved report quality, semantic similarity, and clinical efficacy compared with a matched baseline and several state-of-the-art methods. Gains were most pronounced for recall, suggesting fewer omitted findings. Human expert evaluation by radiology residents also favored MonteRET.

</details>


### [7] [XCT-SAM: Sequential Parameter-Efficient Domain Adaptation of SAM for Industrial XCT Defect Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14287)
*Md Mahedi Hasan,Md Mushfiqur Rahaman,Alan Pachkovskiy,Imtiaz Ahmed,Jeremy Dawson,Srinjoy Das*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出XCT-SAM，一种用于增材制造X射线计算机断层扫描缺陷分割的序列化参数高效适应框架。通过在合金微观结构数据集上先微调Conv-LoRA适配器，再迁移至XCT图像，逐步缩小领域差距。使用低秩r=2的Conv-LoRA适配器注入卷积空间归纳偏置，仅训练约415万参数，保持99%以上模型冻结。在分布外CycleGAN-XCT基准和真实NIST XCT扫描上均优于零样本SAM及其他领域自适应基线，显著提升交并比与Dice分数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AM XCT图像中的缺陷分割面临严重类别不平衡和跨扫描条件的大分布偏移问题。现有基础模型如SAM虽具强大通用分割先验，但其自然图像预训练难以有效迁移到AM XCT域，因缺陷表现为细微的非语义微结构异常，且真实XCT标注数据稀缺，限制了直接适应。

Method: 提出XCT-SAM框架，采用两阶段参数高效适应策略：首先在合金微观结构数据集上微调Conv-LoRA适配器以引入卷积空间归纳偏置；随后将训练好的适配器迁移至XCT图像，实现渐进式领域对齐。利用低秩适配器（rank r=2）仅更新少量参数（约415万），同时冻结超过99%的原始模型参数。

Result: XCT-SAM在分布外的CycleGAN-XCT基准和真实NIST XCT扫描数据上均表现优异，显著超越零样本SAM和其他领域自适应基线，获得最高平均交并比（IoU）和Dice系数，验证了中间领域适应与参数高效适配在工业级XCT缺陷分割中的有效性。

Conclusion: XCT-SAM通过参数高效、分阶段的领域适应策略，有效缓解了自然图像预训练模型在工业XCT场景下的性能下降问题，为复杂制造质量检测提供了可扩展、高精度的解决方案。代码已公开。

Abstract: Defect segmentation in additive manufacturing (AM) X-ray computed tomography (XCT) images remains challenging due to severe class imbalance and large distribution shifts across scan conditions. Although recent foundation models such as the Segment Anything Model (SAM) provide strong general-purpose segmentation priors, their natural-image pre-training transfers poorly to the AM XCT domain, where defects appear as subtle non-semantic microstructural anomalies. Moreover, adapting SAM to the AM domain is further limited by the large domain gap and scarcity of labeled real XCT data. We present XCT-SAM, a sequential parameter-efficient adaptation framework for AM XCT defect segmentation. Instead of adapting SAM directly from natural images to XCT data, we first fine-tune Conv-LoRA adapters on an alloy-microstructure dataset and subsequently transfer the adapted model to XCT images, progressively bridging the domain gap. Using Conv-LoRA adapters with rank r=2, the framework injects convolutional spatial inductive bias into SAM's backbone while training approximately 4.15M parameters and keeping over 99% of the model frozen. We evaluate XCT-SAM on out-of-distribution CycleGAN-XCT benchmarks and real-world NIST XCT scans. Across both settings, XCT-SAM consistently outperforms zero-shot SAM and other domain-adapted SAM baselines, achieving the best overall IoU and Dice scores. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of intermediate domain adaptation with parameter-efficient adapters for industrial XCT defect segmentation. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/Mahedi-61/XCT-SAM.git

</details>

Abstract: In this paper we propose DCVC-Mamba (DCVC-MB), a neural video codec framework for B-frame coding. Our approach incorporates an IBP frame strategy for low-delay B-frame coding, a spatio-temporal fusion model based on state-space models for bidirectional temporal prediction, and an entropy-aware skipping mechanism that selectively omits coding certain latents to reduce entropy coding times. In addition to our model contributions we also implement two inference-time strategies that enhance compression performance. Experimental evaluation shows that DCVC-MB compares favorably to existing NVCs and traditional codecs. Method: 构建基于受控扰动的配对视觉场景，生成涵盖语义变化归因与定量比较的推理任务；使用GRPO-lite结合反向折扣分配（BDA）的强化学习方法进行微调，消除KL正则化以促进更强策略优化，并将更多奖励分配给推理后期形成结论的关键步骤。

Abstract: Vision Language Models (VLMs) demonstrate strong perceptual abilities but remain limited in tasks requiring analytical reasoning across multiple visual states, such as multi-image comparison, change detection, and multi-step visual inference. These capabilities are critical for real-world multimodal applications where reasoning must be grounded in systematic differences between visual contexts. However, existing benchmarks rarely require both explicit visual comparison and analytical reasoning, leaving this capability underexplored. To address this gap, we introduce SD-MAR (Synthetic Data for Multi-image Analytical Reasoning), a framework for training and evaluating VLMs on multi-image analytical reasoning. ### [10] [MixCompress: Mixture of Experts for Variable Rate Learned Image Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14334)
*Calvin-Khang Ta,Praneet Singh,Tong Shao,Peng Yin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MixCompress提出一种基于稀疏结构专化的统一可变比特率（VBR）框架，通过稀疏门控专家混合（MoE）路由缓解梯度冲突，并引入混合深度（MoD）扩展以动态调整模型容量，结合条件辅助变换（CAT）实现子带能量的动态调制，从而在保持计算效率的同时实现卓越的压缩性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可变比特率图像压缩方法因共享主干网络导致特征纠缠，尤其在低比特率下平滑梯度与高频率纹理细节保护之间存在冲突，限制了性能提升。

Method: 采用稀疏门控专家混合（MoE）减少梯度冲突，引入混合深度（MoD）动态扩展模型容量，并结合条件辅助变换（CAT）进行子带能量的动态调节，构建分层可扩展架构。

Result: MixCompress不仅达到甚至超越单速率优化基线，还在计算效率与压缩性能间建立了新的帕累托前沿。

Conclusion: MixCompress通过稀疏结构专业化和动态容量扩展，有效解决了传统VBR方法中的特征纠缠问题，实现了高效且高性能的统一图像压缩框架。

Abstract: Learned image compression (LIC) is bottlenecked by the need to store independent models for each rate-distortion operating point. Existing variable bit-rate (VBR) methods aim to reduce this overhead via dense parameter modulation, but forcing a shared backbone to approximate divergent mappings causes severe feature entanglement. Specifically, low-rate smoothing gradients inherently conflict with the preservation of high-frequency textural details, leading to sub-optimal performance. To resolve this, we propose MixCompress, a unified VBR framework based on sparse structural specialization. While sparsely gated Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) routing successfully mitigates gradient conflict, it operates on a fixed computational budget. To address the increased representational demands of higher bit-rates we introduce a Mixture-of-Depths (MoD) extension to dynamically scale model capacity. Combined with Conditional Auxiliary Transforms (CAT) for dynamic sub-band energy modulation, our hierarchical framework effectively dynamically scales capacity. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that MixCompress not only matches individually optimized single-rate baselines but can even surpass them, establishing a new Pareto frontier for computationally efficient image coding.

### [11] [Beyond scalar losses: calibrating segmentation models via gradient vector field surgery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14338)
*Laurin Lux,Alexander H. Berger,Moritz Knolle,Daniel Rückert,Johannes C. Paetzold*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的梯度视角来理解基于区域的损失函数（如Dice损失）在医学图像分割中导致预测过度自信的问题，并通过修改梯度向量场中的梯度幅度，引入一种简单有效的干预方法，以缓解校准问题。该方法在保持高精度的同时显著改善了模型的置信度校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于区域的损失函数（如Dice损失）虽在类别和区域不平衡的分割任务中表现优异，但其训练出的模型往往过度自信，导致预测校准不良，这在医学影像应用（如肿瘤切除范围界定）中严重阻碍临床采纳。因此，亟需解决此类模型的校准问题。

Method: 提出对损失函数的偏导数添加一个因子，使梯度大小与预测误差线性相关，从而实现对梯度向量场的‘手术’式修正，以抑制过度自信。该方法可与任意基于区域的损失函数结合使用。

Result: 在2D和3D医学分割任务的实验中，该方法有效提升了模型的校准性能，同时保持了原有的高预测准确性。

Conclusion: 通过梯度层面的简单干预，可有效缓解基于区域损失函数的过度自信问题，提升模型在医疗场景下的可靠性与临床可用性。

Abstract: Region-based loss functions, such as the Dice loss, have established themselves as the de facto standard for highly class- and region-imbalanced segmentation tasks. However, models trained using region-based loss functions are notoriously miscalibrated and typically yield over-confident predictions. In medical imaging applications, such as defining tumor resection margins, this miscalibration is hindering clinical adoption. In this work, we outline a novel gradient perspective on this overconfidence and show how it affects region-based loss functions. We propose a "surgery" on the gradient vector field as a simple, yet effective intervention to mitigate calibration issues. This surgery adds a factor to the loss's partial derivative, scaling the gradient's magnitude linearly with the prediction error. In empirical evaluations across 2D and 3D medical segmentation tasks, we demonstrate the effectiveness of this intervention while maintaining high prediction accuracy when used in conjunction with any region-based loss function.

### [12] [Dynamic Manipulation Hypergraphs for HAR: Beyond Pairwise Relations: Dynamic Manipulation Hypergraphs for Vision-Based Human Activity Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14350)
*Fatemeh Ziaeetabar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种动态操作超图框架，用于细粒度操作识别。该框架通过高阶关系单元建模手、物体、工具和支撑面之间的演化关系，利用外观、空间、运动和语义角色特征编码实体，并通过邻近性、接触和运动耦合谓词生成和排序超边。通过节点-超边和超边-节点的消息传递以及时间注意力机制，实现对动态交互结构的推理。实验在EPIC-KITCHENS-100/VISOR和Assembly101上进行，结果表明该方法相比配对图提升HO-F1 6.9和9.5个百分点，相比静态超图提升4.4和5.8个百分点，且高排名超边与接触密集的操作区间高度对应，验证了时变高阶关系建模的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出动态操作超图框架，包括：1）在每个时间步编码相关实体的多模态特征；2）基于邻近性、接触和运动耦合谓词生成并排序超边候选；3）设计超图推理网络，实现节点与超边间双向消息传递；4）引入时间注意力机制处理演化交互结构；5）输出类无关的超边重要性评分，用于识别关键实体配置和时间区间。

Result: 在EPIC-KITCHENS-100/VISOR和Assembly101数据集上，该方法相比匹配的成对图分别提升HO-F1 6.9和9.5个百分点，相比静态超图提升4.4和5.8个百分点；在ARCTIC数据集上的定性分析显示高排名超边与接触丰富的操作阶段一致，证明模型关注的关键区域具有实际意义。

Conclusion: 时间变化的高阶关系建模对于细粒度操作活动识别具有显著价值，所提出的动态超图框架有效捕捉了多实体间的复杂互动演化过程，优于现有基线方法。

Abstract: Fine-grained manipulation recognition requires modeling evolving relations among hands, objects, tools, and supporting surfaces. Conventional graph-based methods use pairwise edges that can fragment a coordinated event into disconnected binary relations. We propose a dynamic manipulation hypergraph framework that represents multi-entity configurations as higher-order relational units. At each temporal step, relevant entities are encoded using appearance, spatial, motion, and semantic-role features. Hyperedge candidates are instantiated and ranked using proximity, contact, and motion-coupling predicates. A hypergraph reasoning network performs node-to-hyperedge and hyperedge-to-node message passing, followed by temporal attention over the evolving interaction structure. The framework provides class-agnostic hyperedge-importance scores that identify entity configurations and temporal intervals emphasized by the model without treating them as causal explanations. Quantitative evaluation is conducted on EPIC-KITCHENS-100/VISOR and Assembly101 under an annotation-assisted entity-localization protocol. Video-only and entity-based methods provide contextual comparisons, while a matched pairwise graph and a static hypergraph serve as the principal controlled baselines because they use identical entity inputs and comparable relational settings. The proposed method improves HO-F1 over the matched pairwise graph by 6.9 percentage points on EPIC-KITCHENS-100/VISOR and 9.5 points on Assembly101, and exceeds the static hypergraph by 4.4 and 5.8 points, respectively. Qualitative analysis on ARCTIC further shows correspondence between highly ranked hyperedges and contact-rich manipulation intervals. These results demonstrate the value of time-varying higher-order relational modeling for fine-grained manipulation activity recognition.

### [13] [$K$-NeAS: Scalable Multi-Material CT Reconstruction Using Neural SDFs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14415)
*Daksh K. Shah,Emmanouil Nikolakakis,Razvan V. Marinescu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: K-NeAS提出一种统一且可扩展的架构，用于自动多材料表面重建。通过共享潜在骨干和可微分的K材料软选择器，实现任意数量重叠组织的建模，并利用高斯混合模型自动确定衰减范围，结合调度辅助浮点损失减少极端稀疏条件下的几何幻觉。在四个临床锥束CT数据集上验证，K-NeAS在3种材料下显著提升3D体素保真度（腹部33.28 dB PSNR，优于基线1.88 dB），并在5-10视角条件下表现出更强鲁棒性（最高提升1.17 dB PSNR）


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有隐式场景表示方法受限于手动设定的衰减范围和刚性的双材料约束，难以适应复杂多组织结构及极端稀疏采样条件

Conclusion: K-NeAS是一种高效、灵活且自动化的多材料表面重建框架，能够有效应对稀疏投影下的挑战，为临床CT低剂量成像提供强有力的技术支持

Abstract: Computed Tomography (CT) carries significant ionizing radiation risks, driving the need for sparse-view reconstruction. Implicit scene representations (ISRs) address this by recovering continuous volumetric attenuation fields directly from sparse projections, and recent geometry-aware extensions jointly model surface geometry alongside attenuation to improve fidelity and enable clean tissue segmentation without manual thresholding. However, these methods remain limited by manually tuned attenuation bounds and rigid two-material constraints. This paper proposes $K$-NeAS, a unified and scalable architecture for automated, multi-material surface reconstruction. We replace independent material networks with a shared latent backbone and introduce a fully differentiable $K$-material sequential soft selector to model an arbitrary number of overlapping tissues. To eliminate manual tuning, we automate attenuation bounding using a Gaussian Mixture Model (GMM) and implement a scheduled auxiliary floater loss to mitigate geometric hallucinations common under extreme sparsity. Evaluated across four clinical Cone-Beam CT (CBCT) datasets, $K$-NeAS successfully scales to arbitrary material counts, achieving superior 3D volumetric fidelity at $K=3$ materials on complex multi-tissue regions such as the Abdomen ($33.28\text{ dB}$ 3D PSNR vs. $31.40\text{ dB}$ single-material NeAS baseline, a $+1.88\text{ dB}$ improvement). Furthermore, our model exhibits enhanced robustness under sparse-sampling conditions, outperforming baseline 3D PSNR by up to $1.17\text{ dB}$ under 5- and 10-view constraints.

### [14] [Emergent Region-Level Facial Correspondence in Frozen Vision Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14423)

Using DINOv3 ViT-L/16 patch embeddings and FaRL only as a face-part labeling interface, we evaluate cross-identity nearest-neighbor matching and temporal label propagation on 200 CelebDF-v2 real videos. DINOv3 achieves 83.0% region-level semantic accuracy under unconstrained cross-identity matching, compared with a 23.0% area-weighted random baseline, and 95.5% temporal tracking accuracy without a learned temporal module. A no-FaRL control collapses to 0.9%, showing that FaRL supplies semantic initialization while DINOv3 supplies dense spatial correspondence. The strongest correspondence appears at an intermediate layer: block 18 gives a 4.93x same-region versus cross-region discrimination ratio, compared with 1.48x at the final block. Against CLIP ViT-L/14, DINOv3 shows only a small aggregate advantage but a +16.8 pp gain on anatomical regions, indicating that image-level contrastive supervision captures coarse facial layout but not fine-grained anatomical identity. These results establish frozen DINOv3 as a strong zero-shot representation for region-level facial correspondence and identify intermediate self-supervised features as the most useful layer for dense face analysis.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在复杂田间环境下对早期小尺寸、易遮挡、低对比度的棉花蕾检测效果不佳，亟需一种高效精准的自动检测技术以支持棉花生长监测与精准栽培管理。

Method: 基于YOLO26m构建Cotton-SF YOLO框架，引入动态蛇形卷积以自适应提取可变形边缘特征，并在C2f结构中融合频域增强设计频率域特征调制模块，强化边缘与纹理判别信息，抑制背景干扰。

Result: 在新构建的标注田间数据集上，模型达到mAP$_{50}$ 0.8196、mAP$_{50:95}$ 0.4942、召回率0.7939，相比基线YOLO26m分别提升1.25%、3.45%、2.96%，消融实验与可视化验证了结构与频域线索的互补性优势。

Conclusion: 所提Cotton-SF YOLO框架通过结合动态边缘感知与频域特征调制，在复杂田间环境中实现了对棉花蕾的高精度检测，为棉花生长监控与智慧农业提供了有力技术支持。

Abstract: Cotton squares are important phenotypic indicators of the early reproductive growth of cotton, and automatic field detection of cotton squares provides an important basis for cotton growth monitoring and precision cultivation management. However, early cotton square detection in complex field environments remains insufficiently explored, as cotton squares are small, frequently occluded, easily blurred, subject to illumination variations, and exhibit low contrast against surrounding cotton leaves. To address these challenges, we propose a task-oriented framework based on YOLO26m, named Cotton-SF YOLO, for cotton square detection under natural field conditions. To improve the perception of small and irregular cotton square boundaries, we introduce Dynamic Snake Convolution into the detector, enabling adaptive extraction of deformable edge features. Furthermore, a frequency-domain feature modulation module is designed by incorporating spectral enhancement into the C2f structure, which recalibrate frequency-domain representations and strengthen discriminative edge and texture cues while reducing interference from complex cotton leaf backgrounds. Trained and evaluated on our newly constructed and annotated field dataset with manually annotated cotton squares, the proposed model achieves mAP$_{50}$, mAP$_{50:95}$, and recall values of 0.8196, 0.4942, and 0.7939, improving over the baseline YOLO26m by 1.25%, 3.45%, and 2.96%, respectively. Ablation experiments and visualization demonstrate that the best performance is achieved with the complementary effects of structural and frequency cues.

### [16] [G$^2$SR: Geometric Methods for Fast and Memory-Efficient Gaussian-based Surface Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14470)
*Dasong Gao,Vivienne Sze,Sertac Karaman*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: G2SR 是一种轻量级的少视角表面重建方法，利用多视图几何关系从2D高斯点对应关系中解析推导3D高斯点，避免了传统方法中的“浮点”伪影。其前端使用神经网络检测和追踪图像平面上的2D高斯点，后端通过解析三角化生成度量尺度的3D高斯点。在ScanNet、Replica和DTU数据集上，G2SR在几何精度上达到或超过现有端到端方法，同时以每秒69-89次重建速度运行，仅需203MB GPU内存（减少5-107倍），适用于移动平台的实时在线重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有少视角表面重建方法在移动平台上面临计算资源与精度的矛盾：3D高斯泼溅（3DGS）虽能提供高质量场景表示，但由少数视角构建时存在病态问题，易产生‘浮点’伪影；而现有的端到端方法依赖大型神经网络（如Transformer），计算开销大、内存占用高且泛化能力差。因此需要一种高效、准确且轻量的方法实现在线重建。

Method: G2SR提出利用多视图几何的良构性——给定跨视角的2D高斯点对应关系，3D高斯点可解析地通过三角化获得。该方法包含两个部分：（1）轻量级神经前端，用于在图像平面检测和跟踪2D高斯点；（2）解析式后端，基于多视图几何对每个2D对应点进行三角化，生成度量尺度的3D高斯点。

Result: 在ScanNet、Replica和DTU数据集上，G2SR在2-3视角输入（384×512分辨率）下，实现了与当前最优端到端方法相当或更优的几何精度；同时，推理速度达69-89帧/秒，仅需203MB GPU内存，相比现有方法降低5-107倍内存占用，具备显著的实时性和轻量化优势。

Conclusion: G2SR通过结合神经前端检测与解析几何后端，有效解决了少视角表面重建中的病态性问题，在保持高精度的同时大幅降低计算与内存开销，为移动端和在线场景下的高斯基表面重建提供了实用可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Few-view surface reconstruction recovers the visible surfaces of a scene from a few posed RGB images, providing the 3D models that robots need to explore and interact online. On mobile platforms, the reconstruction must be fast and geometrically accurate while keeping a small memory footprint to ensure safe and efficient operation. 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) offers a high-fidelity scene representation, but building it from a few views is ill-posed, as many distinct surfaces reproduce the same images, making traditional photometric methods prone to "floater" artifacts. End-to-end methods resolve the ambiguity by regressing splats with large, usually Transformer-based, networks that require heavy compute and memory while generalizing poorly to new scenes. We propose G2SR, which exploits a well-posed core of the task: given cross-view 2D splat correspondences, 3D splats follow analytically from multi-view geometry. G2SR employs a lightweight neural frontend to detect and track 2D Gaussian splats on the image plane and an analytic backend to triangulate each into a metric-scale 3D splat. On ScanNet, Replica, and DTU, G2SR matches or exceeds the geometric accuracy of state-of-the-art end-to-end methods while running at 69-89 reconstructions per second within 203 MB of GPU memory (5-107x less) for 2- and 3-view inputs at 384 x 512 resolution, offering a practical path to online Gaussian-based surface reconstruction.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理无序拍摄的图像序列时，要么需要等待所有数据完成才能进行重建（如SfM），要么无法处理无序输入（如传统SLAM）。为实现即时反馈且保持高质量重建，亟需一种能适应无序序列、具备全局一致性并可扩展的大规模重建方案。

Method: 利用视觉位置识别模型与共视图进行快速匹配；设计基于聚类的环路闭合机制以避免依赖顺序输入；引入渐进式层次结构提升大场景下的效率；结合GPU优化与精细的高斯原型布局实现快速局部重建。

Abstract: 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) has become the method of choice for reconstructing and real-time rendering of captured scenes. To capture a scene with good visual quality, continuous image sequences are usually combined with out-of-order shots for better scene coverage. Structure from motion can reconstruct such captures, but only after they are all available and often with high computational cost. Incremental reconstruction methods -- often derived from SLAM solutions -- provide immediate feedback, but cannot handle the out-of-order capture we require. We provide the first immediate feedback solution for such radiance field capture that provides global consistency. We first introduce a method for fast matching in out-of-order sequences, by repurposing visual place recognition models and a covisibility graph, and provide an efficient way to find highly connected keyframes, improving quality even for ordered sequences. We show how these steps -- together with GPU optimization and careful Gaussian primitive placement -- provide fast local reconstruction, in our challenging radiance field reconstruction case. We then introduce a novel cluster-based method, again using the covisibility graph, to provide efficient loop closure that does not require sequential input. Finally, to handle large scenes in our context, we introduce a progressive hierarchy that allows our method to scale to large environments, without compromising efficiency. Our results show we provide immediate feedback 3DGS reconstruction with good visual quality in several datasets, with up to thousands of input images.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于微调DINOv2 ViT-L/14的多尺度图像切片分析，结合FAISS kNN检索、源感知时空融合、地理与海拔先验的拟合度降权，以及区域掩码策略。

Abstract: This paper describes DS@GT ARC's third-place solution to the PlantCLEF 2026 challenge on multi-species plant identification in vegetation quadrat images, where systems must predict every species present in high-resolution (~3000 x 3000 pixel) plot photographs while training only on single-label images of individual plants. The pipeline is built around a fine-tuned DINOv2 ViT-L/14 classifier applied over a multi-scale tile decomposition of each quadrat, with per-tile predictions blended with a FAISS kNN retriever and post-processed by source-aware temporal fusion across repeated plot visits, a habitat-fit demotion that injects geographic and altitude priors from the training data, and a South-Western Europe geographic mask. Habitat-fit demotion and multi-scale aggregation are the largest individual contributors in the ablations. Two complementary training-centric directions, a cross-region transformer with noisy-student distillation on the LUCAS dataset and a label-as-query transformer decoder over synthetic CLS-domain pseudo-quadrats, yielded null results. An inference-time augmentation with instance-aware segmentation crops also did not improve performance. The selected submission reaches a private-leaderboard macro-F1 of 0.43902 (third place; public 0.51096); an unselected configuration of the same pipeline scored above 0.45 on the private set. Code: https://github.com/dsgt-arc/plantclef-2026.

### [20] [Compression of 3D Gaussian Splatting Data Using GPU-friendly Graphics Texture Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14513)
*Amir Said,Randall Rauwendaal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于纹理压缩的3D高斯点云颜色系数压缩方法，利用GPU硬件加速实现高效并行解码，显著降低内存占用，并支持随机访问以保证大规模并行渲染性能。实验表明，使用BC1和BC7格式可在几乎无视觉损失的情况下实现快速GPU解压。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3D高斯点云（3DGS）虽能生成高质量新视角，但依赖球谐函数（SH）表示视图相关颜色，导致每个基元需存储大量系数，内存开销大；现有压缩方法未充分利用现代GPU的并行解码能力。

Method: 采用专为GPU并行解码设计的纹理压缩方案（如BC1、BC7），对SH颜色系数进行压缩；通过局部分组与重排序优化压缩效率；引入比特率控制策略以保持随机访问能力，支持大规模并行处理。

Result: 实验验证了该方法在使用BC1和BC7压缩格式时，可实现接近无损的视觉质量，且解码过程由GPU高效完成，延迟极低，适用于大规模3DGS场景渲染。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效降低了3DGS中视图相关颜色的内存开销，同时充分发挥了现代GPU的并行解码优势，为高保真、高性能3D场景重建与渲染提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Techniques for modeling 3D scenes from image collections, such as 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS), are capable of generating high-quality novel views by leveraging graphics primitives with view-dependent appearance. In 3DGS, spherical harmonic (SH) are employed to model view-dependent color, resulting in a large number of SH coefficients per primitive and large memory requirements. While compression approaches have been proposed to mitigate this problem, they do not exploit the capabilities of modern Graphics Processing Units (GPUs) for parallel decoding and rendering. In this paper, we propose a method for compressing SH color coefficients using texture compression schemes specifically designed for efficient parallel GPU decoding and supported by dedicated hardware acceleration. It is shown that those methods can compress color coefficients more effectively than 2D textures by exploiting the fact that primitives can be locally grouped and reordered according to color. Furthermore, we introduce a bit-rate control strategy that preserves random access, enabling large-scale parallelization without compromising rendering performance. Experimental results using BC1 and BC7 texture compression formats show that GPU-based decompression can be achieved with negligible or imperceptible degradation in the visual quality of rendered 3DGS scenes.

### [21] [VTM-Nav: Hierarchical Visual-Topological Memory for Cross-Episode Object-Goal Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14514)
*Xiaoran Xu,Yupeng Wu,Tianyu Xue,Yifan Xu,Xuanran Dong,Xiaoshan Yang,Changsheng Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为\method{}的无训练视觉-语言模型导航框架，用于跨回合物体目标导航（Cross-Episode Object-Goal Navigation），其核心是持久化的分层视觉-拓扑记忆（VTM）。该框架在相同场景中持续操作，保留自获经验并固定模型参数，通过粗到细的匹配机制组织房间与物体级别的场景知识，并仅在记忆与当前观察一致时提供软性引导。此外，引入保守执行保护机制以减少振荡、阻塞和过早停止问题。在HM3D v0.1、HM3D v0.2和MP3D三个基准上，\method{}优于增强版的WMNav基线，证明了结构化视觉-拓扑经验复用的有效性与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练-free方法通常在每次实验后重置场景状态，限制了经验积累；而真实场景中智能体需在相同环境中长期运行并复用经验。因此，本文旨在构建一个支持跨回合经验保留与复用的导航系统，提升智能体在复杂室内环境中的长期适应能力。

Method: \method{}采用持久化分层视觉-拓扑记忆（VTM），将场景知识按房间和物体层级组织，利用视觉-语言模型进行语义理解，通过粗到细的匹配策略检索相关经验，并仅在记忆与当前观测一致时提供软性指导。同时引入保守执行保护机制，防止导航过程中的不稳定行为。

Result: \method{}在三个基准数据集（HM3D v0.1, HM3D v0.2, MP3D）上均取得最佳性能，显著优于增强版的WMNav基线，验证了其在跨回合场景下结构化经验复用的有效性与泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的\method{}框架成功实现了跨回合物体目标导航中的有效经验复用，通过分层视觉-拓扑记忆与保守执行机制，在不更新模型参数的前提下提升了导航稳定性与成功率，为训练-free视觉-语言导航系统在真实长期任务中的应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Object-goal navigation requires an embodied agent to locate and reach an instance of a specified object category in an indoor environment. Recent training-free approaches leverage vision-language models (VLMs) for open-vocabulary semantic reasoning, but are typically evaluated under an episodic protocol that resets all scene-specific state after each episode. We introduce Cross-Episode Object-Goal Navigation, in which an agent repeatedly operates in the same scene, retains only self-acquired experience, and keeps its model parameters fixed. To support experience reuse, we present \method, a training-free VLM navigation framework with a persistent hierarchical Visual-Topological Memory (VTM). The VTM organizes scene knowledge at room and object levels and retrieves relevant experience through coarse-to-fine matching, providing memory as soft guidance only when it agrees with current observations. A conservative execution guard further mitigates oscillations, blocked motions, and premature stopping. Under a controlled same-scene protocol, we evaluate \method{} on three benchmarks, HM3D v0.1, HM3D v0.2, and MP3D, and compare it with a strengthened WMNav baseline augmented with cross-episode textual memory, while keeping the VLM backbone and action pipeline identical. \method{} achieves the best performance across all three benchmarks, demonstrating the effectiveness and robustness of structured visual-topological experience reuse across datasets.

### [22] [Uni-AdaVD: Universal Concept Erasure for Visual Generation via Orthogonal Value Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14521)
*Qifan Zhou,Yuan Wang,Yanbin Hao,Xiang Wang,Kuien Liu,Richang Hong,Meng Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Uni-AdaVD 是一种通用的推理时概念擦除框架，通过将多模态注意力的值空间视为统一干预空间，结合编码器感知的目标表示构建和正交值分解，实现无需更新模型权重即可有效擦除目标概念，适用于多种视觉生成模型并保持非目标内容与生成先验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有概念擦除方法通常依赖特定架构，难以在不破坏非目标内容和生成先验的前提下有效移除目标概念，因此亟需一种通用、高效且无需微调的擦除框架。

Method: Uni-AdaVD 将多模态注意力的值空间作为统一干预空间，提出编码器感知的目标表示构建方法以定位异构文本编码器中的目标语义，并结合正交值分解与自适应擦除偏移，实现对目标语义方向的抑制而不修改原始模型权重。

Result: 在 U-Net、DiT、自回归图像生成器及文生视频模型上均实现了单概念和多概念的有效擦除，同时显著保留了非目标生成先验，验证了其通用性与高效性。

Conclusion: Uni-AdaVD 提供了一种高效、可适配的视觉生成模型安全机制，适用于现代复杂生成模型的部署需求。

Abstract: Visual generative models inevitably absorb undesirable concepts from uncurated pretraining data, making concept erasure essential for safe deployment. Existing erasure methods, however, are often architecture-specific and struggle to remove target concepts while preserving non-target content and generative priors. We present Uni-AdaVD, a universal inference-time concept erasure framework for visual generation. Uni-AdaVD treats the value space of multimodal attention as a unified intervention space and introduces encoder-aware target representation construction to localize target semantics across heterogeneous text encoders. It further combines orthogonal value decomposition with an adaptive erasing shift to suppress target semantic directions without updating the original model weights. Extensive experiments on U-Net-, DiT-, and autoregressive image generators, as well as text-to-video models, demonstrate strong performance on single- and multi-concept erasure while preserving non-target priors. These results suggest that Uni-AdaVD provides an efficient and adaptable safety mechanism for modern visual generative models. Our code is available at https://github.com/QifanZhou/Uni-AdaVD.

### [23] [SwinAD: Multi-stage feature reconstruction for unsupervised industrial anomaly detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14534)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无监督方法多针对单类场景，难以应对多类场景中因正常模式多样导致的过拟合问题，降低正常与异常区域的区分能力。

Method: 采用冻结的 Swin Transformer V2 编码器提取多层次语义特征，通过分阶段瓶颈模块加丢弃机制防止平凡映射，提升对正常模式的鲁棒重建；引入特征多样性保持的重建框架，保留多个互补的重建假设，通过多尺度特征差异聚合生成最终异常图。

Result: 在 MVTec AD、VisA、Real-IAD 三个基准上均取得竞争力的图像级性能和强像素级定位精度，尤其在像素级 AP 和 1 上显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Industrial anomaly detection aims to identify and localize defective regions without relying on exhaustive annotations of all possible defect types. Although recent unsupervised methods have achieved strong performance, most are primarily designed for single-class settings and often struggle in multi-class scenarios, where diverse normal patterns may lead to over-generalization and reduce the discriminative capability between normal and anomalous regions. In this paper, we propose SwinAD, a reconstruction-based framework for multi-class unsupervised anomaly detection that leverages a frozen pretrained Swin Transformer V2 encoder and a feature diversity-preserving reconstruction decoder. The hierarchical encoder provides semantically rich multi-scale features, while stage-wise bottleneck modules with dropout prevent trivial identity mapping and encourage robust reconstruction of normal patterns. To further improve localization, we introduce a feature diversity-preserving reconstruction framework that maintains complementary reconstruction hypotheses instead of relying on a single decoding branch. The discrepancies between encoder features and the two reconstructed features are then aggregated across multiple scales to produce the final anomaly map. Experiments conducted on three industrial anomaly detection benchmarks, including MVTec AD, VisA, and Real-IAD, demonstrate that SwinAD achieves competitive image-level performance and strong pixel-level localization accuracy, with particularly notable improvements in pixel-level AP and 1 on MVTec AD. These results indicate that combining hierarchical Swin features with diverse multi-scale reconstruction substantially improve pixel-level localization in multi-class unsupervised anomaly setting.

### [24] [3D Geometric Tooth Alignment Planning via Deep Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14544)

Method: 将牙齿排列建模为马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），采用改进的深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）算法，结合Transformer结构处理高维状态-动作空间，引入动态掩码机制限制每步仅移动部分牙齿以符合临床顺序性，并采用两阶段课程学习策略逐步提升任务难度以保障训练稳定性。

Abstract: 3D geometric tooth alignment planning, which determines sequential trajectories from initial malocclusion to the final target alignment, is a cornerstone of modern digital orthodontics. This paper presents a novel deep reinforcement learning (DRL) framework to automate the generation of these alignment paths. We formulate the planning process as a Markov Decision Process (MDP) to capture its sequential decision-making nature, focusing on optimizing geometric trajectories while integrating essential spatial constraints, such as inter-dental collision avoidance and path efficiency. The proposed method leverages the Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (DDPG) algorithm, enhanced by three key innovations: (1) a Transformer-based agent to model complex spatial interactions between teeth and manage high-dimensional state-action spaces; (2) a dynamic masking scheme that restricts movement to a sparse subset of teeth per step, better reflecting the clinical logic of sequential alignment; and (3) a two-stage curriculum learning strategy that gradually increases task difficulty to ensure training stability and efficient path discovery. We evaluate our approach on a dataset of 10K expert-designed treatment plans based on clinical data. Experimental results demonstrate that our method outperforms existing baselines in terms of path safety and geometric efficiency, providing a robust and automated solution for 3D geometric orthodontic alignment planning.

### [25] [AdaTurn: Budget-Aware Test-Time Scaling for Active Visual Perception Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14547)
*Susan Liang,Chao Huang,Filippos Bellos,Jing Bi,Jason J Corso,Chenliang Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AdaTurn 是一种预算感知框架，通过将可用回合数作为条件输入，显式训练代理在预算限制下的边界行为，以解决因预算不足导致的‘灾难性截断’问题。其核心组件 FA-DAPO 将超预算情况转化为可训练的最终决策步骤，使模型能在无法继续操作时合成部分证据。通过训练和推理阶段随机化预算并引入负载均衡调度器，AdaTurn 显著提升了低预算下的准确率（如 VisualProbe-Medium 在4回合下从36.7%提升至47.6%），同时保持大预算下的良好扩展性，并可迁移至多种骨干网络和通用多模态基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在训练时忽略实际部署中的滚动预算变化，导致当实际预算低于代理期望时，交互被提前截断，无法生成有效答案，这种现象称为‘灾难性截断’。为解决该问题，需要让代理具备对预算变化的感知与适应能力。

Method: 提出 AdaTurn 框架，将允许的回合数作为条件输入；引入 Forced-Answer DAPO（FA-DAPO），将超预算事件转化为可训练的最终决策步骤，鼓励模型在资源耗尽时仍能基于已有信息做出合理判断；在训练和推理中随机化预算，并设计负载均衡调度器以支持高效执行。

Result: 在低预算条件下显著提升性能，例如 VisualProbe-Medium 在4回合下准确率从36.7%提升至47.6%；在高预算下保持良好扩展性；适用于多种模型架构和多模态任务，具备良好的迁移能力。

Conclusion: AdaTurn 有效缓解了预算受限场景下的灾难性截断问题，实现了在不同预算条件下的稳定表现，是实现鲁棒、实用视觉代理的关键进展。

Abstract: Active visual agents solve fine-grained image tasks by interleaving reasoning with image-grounding actions across multiple turns. However, deployment-time rollout budgets are rarely fixed: some requests permit long rollouts, while others require the agent to act under a tight turn limit. Existing methods train the policy as if the rollout budget were hidden, so when the available budget is smaller than the trajectory the agent prefers, the interaction is often truncated before any valid answer is produced; we term this failure \emph{catastrophic truncation}. To overcome this challenge, we present AdaTurn, a budget-aware framework that conditions the agent on the allowed number of turns and explicitly trains the boundary behavior induced by the budget. Our key component, Forced-Answer DAPO (FA-DAPO), converts the over-budget event from a masked or penalized failure into a trainable final-decision step, teaching the model to synthesize partial evidence when further tool use is no longer possible. We further randomize rollout budgets during both training and inference and introduce a load-balanced scheduler that makes such operations practical. AdaTurn substantially improves low-budget accuracy, for example raising VisualProbe-Medium from 36.7% to 47.6% at four turns, while preserving strong scaling at larger budgets and transferring effectively to multiple backbones and general multimodal benchmarks.

This report presents HyMobileAgent, a mobile GUI agent built on Hy3.0-VL-A3B, a vision-native foundation model featuring native any-resolution input, an A3B-scale deployment budget, and a 32K context window to model extended interaction histories. ### [27] [Breaking the Model Forgetting Cycle in Long-Incremental 3D Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14560)
*Peisheng Qian,Jie Xu,Xulei Yang,Na Zhao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LDMR提出一种受人类学习动态启发的框架，通过监控每类检测质量并驱动两个创新机制：(i) 类似人类的阶段内回顾，将每个增量阶段划分为多个子阶段以集中记忆最易遗忘的对象；(ii) 场景感知的跨阶段记忆演化，通过结合场景可学习性和多样性来演化记忆库以实现知识迁移。该方法有效缓解了长期增量学习中的模型遗忘问题，在SUN RGB-D和ScanNetV2上显著优于现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于伪标签的增量3D目标检测方法在短序列中表现尚可，但在长序列中因数据分布偏移导致模型遗忘，进而引发伪标签误差累积，形成自我强化的退化循环。

Method: LDMR框架通过周期性训练检查点监测每类检测质量，利用学习动态信号驱动两个机制：(i) 阶段内回顾机制将增量阶段分块训练，聚焦于最易遗忘对象的记忆恢复；(ii) 跨阶段记忆演化机制基于场景可学习性和多样性更新记忆库，促进知识迁移。

Result: 在SUN RGB-D和ScanNetV2上的多组长期增量实验表明，LDMR显著缓解了模型遗忘，性能全面超越现有基线方法。

Conclusion: LDMR通过模拟人类学习过程中的动态记忆与复习机制，有效应对长期增量3D目标检测中的模型遗忘问题，为持续学习提供了新思路。

Abstract: Incremental 3D object detection requires a detector to learn novel object classes while remembering previously learned ones over sequentially arriving data. Previous methods, primarily based on pseudo-labeling, perform reasonably in short-incremental stages but still suffer from severe model forgetting when dealing with long-incremental sequences. We investigate this failure and reveal a detrimental self-reinforcing cycle: data distribution shift of novel classes causes model forgetting on old classes, which further produces accumulated error in pseudo-labeling that exacerbates model degradation. To address this issue, we draw inspiration from the human learning process and propose the \emph{Learning-Dynamics-driven Memory and Review} (LDMR) framework. LDMR monitors per-class detection quality at periodic training checkpoints and uses these learning-dynamics signals to drive two innovative mechanisms, namely (i) human-like intra-stage review that divides each incremental stage into multiple sub-stages' training and concentrates on remembering the most-forgotten objects, and (ii) scene-aware cross-stage memory evolution that evolves a memory bank to transfer knowledge between two consecutive stages by jointly considering scene learnability and diversity. Extensive experiments across multiple long-incremental protocols on indoor benchmarks SUN RGB-D and ScanNetV2 show that LDMR substantially mitigates the model forgetting and outperforms all baselines by a clear margin. Code is available at https://github.com/qianpeisheng/LDMR.

Existing studies mainly focus on the Big Five personality model and often rely on language or multimodal inputs. This question is particularly relevant for MBTI types, which are widely used in practice and more readily interpretable by large language models. To this end, we propose \textbf{GlanceFace}, an end-to-end framework for apparent personality inference leveraging vision-language models to introduce semantic priors and a semantic-enhanced facial representation module to capture subtle personality-related cues, together with an uncertainty-aware learning strategy to handle noisy and subjective annotations. Extensive experiments demonstrate strong performance on MBTI-based apparent personality benchmarks and reveal relationships between facial characteristics and perceived personality traits, highlighting its potential to support adaptive initial interaction strategies for embodied agents. The code and dataset are available at https://github.com/MrHuan3/GlanceFace.

</details>


### [32] [Autoregressive Modeling of Film with Applications in Video Montage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14645)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用长上下文自回归变压器架构，在大规模电影数据集上训练，以学习电影的统计结构与叙事模式。在推理阶段，引入一种受原始素材约束的解码算法，仅从给定的原始镜头中选择最符合已学习模式的下一个镜头，而不生成新画面。

Result: 在标准镜头排序基准测试中，FilmGPT 在下一镜头预测任务上表现优于现有最优方法；用户研究表明，其生成的剪辑结果在连贯性、叙事流畅性和观众满意度方面均显著优于传统方法；同时，该方法可广泛应用于自动剪辑、智能剪辑建议及人机协作编辑等场景。

Conclusion: FilmGPT 成功展示了从数据中学习电影语言的可能性，无需人工规则即可实现高质量视频蒙太奇。该方法为自动化视频编辑提供了新的范式，并具备良好的实用性和扩展性。

Abstract: This work introduces FilmGPT, an autoregressive transformer designed to address the challenge of video montage--turning a collection of raw, "unwatchable" footage into coherent cinematic sequences. Inspired by language learning in modern LLMs, we train a long-context autoregressive transformer on a large corpus of movies. The aim is to implicitly capture the "grammar" of film directly from data rather than from hand-coded rules. Unlike other generative models, FilmGPT does not generate any new video frames. Instead, at inference time, we introduce a footage-constrained decoding algorithm to select the best next shot from the input raw footage according to the statistical patterns learned from films. We first evaluate these learned statistics directly by using the FilmGPT autoregressive model for next shot prediction on a standard benchmark of shot sequence ordering, outperforming the previous state of the art. We then evaluate our footage-constrained decoding algorithm on the full film editing task via a user study, and find that our FilmGPT-based editing significantly outperforms previous approaches. Finally, we demonstrate the applicability of FilmGPT to a wide range of applications in video montage, from automatic video segment trimming to human-in-the-loop film editing.

### [34] [ReBind: Multi-Reference Video Editing via Structured Instructions with Explicit Reference Relationships](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14681)

Abstract: Recent diffusion-based video generation models have made significant progress in multi-reference image-conditioned video editing. Existing editing instructions lack explicit reference relationships, and most multimodal large language models (MLLMs) cannot generate them reliably. To address this problem, we propose ReBind, a systematic framework that introduces semantic instructions with embedded reference tokens as the intermediate representation for multi-reference image-conditioned video editing. Our key insight is embedding reference tokens at semantic positions to eliminate ambiguity and establish precise bindings between visual attributes and their sources. We develop ReBind-Instruct, a specialized MLLM that learns to establish explicit bindings between visual attributes and their reference sources through a two-stage progressive scheme for precise reference relationships. We further develop ReBind-Edit, which enables lightweight adaptation of text-to-video models to coordinate multiple references by binding visual attributes to their designated sources. ### [35] [GlobalForge: Towards Robust AI-Generated Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14684)
*Manni Cui,Ruiqi Liu,Dianyuan Zou,Ziheng Qin,Jingrui Xu,ZiAn Wang,Jianglan Wei,Han Zhou,Yu Liu,Yan Wang,Shu Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文提出GlobalForge框架，通过抑制局部伪影并增强全局结构推理，提升AI生成图像检测器在真实世界退化下的鲁棒性。引入RealDeg-Bench评估基准，验证了其在多种退化场景下的优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI生成图像检测器在干净数据集上表现良好，但在经过真实世界传播退化（如JPEG压缩、模糊）后性能显著下降，主要原因是过度依赖局部生成伪影，这些伪影易被破坏。

Method: 提出GlobalForge框架，包含两个互补模块：局部信息瓶颈（LIB）用于抑制局部特征以防止捷径学习，全局结构推理（GSR）模块强制每个令牌从远距离区域收集证据。两者通过基于退化的对比结构损失联合训练，确保特征在退化下保持稳定。

Result: GlobalForge在8个真实场景基准组上平均准确率提升5.89%，显著优于现有最先进方法；在RealDeg-Bench上对单步和复合退化均表现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 通过将判别线索从脆弱的局部特征转向更稳健的全局结构，GlobalForge有效提升了AI生成图像检测器在真实复杂环境中的稳定性与泛化能力。

Abstract: AI-generated image (AIGI) detectors achieve strong accuracy on clean benchmarks, but their performance drops sharply after images are propagated through real-world channels. We trace this fragility to what these detectors actually learn: they overfit to local artifacts left by generators in small spatial neighborhoods, which are easily destroyed by common propagation degradations such as JPEG compression and blur. Instead, we shift the discriminative cue from fragile local artifacts to more robust global structure. Building on this, we propose GlobalForge, a framework with two complementary modules. The Local Information Bottleneck (LIB) suppresses local components to block shortcut learning, while the Global Structural Reasoning (GSR) module forces every token to gather evidence from distant regions. Both modules are trained jointly under a contrastive structural loss based on degradation that keeps the resulting features stable under degradation. To support fine-grained robustness evaluation, we further introduce RealDeg-Bench, covering 7 common degradation operators and multi-step compound chains. GlobalForge improves average BAcc on 8 in-the-wild benchmark groups by $\mathbf{5.89\%}$ over the previous state-of-the-art, and is clearly ahead of representative baselines on RealDeg-Bench under both single and compound degradations. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/GlobalForge-BE0F/.

Abstract: Automatic recognition of ambivalence and hesitancy is challenging because these states may be expressed through inconsistent linguistic, acoustic, facial, and contextual patterns, while top-performing systems often rely on computationally expensive ensembles. Text Residual Fusion treats text as the anchor modality and applies gated residual adjustments based on the other modalities. Experiments on the Behavioural Ambivalence/Hesitancy (BAH) corpus confirm that text is the strongest unimodal modality. As a result, they often suffer from unstable optimization, overfitting, and limited transferability. Similar to pretrained ResNet and Vision Transformer models in natural image learning, MIL also requires reusable pretrained initialization. However, high-quality slide-level pretraining data remain scarce, and MIL models are usually lightweight and weakly supervised, making large-scale pretraining difficult in practice. To address this challenge, we propose a distillation-based pretraining framework for MIL, which leverages two slide-level foundation models, TITAN and CARE, as teachers to transfer their representational knowledge into a diverse set of MIL architectures. The distilled weights are then used as initialization for downstream adaptation. We conduct systematic evaluations on 15 benchmark datasets under both linear probing and full-parameter fine-tuning, and further validate its advantages in few-shot scenarios. Experimental results show that pretraining generally improves MIL aggregators over from scratch training, especially in linear-probing and few-shot settings, while maintaining the computational efficiency of lightweight MIL models. Abstract: The bird's eye view (BEV) has emerged as a pivotal approach for environmental perception in autonomous driving, providing a unified spatial representation for vehicles. Nevertheless, despite BEV's significance in addressing the challenges inherent to autonomous driving, effectively fusing data from multiple camera sensors and operating in complex external driving environments remains a considerable challenge. To mitigate this issue, we recast the BEV segmentation problem within a variational inference framework. In this paper, we propose a novel transformer-based variational flow transformation network for BEV segmentation, denoted as TVB. Our architecture implicitly learns the mapping from multiple camera views to a unified canonical BEV map during training by exploiting posterior BEV supervision. TVB employs a conditional variational auto encoder (CVAE) as its backbone and produces multiple BEV map candidates. To augment the realism of the generated BEV maps, we integrate normalizing flows into the map generation process, enabling the construction of more complex and expressive probability distributions. Furthermore, we design a BEV-attention fusion (BAF) module that harnesses attention mechanisms to adaptively integrate the multiple candidate BEV maps. Experimental results, evaluated on both the nuScenes and OPV2Vdatasets, demonstrate that our proposed method achieves superior performance in multi-camera view BEV segmentation and lane environment perception.

### [39] [VideoSEMA: a scalable and efficient Mamba-like attention for video understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14711)
*Nhat Thanh Tran,Fanghui Xue andShuai Zhang,Jiancheng Lyu,Yunling Zheng,Yingyong Qi,Jack Xin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VideoSEMA模型，通过分离空间和时间注意力机制实现高效视频理解。空间部分采用类Mamba的局部窗口与全局平均并行的SEMA块，时间部分使用softmax注意力。理论证明在特定秩条件下，该方法等价于全空间-时间注意力。在K400和SSv2数据集上优于同类参数量的视觉变换器和Mamba模型，且在高分辨率下表现更稳定，适合扩展至长视频。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频理解模型如视觉变换器和Mamba在处理高分辨率或长视频时存在计算成本高、性能下降快的问题，亟需一种高效且可扩展的注意力机制以提升视频分类性能。

Method: 设计Split Space-Time Attention架构，空间部分采用Mamba-like SEMA块，结合局部窗口注意力与全局平均；时间部分使用softmax注意力。利用矩阵秩条件保证计算效率与全注意力等价性。

Result: 在K400和SSv2基准测试中，VideoSEMA在相同参数量下超越Vision Transformer和VideoMamba模型，尤其在高分辨率（1024²）下精度衰减更小，表现出更强的可扩展性。

Conclusion: VideoSEMA通过分离空间-时间注意力，在保持高性能的同时显著降低计算开销，具备良好的可扩展性与实用性，是视频理解任务中极具潜力的新范式。

Abstract: We present for video understanding (classification) a split space-time attention model, VideoSEMA, consisting of a scalable and efficient Mamba-like attention (SEMA) block in space and a softmax temporal attention in time. In each frame, SEMA attention applies a local window attention in parallel with a global averaging in a Mamba macro-architecture, which is called Mamba-like. Under certain rank conditions, we prove that the computationally cheaper split space-time attention is equivalent to full space-time attention. On benchmark K400 data sets, VideoSEMA out-performs heavier vision transformer and Mamba models. On benchmark SSv2 data, VideoSEMA leads in top-1 accuracy among models of similar parameter sizes. As image resolution scales up from standard $224^2$ to $1024^2$ on K400 and without fine-tuning, VideoSEMA degrades much more gracefully than VideoMamba in accuracy. It is promising to extend VideoSEMA to longer videos with a dilated/sparse temporal attention.

</details>


### [40] [Causal-Adversarial Probing of Clinical Covariates for Prostate MRI Grading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14720)
*Yipei Wang,Shiqi Huang,Wen Yan,Weixi Yi,Dean C. Barratt,Mark Emberton,Daniel C. Alexander,Veeru Kasivisvanathan,Yipeng Hu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于因果推理的框架，用于分析前列腺MRI-based ISUP分级模型中临床协变量的影响。通过对抗性方法抑制单个临床变量的可解码性，同时保持MRI分级预测性能，以区分非泛化性的捷径信息与真正相关的疾病信号。在2,903例MRI数据上训练并外部验证于576例患者，结果显示抑制年龄、BMI和饮酒史可提升AUC，表明这些变量可能引入非泛化性偏差；而抑制PSA和前列腺体积则显著降低AUC，说明其携带重要任务相关信号。该方法为深度学习模型中的协变量依赖性提供了可解释的分析工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习模型在前列腺MRI癌症分级中可能编码了临床协变量，但这些协变量的作用常被假设而未被检验。部分协变量可能反映非泛化性的捷径信息，而另一些则携带真实疾病信号。因此需要一种机制来区分两者，以提升模型的泛化能力和可解释性。

Method: 提出一种基于因果推理的对抗性框架，将MRI表现和ISUP分级视为潜在肿瘤病理的观测结果，通过逐个抑制特定临床协变量的可解码性，评估其对模型预测性能的影响，从而判断其是干扰项、疾病相关代理变量还是无关变量。

Result: 在二分类（ISUP GG ≥2）任务中，抑制年龄、BMI和饮酒史分别使AUC提升1.23%、0.84%和1.42%（均p<0.05），表明这些变量可能引入非泛化性偏差；抑制PSA和前列腺体积则使AUC下降1.91%和7.61%（均p<0.001），说明它们包含关键任务相关信号。

Conclusion: 对抗性协变量抑制方法能够有效揭示深度学习模型中协变量依赖性的本质，有助于识别有害的非泛化性信号与真正的疾病相关特征，从而提升模型的可解释性和泛化能力。

Abstract: Deep learning models for prostate MRI-based cancer grading may encode clinical covariates that either reflect useful disease-related signal or non-generalising shortcut information, but their role is usually assumed. We propose a causal-reasoning framework for probing covariate dependence in MRI-based International Society of Urological Pathology (ISUP) Grade Group prediction. Rather than treating mpMRI as a direct cause of grade, we model MRI appearance and ISUP grade as observations of latent tumour pathology, and test whether candidate clinical variables act as nuisance correlates, disease-related proxies, or irrelevant covariates in the learned representation. We implement this using an adversarial framework that suppresses the decodability of individual clinical covariate at a time while preserving MRI-based grade prediction. The approach is developed and evaluated on 2,903 prostate MRI examinations, with external validation on 576 patients. We report a set of interesting and previously under-explored imaging-to-clinical-variable interactions in the context of deep learning generalisation. For examples, in binary ISUP Grade Group $\geq2$ classification, suppressing age, BMI, and alcohol use improved AUC by 1.23%, 0.84%, and 1.42%, respectively (all p < 0.05), suggesting reduced non-generalising covariate information; In contrast, suppressing PSA and prostate volume degraded AUC by 1.91% and 7.61% (all p < 0.001), indicating that these variables carried task-relevant signal. These findings show that adversarial covariate suppression can provide a practical representation-level analysis for distinguishing potentially harmful dependence from informative signal in prostate MRI grading models.

### [41] [Multimodality as Supervision: Self-Supervised Specialization to the Test Environment via Multimodality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14721)
*Kunal Pratap Singh,Ali Garjani,Rishubh Singh,Muhammad Uzair Khattak,Efe Tarhan,Jason Toskov,Andrei Atanov,Oğuzhan Fatih Kar,Amir Zamir*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为Test-Space Training (TST)的自监督学习框架，通过在特定测试环境中收集多模态数据并利用跨模态学习进行预训练，实现对特定环境的模型优化。实验表明，在仅依赖测试环境数据的情况下，TST可达到与在大规模互联网数据上预训练的通用模型（如DINOv2和CLIP）相当的性能，从而减少对外部大规模数据集的依赖。研究还揭示了多模态数据在模型特化与泛化能力之间的权衡机制。

Conclusion: 在特定测试环境中，通过多模态数据收集与跨模态学习进行自监督预训练，可有效替代大规模互联网数据，实现高性能模型。这为减少对外部数据依赖、构建面向具体场景的专用智能系统提供了新路径。

Abstract: Cross-modal learning, i.e., learning to predict one modality from another, is a fundamental mechanism for self-supervision via leveraging multimodality. Many practical applications, e.g., deploying a household robot, involve devices that are equipped with a rich set of sensors that enable multimodal sensing in their test environment. This presents an opportunity to apply cross-modal learning to the multimodal data sensed by these devices to learn representations. Findings in developmental psychology also suggest that biological agents leverage it to build an effective representation of their surroundings.
  To study this, we propose a controlled setup, where we restrict a user device to just a given test environment. It results in a specialization setup where we attempt to develop a performant model for this specific test environment. Under this setup, we develop Test-Space Training (TST), which performs multimodal data collection in the test environment and performs self-supervised pre-training on it. We evaluate these models on various downstream tasks in the same environment.
  Under this setup, we find various interesting insights, such as collecting rich multimodal data only from the test environment and leveraging cross-modal learning, we can achieve competitive results with generalist models (e.g., DINOv2 and CLIP) pre-trained on large-scale internet datasets. This enables an alternative scenario where the need for external Internet-scale datasets for pre-training models is reduced. We also present a set of analyses and ablations that raise intriguing points on substituting data with (multi)modality, and how varying pre-training data enables a tradeoff between a model's abilities to specialise to a test environment, and generalize to held-out spaces.

### [42] [AE-UAV: An Air-to-Air Event-Based UAV Tracking Benchmark and a Real-Time Frequency-Domain Tracker](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14726)
*Zixin Jiang,Bing He,Chaoran Xiong,Zhenzhen Wang,Xin Zhao,Ling Pei*

Method: 提出Fast-Slow Frequency-domain Tracking (FSFT)框架，融合频域模板匹配、搜索区域预测与检测驱动的漂移校正，无需训练，可在CPU上高效运行。

Abstract: Air-to-air (A2A) unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) tracking is fundamental to airborne remote sensing of low-altitude aerial targets. However, the deployment of continuous, real-time tracking systems on UAVs presents significant challenges. In A2A scenarios, traditional frame-based cameras suffer from severe performance degradation under low illumination, overexposure, and high-speed motion owing to their limited dynamic range and fixed temporal sampling. Although event cameras offer a promising alternative with microsecond temporal resolution and a high dynamic range, current research is bottlenecked by two primary issues: 1) the absence of dedicated A2A event-based datasets, and 2) the heavy reliance of existing trackers on GPU acceleration and extensive training data, rendering them impractical for resource-constrained UAVs. To bridge these gaps, we introduce AE-UAV, an air-to-air event-based UAV tracking benchmark. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first airborne-captured event camera dataset for A2A tracking, comprising 178 flight sequences with continuous-time cubic B-spline annotations. Furthermore, we propose the Fast-Slow Frequency-domain Tracking (FSFT) method. This lightweight, training-free framework seamlessly integrates frequency-domain template matching with search region prediction and detection-based drift correction. Extensive experiments demonstrate that FSFT operates at an ultra-fast 420 frames per second (FPS) on CPU-only hardware. It retains 93.97% of the accuracy of state-of-the-art GPU-dependent methods while delivering a 5.32-fold effective speedup and exhibiting superior temporal resolution generalization, thereby providing a highly efficient and robust solution for airborne remote sensing of aerial targets. The dataset and source code are available at https://github.com/MSP-xEN/AE-UAV.

We propose WorkDrive, a framework that constructs perception-grounded causal reasoning for work zones and aligns it with trajectory prediction. The resulting reasoning labels are used for supervised fine-tuning, followed by reinforcement learning with a single reward: consistency between lateral meta-actions and the predicted trajectory. ### [45] [GeoDetect: Geometric Adversarial Detection for VLPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14737)
*Afsaneh Hasanebrahimi,Hanxun Huang,Christopher Leckie,James Bailey,Sarah Erfani*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究视觉-语言预训练模型（VLPs）的嵌入空间几何特性，发现其存在与单模态视觉模型不同的结构化各向异性。理论分析表明，在这种各向异性结构下，对抗攻击会增加干净样本与对抗样本之间的预期几何距离。基于此，本文提出GeoDetect方法，利用几何分数检测对抗样本，通过大量实验验证了该方法在多种VLP架构和攻击场景下的有效性，包括单模态、多模态及自适应攻击，显著提升了模型的安全性与可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对抗检测方法在单模态场景中表现良好，但在多模态视觉-语言预训练模型（VLPs）中的适用性和可靠性尚未得到充分研究，亟需针对VLPs的特殊结构设计有效的对抗检测机制。

Method: 通过分析VLP嵌入空间的几何特性，揭示其结构化各向异性；理论推导表明对抗样本倾向于远离数据流形，导致其与随机采样点的平均距离更大；据此提出基于几何分数的GeoDetect方法，利用这一离群特征识别对抗样本。

Result: GeoDetect在多种VLP架构和攻击类型（包括单模态、多模态及自适应攻击）上均表现出高检测率和鲁棒性，能够有效识别对抗样本，显著提升VLPs的安全性。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了VLP嵌入空间的内在几何特性，并提出了一个基于几何偏离的通用对抗检测框架GeoDetect，为多模态模型的对抗防御提供了可靠且可推广的技术方案。

Abstract: Vision-language pre-trained models (VLPs) are widely used in real-world applications. However, they remain vulnerable to adversarial attacks. Although adversarial detection methods have demonstrated success in single-modality settings (either vision or language), their effectiveness and reliability in multimodal models such as VLPs remain largely unexplored. In this work, we study the geometry of VLP embedding spaces and observe structured anisotropy that differs from unimodal vision models. Our theoretical analysis shows that under this anisotropic structure, adversarial attacks increase the expected geometric separation between clean and adversarial examples (AEs). Specifically, we demonstrate that AEs consistently exhibit greater expected distances to randomly sampled points than their clean counterparts, indicating that AEs tend to push representations out of manifold regions. Building on these insights, we propose GeoDetect, which leverages these off-manifold deviations via geometric scores to identify AEs. Through comprehensive evaluations, we show that our approach reliably detects AEs across diverse VLP architectures and threat settings, covering unimodal and multimodal attacks as well as adaptive attacks, thereby providing a robust and practical approach to improving the safety and reliability of these models.

### [46] [FoMoVLA: Bridging Visual Foresight and Motion Guidance for Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14739)
*Wei Li,Peijin Jia,Yuan Ma,Xuefeng Jiang,Titong Jiang,Sheng Sun,Yujian Li,Xin Wen,Han Hong,Zhikang Liu,Bailin Li,Kun Zhan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FoMoVLA 提出一种新框架，通过联合学习未来特征预测和稀疏2D点跟踪，增强视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型的前瞻性能力。该方法引入紧凑的前瞻标记解码未来特征状态，并通过解码稀疏时空2D点轨迹建模几何运动路径，利用轻量级未来条件交叉注意力模块实现状态与运动的一致推理。在LIBERO、RoboCasa GR-1 Tabletop 和 LIBERO-Plus 上的实验表明，该方法达到当前最优性能并具备强大的零样本泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型缺乏对世界动态的显式前向预测，而现有的视觉预见方法虽能预测未来视觉状态但缺少明确的动作引导，无法提供如何到达目标的路径信息。因此，需要结合目标状态预测与连续运动路径建模，以提升策略的前瞻性与可控性。

Method: FoMoVLA 通过引入紧凑的未来特征标记来解码未来特征状态，同时解码稀疏的2D点轨迹以建模几何运动路径，并使用轻量级未来条件交叉注意力模块将两者耦合，实现对未来状态与运动动态的一致性推理。

Result: 在LIBERO、RoboCasa GR-1 Tabletop 和 LIBERO-Plus 数据集上均取得领先性能，且表现出优异的零样本泛化能力，验证了方法的有效性和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 未来特征预测与稀疏点跟踪具有天然互补性，通过联合建模可显著提升VLA模型的前瞻性与连续动作规划能力。FoMoVLA 为构建更具前瞻性的智能体提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have achieved impressive results in visuomotor policy learning, yet remain fundamentally reactive, mapping current observations and language to actions without explicit forward prediction of world dynamics. Existing visual foresight methods predict future visual states but lack explicit motion guidance: they show where to go but not how to get there. We argue that future feature prediction and sparse point tracking are naturally complementary: the former provides the goal state, while the latter captures the continuous motion path toward it. We propose FoMoVLA, a framework that augments VLA representations with explicit spatio-temporal supervision by jointly learning future feature foresight and sparse 2D point tracking, enhancing the continuous action policy. FoMoVLA introduces compact foresight tokens to decode future feature states, decodes sparse temporal 2D point trajectories to model compact geometric motion, and couples both through a lightweight future-conditioned cross-attention module that enables consistent reasoning between anticipated states and point dynamics. Extensive experiments on LIBERO, RoboCasa GR-1 Tabletop, and LIBERO-Plus demonstrate state-of-the-art performance and strong zero-shot generalization. Project page is available at https://liauto-research.github.io/FoMoVLA.
