### [131] [D-cut: Adaptive Verification Depth Pruning for Batched Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14647)
*Tianyu Liu,Yuhao Shen,Rui Cen,Junhan Shi,Jiebin Zhang,Guangshuo Qin,Hong Liu,Song Liu,Guanghua Yu,Jianchen Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: D-Cut提出一种自适应剪枝方法，通过跨请求联合选择草案令牌并根据验证预算动态分配，以应对高并发下长草案带来的计算浪费问题。该方法结合运行时成本模型，根据硬件环境和请求特性自适应调整剪枝深度，在密集模型和MoE模型上显著提升推理速度，最高实现3.0倍于自回归解码的加速效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高并发场景下，传统长草案方法因大量拒绝令牌导致验证开销过高，反而使推测解码慢于自回归解码；因此需要一种能动态分配验证资源、适应不同请求和部署环境的自适应剪枝机制。

Method: D-Cut采用跨请求的联合剪枝策略，基于草案置信度动态分配验证预算，并引入运行时成本模型以适配不同GPU架构与并行策略，从而优化验证过程的效率。

Result: 实验表明，在高并发下D-Cut将平均加速比从1.26×提升至1.65×，在密集模型中恢复了推测解码的优势，并在MoE模型上实现了最高3.0×的加速，显著优于基线方法。

Conclusion: D-Cut通过自适应剪枝与环境感知的验证预算分配，有效缓解了高并发下推测解码的性能瓶颈，为大规模语言模型高效推理提供了实用且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates large language model (LLM) inference without compromising output quality. Recent parallel drafting methods further improve single-request performance by decoupling draft length from drafting latency, enabling longer drafts and higher mean accepted tokens (MAT). However, under high request concurrency, long drafts waste substantial computation on rejected tokens, increasing verification cost and potentially making speculative decoding slower than autoregressive decoding. We present D-Cut, an adaptive pruning method that selects draft tokens jointly across the batch and concentrates the verification budget on tokens most likely to be accepted. D-Cut is motivated by two observations. First, acceptance lengths vary considerably across concurrent requests; D-Cut therefore performs cross-request pruning, allocating the verification budget adaptively according to draft confidence. Second, verification cost depends strongly on the deployment environment, including GPU architecture and parallelism strategy; D-Cut incorporates a runtime cost model to adapt its pruning depth to the target environment. Experiments on dense and mixture-of-experts (MoE) models show that, under high concurrency, D-Cut improves the average speedup from \(1.26\times\) to \(1.65\times\), restores acceleration in dense-model configurations where long-draft baselines are slower than autoregressive decoding, and achieves up to \(3.0\times\) speedup over autoregressive decoding on MoE models.

### [132] [Harnessing LLMs for Reliable Academic Supervision: A Comparative Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14707)
*Akash Raj*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文通过案例研究探讨了在学术指导领域中，如何通过“ harness engineering”（框架工程）提升小型大语言模型（如GPT-4o-mini）的可靠性与可审计性。相比无框架的大型模型（ASA），采用多模块框架（ASuS）的小型模型在六个评估维度（可追溯性、可解释性、一致性、流程完整性、认知负荷、约束遵守）上全面胜出，且其性能不受基础模型大小影响，验证了框架设计的普适价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型虽能生成流畅回答，但在高风险决策系统中缺乏可靠性、可审计性和流程一致性；需通过结构化框架弥补这一差距，尤其在学术指导这类需长期责任追踪和规范操作的场景中。

Method: 构建基于LangGraph的多模块系统ASuS，集成符号-语义检索、模式验证输出、LLM作为裁判的有限重试机制、人工介入（HITL）门控、确定性加权风险评分及节点级SQLite审计日志，并与无框架的GPT-5基线（ASA）进行盲评对比，辅以2×2模型-框架消融实验。

Result: ASuS在所有六项评估维度上显著优于ASA，十位评审者平均得分分别为4.08 vs 1.23，8位评审在配对威尔科克森检验中拒绝零假设（p<0.05）。消融实验表明框架贡献具有模型无关性。

Conclusion: 当可靠性、可追溯性和制度一致性比开放流畅性更重要时，框架工程挑战了‘越大越好’的模型观念，证明精心设计的系统架构能显著提升小模型的实际应用效能。

Abstract: Large language models routinely produce fluent answers to single-shot prompts, yet deploying them as reliable components of a domain decision system is substantially harder. Closing this gap is the work of harness engineering: the deliberate composition of deterministic scaffolding (symbolic filters, retrieval, schema-typed I/O, LLM-as-judge loops, HITL gates, persistent state, audit trails) around an LLM core. We present a case study in academic supervision, a domain combining high-stakes recommendation, longitudinal accountability, and structured operational workflows.
  We compare a baseline (ASA), a GPT-5 chatbot with no scaffolding, against a multi-module system (ASuS) that wraps the much smaller GPT-4o-mini in a LangGraph harness with symbolic-semantic retrieval, schema-validated outputs, LLM-as-judge with bounded retry, HITL gates, deterministic weighted risk scoring with LLM narration, and a per-node SQLite audit trail. The evaluation rubric is retargeted at six harness-mechanism dimensions (grounding, explainability, consistency, process integrity, cognitive load, constraint adherence). A blind ten-rater hybrid evaluation, supplemented by a 2 x 2 model-harness ablation, finds that ASuS, despite using a much smaller base model, outscores ASA on every dimension. Across ten raters the pooled mean for ASuS is 4.08 versus 1.23 for ASA, and 8 of 10 raters reject the null at alpha = 0.05 on a paired Wilcoxon test; full numbers are in Sections 6.4 and 6.7. The ablation confirms that the structural contributions of the harness are largely model-invariant. We extract seven recurring harness-engineering patterns and argue that where reliability, traceability, and institutional consistency matter more than open-ended fluency, harness engineering challenges the prevailing 'bigger model is better' intuition.

### [133] [Gold-Guided Programmatic Distillation for Financial Reasoning over Hybrid Tables and Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14709)
*Yun Dong,Erica Zhao,Elana Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于执行验证的程序化蒸馏方法，通过可靠数值推理的Python程序而非自由文本推理解释，将大型教师模型的知识迁移到小型学生模型中。该方法利用精确答案引导程序合成，并仅保留可正确执行且产生正确答案的程序，确保高质量监督信号。此外引入迭代恢复阶段，重新处理教师失败的样本，使学生能学习新验证的程序。在TAT-QA数据集上的实验表明，该框架在混合金融推理任务上表现优异，最佳7B学生模型在测试集上达到87.00 EM / 87.18 F1，显著优于72B教师模型（78.46 EM）及现有强基线模型（如TAGOP和TAT-LLM），证明了执行验证的程序化蒸馏在训练小型模型实现可靠数值推理方面的有效性与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统自然语言推理容易出现算术错误，不适合作为大模型到小模型蒸馏的监督信号；而金融问答任务需要多源推理和精确数值计算，因此亟需一种更可靠的监督方式来提升小模型的数值推理能力。

Method: 采用执行验证的Python程序作为监督信号，通过黄金推导路径引导教师模型生成程序，只保留能够正确执行并产出正确答案的程序进行蒸馏；引入迭代恢复机制，对教师失败案例重新分析，获取新验证的程序以增强学生模型的学习能力。

Result: 在TAT-QA数据集上，7B学生模型达到87.00 EM / 87.18 F1，显著优于72B教师模型（78.46 EM）以及现有主流方法（如TAGOP、TAT-LLM），验证了方法的有效性和优越性。

Conclusion: 执行验证的程序化蒸馏提供了一种高效、可扩展的框架，使小型模型能够学习并具备可靠的数值推理能力，尤其适用于涉及复杂计算和多源信息融合的金融问答任务。

Abstract: Financial question answering over hybrid tabular and textual data may require multi-source reasoning and precise numerical computation. While large language models (LLMs) can generate intermediate reasoning steps, natural-language rationales remain prone to arithmetic errors, making them an unreliable supervision source for distillation. Building on programmatic distillation, we develop an approach that transfers reliable numerical reasoning from a large teacher model to a compact student using execution-verified Python programs instead of free-form textual rationales. It leverages gold derivations to guide teacher-side program synthesis and retains only programs that execute correctly and produce the gold answer, ensuring high-quality supervision. We further introduce an iterative recovery stage that revisits teacher-failed examples, enabling the student to recover and incorporate newly verified programs into training. Experiments on TAT-QA show that our framework is highly effective for hybrid financial reasoning. Our best 7B student achieves 87.00 EM / 87.18 F1 on the test set, substantially outperforming the 72B teacher (78.46 EM) as well as traditional and strong LLM-based baselines, including TAGOP and TAT-LLM. These results demonstrate that execution-verified programmatic distillation provides an effective and extensible framework for training smaller models to perform reliable numerical reasoning.

</details>

Conclusion: AI检测模型可能存在对自闭症写作者的系统性偏见，其广泛应用可能带来伦理风险。建议对模型本身及其在学术场景中的使用进行更深入的批判性审视。

In the present study, anecdotal claims that autistic writers more often have their work flagged as AI-generated are examined empirically. A corpus of approximately 60,000 Reddit posts split into "likely-autistic" and "general-Reddit" subcorpora is used to compare the distribution of probabilities output by the OpenAI GPT-2 detection model. Differences in textual features between subcorpora are observed and compared to reported features of AI-generated text. Results showed that while less than two-percent of either subcorpus was flagged as AI-generated by the model, significantly more texts from the likely-autistic subcorpus were flagged. Connections between features of text with likely-autistic authors and AI-generated text were not straightforward. The widespread use of AI-detection models with a potential bias against autistic writers in their output prompts ethical scrutiny, and the authors recommend further critical examination of the models themselves as well as their use in academic contexts.

### [135] [CoTu at EXACT 2026: Neuro-Symbolic Reasoning for Transparent Educational QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14735)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Transparent educational question answering asks for answers that are not only correct but explainable, and doing so with small models rules out the reasoning power of the largest proprietary systems. The EXACT 2026 competition poses this problem concretely: open-weight language models of at most 8B parameters, self-hosted, with a natural-language explanation for every answer. It pairs two tasks: logical reasoning over university regulations, and multi-step physics problem solving. We describe the system that team \cotu{} developed to address both, a neuro-symbolic Program-of-Thought pipeline in which a 4B backbone writes a program rather than stating an answer directly: for regulation queries it emits a Z3 encoding whose entailment verdict grounds the deduction, and for physics it emits numerical Python, both wrapped in a shared self-correction loop and a unified explained-JSON output. Answer-type routing, distillation-based task fine-tuning, and a latency-aware serving stack -- SGLang with speculative decoding -- keep the system within the 60-second per-query limit. The system achieved a \textbf{perfect score} on the physics task in both automated selection rounds and obtained the \textbf{highest final-round technical score} of any team -- $13.44/15$, combining automated answer evaluation with expert-judged reasoning depth -- with the equally weighted presentation score included, \cotu{} placed 3rd overall. Grounding answers in a symbolic solver yields correct, verifiable deductions at the 4B scale, and the residual difficulty lies in premise selection rather than the deduction itself.

### [136] [Dialogue Summarization with Emotion Dynamics Using Topic- and Participant-Centric Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14769)
*Linyun Xiang,Mark Neerincx,Stephanie Tan*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 实验结果表明，该框架在小语言模型上能够生成既包含语义内容又体现情感轨迹的高质量对话摘要。引入的情感轨迹度量有效提升了评估维度，验证了方法的有效性与在对话分析中的应用潜力。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了一个能够同时捕捉对话语义与情感动态的摘要框架，证明了多模态输入和情感建模在对话摘要中的重要性，为未来基于语言模型的对话理解与分析提供了新思路。

Abstract: Existing text summarization research has focused much on monologic information (e.g., newspaper articles, reports) without accounting for the interaction between speakers or authors. In contrast, dialogues are a rich communication channel where multiple participants conduct back and forth exchanges to construct meaning. We propose a dialogue summarization framework that explicitly models both semantic and emotion dynamics using multimodal dialogue inputs, built on an adapted hierarchical Chain-of-Agents approach. We decompose dialogues from two perspectives: (1) topic segments based on the utterances of all participants, and (2) participant-specific utterance segments. These are used to generate corresponding summaries while incorporating automatically inferred emotions. Topic- and participant-level summaries are aggregated into a dialogue summary capturing semantic content and emotion trajectories. To evaluate beyond content accuracy, we introduce emotion trajectory metrics measuring how well summaries preserve emotional flow. Experiments with small language models on multimodal dialogue datasets show that our framework produces summaries with both semantic and emotion content. Further experiments on explicit emotion label availability highlight the efficacy of our proposed methodology and the opportunities in dialogue analysis using language models.

### [137] [SEED: Self-Evolving On-Policy Distillation for Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14777)
*Jinyang Wu,Shuo Yang,Zhengxi Lu,Fan Zhang,Yuhao Shen,Lang Feng,Haoran Luo,Zheng Lian,Shuai Zhang,Zhengqi Wen,Jianhua Tao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SEED提出一种自进化在线策略蒸馏框架，通过将完成的轨迹转化为训练时的后见技能，并将其行为效应回传给策略模型，以解决长时程任务中稀疏奖励导致的中间决策监督不足问题。该方法在强化学习过程中同时收集轨迹并分析生成自然语言技能，利用技能诱导的概率变化构建密集的令牌级蒸馏信号，与结果导向的强化学习联合优化，提升决策能力和样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决大语言模型在长时程交互任务中因稀疏轨迹级奖励导致的中间决策监督不足问题，填补任务结果与令牌级策略学习之间的监督鸿沟。

Method: SEED首先微调策略模型以分析已完成轨迹，生成捕捉可复用工作流、关键观察或避错规则的自然语言技能；在强化学习过程中，当前策略同时负责收集轨迹和提取后见技能；通过重新评分采样动作在普通和技能增强上下文下的概率，将技能引起的概率偏移转换为密集的令牌级在线策略蒸馏信号，并与结果导向强化学习联合优化。

Result: 在文本和视觉基础的代理任务上，SEED显著提升了性能和样本效率，展现出对未见场景的强大泛化能力。

Conclusion: SEED通过自进化式技能提取与蒸馏，实现了后见监督随策略演化的动态对齐，有效缓解了稀疏奖励带来的学习瓶颈，为复杂交互任务中的高效策略学习提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly trained as interactive agents for long-horizon tasks involving multi-turn interaction, tool use, and environment feedback. Outcome-based reinforcement learning (RL) provides a practical optimization paradigm, but its sparse trajectory-level rewards offer limited guidance on intermediate decisions, leaving a supervision gap between episode-level outcomes and token-level policy learning. We propose SEED (SElf-Evolving On-Policy Distillation), a self-evolving framework that converts completed on-policy trajectories into training-time hindsight skills and distills their behavioral effect back into the policy model. SEED first fine-tunes the policy to analyze completed trajectories and generate natural-language skills that capture reusable workflows, decisive observations, or failure-avoidance rules. During RL, the current policy both collects trajectories and serves as the analyzer that extracts hindsight skills from them. Policy updates therefore improve subsequent decision making and skill analysis together, allowing hindsight supervision to evolve with the policy. SEED then re-scores the sampled actions under ordinary and skill-augmented contexts, converting the skill-induced probability shift into a dense token-level on-policy distillation signal. This signal is jointly optimized with outcome-based RL, keeping the auxiliary supervision aligned with the current trajectory distribution. Extensive experiments on text-based and vision-based agentic tasks show that SEED consistently improves performance and sample efficiency, exhibiting robust generalization to unseen scenarios. Our code is available at https://github.com/jinyangwu/SEED.

</details>

### [139] [Latent Trajectory Discrimination for AI-Generated Text Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14967)
*Gianluca Bonifazi,Christopher Buratti,Michele Marchetti,Federica Parlapiano,Giulia Quaglieri,Davide Traini,Domenico Ursino,Luca Virgili*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出GTCL框架，通过建模文本生成过程中的潜在空间动态轨迹来改进AI生成文本检测。与传统静态表示方法不同，GTCL将文档分割为有序局部单元，编码每个单元并构建序列级结构化表示，利用对比学习捕捉自回归生成的几何规律。实验表明，该方法在多个基准上优于现有基线，证明了显式建模序列动态性的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI生成文本检测方法将文档视为静态对象，依赖全局统计或压缩嵌入，忽略了自回归生成过程中内容在潜在空间中的动态演化特性。因此，亟需一种能够捕捉生成轨迹动态性的新方法。

Method: 提出Geometric Trajectory and Contrastive Learning (GTCL)框架，将文档分段为有序局部单元，对每单元进行嵌入编码，构建序列级结构化表示，并通过对比学习挖掘自回归生成的几何规律。

Result: GTCL在三个不同基准和多种方法上均显著优于现有基线，验证了建模生成轨迹动态性可提供鲁棒且跨模型、跨领域的判别信号。

Conclusion: 显式建模生成轨迹差异能有效提升AI生成文本检测性能，为该领域开辟了动态分析的新方向，具有重要研究价值。

Abstract: Most existing approaches to AI-Generated Text Detection (AIGTD) treat documents as static objects and base their decisions on aggregate statistics or globally compressed embeddings. However, this perspective overlooks the inherently dynamic nature of autoregressive generation, where content evolves progressively through the latent space. In this paper, we reformulate AIGTD as the problem of distinguishing between latent generation trajectories. Instead of relying on static representations, we model how textual representations evolve across the sequence. To this end, we propose Geometric Trajectory and Contrastive Learning (GTCL), a framework that segments the document into ordered local units, encodes each unit in an embedding space, and constructs a structured and sequence-level representation. GTCL then applies contrastive learning to these trajectories to learn geometric regularities associated with the autoregressive generation. Evaluations performed on three different benchmarks and several approaches show that GTCL outperforms detection baselines consistently, which implies that explicitly modeling sequential dynamics provides robust discriminative signals across models and domains. These results suggest that modeling trajectory differences could improve detection and open up a dynamic direction that has been underexplored in previous AIGTD literature.

### [140] [OmniaBench: Benchmarking General AI Agents Across Diverse Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14989)

TL;DR: OmniaBench 是一个针对通用智能体的综合性基准测试，涵盖多样化的应用场景和明确的状态空间。它基于应用商店、产品文档等多源数据构建了包含90个一级和354个二级领域的层级分类体系，并通过四种方法生成单轮与多轮任务，形成1,431个任务的数据集。该基准引入十维能力分类与八种组合式难度因子，支持精细化评估。尽管前沿模型如Claude-Sonnet-5和GPT-5.6-Sol在整体通过率上仅达58.54%和57.14%，仍暴露出规划、约束维持和自适应修正等方面的显著局限。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: OmniaBench 提供了一个广泛且具有诊断性的基准，能够有效刻画通用智能体的能力边界，有助于推动其在复杂现实场景中的发展与优化。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly evolving from text generators into general agents capable of understanding user requests, invoking external tools, and completing complex tasks through interaction. However, existing agent benchmarks often focus on limited scenarios, tool ecosystems, or interaction formats, making it difficult to systematically characterize model capabilities across heterogeneous application settings. We introduce OmniaBench, a benchmark for evaluating general agents across diverse scenarios with explicit state spaces. We derive application-oriented scenario knowledge from app stores, product documents, industry resources, Web retrieval, and human refinement, forming a hierarchical taxonomy that spans ToC, ToB and ToE with 90 level-1 and 354 level-2 domains. Based on this taxonomy, we construct executable environments and synthesize single-turn and multi-turn tasks through four complementary routes: DAG, DAG-S, Solver, and Program. OmniaBench further introduces a ten-dimensional capability taxonomy and eight compositional atomic difficulty factors to support fine-grained evaluation and analysis. The resulting dataset contains 1,431 tasks, together with a challenging subset of 644 tasks designed to reduce evaluation cost and mitigate potential contamination of the full set after public release. The bench presents substantial challenges to current frontier models, with even Claude-Sonnet-5 and GPT-5.6-Sol achieving Overall Pass@1 scores of only 58.54 and 57.14, respectively. Further analyses reveal clear differences across domains and capabilities, as well as persistent limitations in planning, constraint maintenance, and adaptive correction. OmniaBench provides a broad and diagnostic benchmark for characterizing the capability boundaries of general agents.

### [141] [Rubrics on Trial: Evolving Rubrics from a Single Query via Synthetic Pairwise Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15092)
*Haocheng Yang,Licheng Pan,Xiaoxi Li,Zhichao Chen,Zhiheng Zhang,Yuan Lu,Haoxuan Li,Hao Wang*

TL;DR: Rubrics on Trial 是一种无需外部标注或模型训练的查询-仅框架，通过合成的基于评分标准的响应对来生成并验证评分标准，从而在不依赖人类编写评分标准、偏好数据或采样响应的情况下，自动演化出有效的评分标准集。该方法可有效筛选出无区分性、过度具体或仅关注风格的无效评分标准，实验表明其在多个基准测试中表现优异，平均准确率最高，并在七项评估中的六项上领先。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的评分标准构建方法依赖于人工编写的评分标准、偏好数据或采样响应，成本高且难以保证质量。直接从查询生成评分标准虽避免了外部资源，但无法确保生成的评分标准具有实际判别能力，可能无法区分答案质量，甚至奖励非必要风格或惩罚合理替代策略。因此需要一种无需外部监督、能自动验证并筛选有效评分标准的方法。

Method: Rubrics on Trial 采用查询-仅框架，从空的评分标准集开始，通过生成合成的评分标准条件下的响应对作为内部监督信号，动态演化评分标准集合。每轮迭代中，新提出的评分标准会经过验证流程，筛选掉无区分性、过于具体或仅关注风格的无效标准，确保最终保留的标准具备实际判别能力。

Result: 在五个偏好基准套件上的实验表明，Rubrics on Trial 在平均准确率上达到最佳，并在七项评估中的六项上取得领先，证明其在生成高质量、实用评分标准方面的有效性。

Conclusion: Rubrics on Trial 成功实现了无需外部标注和模型训练的评分标准自动生成与验证，能够有效生成具有判别力且实用的评分标准，为大语言模型的训练与评估提供了高效、可靠的自动化工具。

Abstract: Rubrics provide structured, fine-grained signals for training and evaluating large language models (LLMs). Yet reliable query-specific rubrics are difficult to construct. Existing approaches often derive supervision from human-written rubrics, preference data, or sampled responses. Direct query-to-rubric generation avoids these resources, but provides no explicit check that a plausible rubric is useful. Such a rubric may fail to distinguish answer quality, reward an optional style, or penalize a valid alternative strategy. We introduce Rubrics on Trial, a query-only framework that evolves a rubric set from an empty set without external annotations or model training. It derives supervision solely from synthetic rubric-conditioned response pairs and validates each proposed rubric before adding it, screening out non-discriminative, over-specific, and style-only candidate rubrics. Experiments across five preference benchmark suites demonstrate the effectiveness of Rubrics on Trial, which achieves the best average accuracy and leads on six of seven evaluation sets.

</details>


### [142] [Digital Pantheon: Simulating and Auditing Coalition Formation with LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15095)
*Dylan Van Mulders,Matthias Bogaert,Dirk Van den Poel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多智能体框架，结合SFT、DPO和RAG技术，使大语言模型在政治联盟谈判中保持党派立场一致性，同时确保政策主张基于各政党官方纲领。通过2019年弗拉芒选举案例，构建了以形式领导人为核心的协商系统，并引入MILT拓扑结构追踪协议条款的来源，评估各党影响力与现实契合度。三次模拟结果稳定，预测排名与历史实际一致，证明该框架可作为前瞻性政党兼容性与妥协机制的透明、可扩展测试平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型因RLHF训练导致中立性与助人偏见，难以真实模拟政党间具有坚定意识形态立场的政治谈判。为克服此问题，需构建能兼顾事实准确性和党派一致性的计算模型，以支持对政治联盟形成过程的仿真与分析。

Method: 采用监督微调（SFT）、直接偏好优化（DPO）和检索增强生成（RAG）相结合的方法，为每个政党构建具有强烈党派特征的代理；通过每党专属的RAG管道确保其言论源自官方纲领；利用枢纽-辐射式协商结构由形式领导人协调谈判；引入多层信息溯源拓扑（MILT），追踪协议条款的起源并分类其出处状态；计算联盟影响得分（CIS）量化各党贡献；最后通过历史协议对比验证模拟结果的真实性。

Result: 在2019年弗拉芒选举的三次独立模拟中，框架稳定产生相同胜者排序（N-VA领先于CD&V和Open Vld），且基于纲领的溯源路径能有效预测真实政策落地情况，而虚构内容则无法实现。该方法实现了高透明度、可解释的政党联盟模拟，具备良好的现实对应性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了一个兼具事实准确性与党派一致性的多智能体政治谈判框架，通过可追溯的协议生成与验证机制，为政党兼容性评估和形式领导人角色研究提供了可靠的计算实验平台，推动了计算政治科学的发展。

Abstract: The formation of political coalitions is a complex negotiation driven by both concrete policy objectives and deep-seated ideological convictions. While Large Language Models (LLMs) open new avenues for computational political science, the neutrality and helpfulness biases instilled by Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) prevent them from sustaining steadfast partisan behaviour. We present a multi-agent framework that reconciles factual grounding with ideological alignment by combining Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT), Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), and Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG): DPO instils aggressive party-specific personas, while a per-party RAG pipeline keeps each agent bounded to its official manifesto. We operationalize the framework on the 2019 Flemish election, deploying the partisan agents in a hub-and-spoke negotiation arbitrated by a formateur. To make the emergent negotiation interpretable, we introduce a Multi-Layered Information Lineage Topology (MILT) that traces every clause in the final agreement back to its manifesto origin and classifies it into five provenance states, a Coalition Influence Score (CIS) that aggregates these traceable contributions to identify which party shaped the agreement, and a real-world grounding pass that benchmarks each simulated provision against the historically adopted coalition agreement. Across three independent simulations the framework yields a stable winner and ranking (N-VA ahead of CD\&V and Open Vld), and manifesto-anchored lineage reliably predicts real-world materialization whereas hallucinated content does not. The result is a transparent, scalable testbed for the ex-ante exploration of party compatibility and formateur-mediated compromise.

Abstract: Online encyclopedias shape political opinion and, through it, democratic discourse. In late 2025, Grokipedia was released, an encyclopedia written entirely by the LLM Grok. ### [144] [Linear representations of grammaticality in neural language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15175)
*Jane Li,Najoung Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨神经语言模型（NLMs）是否能通过内部表示区分语法正确与错误的句子，突破以往依赖概率比较的评估方法。通过大规模均值探测（mass-mean probing），研究发现语法正确与错误句子在表示空间中存在系统性分离，且这种分离不能完全由词汇频率、语义合理性等其他因素解释。该编码在多种语法现象和部分语言间具有泛化能力，表明语法性在现代NLMs中构成一个连贯的表征维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多依赖概率比较来判断语言模型对语法性的理解，但概率受多种相关因素影响，如词汇频率、语义合理性等，因此无法有效区分语法知识与其它语言属性。为更准确评估语言模型的语法知识，需探索其内部表示是否独立编码了语法性。

Method: 采用大规模均值探测（mass-mean probing）方法，分析不同语法类型句子在预训练语言模型内部表示空间中的分布差异，检验语法性是否形成独立于其他句子属性的可分离表征维度，并考察其跨语法现象和跨语言的泛化能力。

Result: 结果显示，语法正确与错误句子在表示空间中存在显著分离，且该分离无法完全由词汇频率、语义合理性等替代因素解释；该语法性表征在多种语法现象中保持一致，并在一定程度上跨语言泛化，表明语法性是当代预训练语言模型中一个稳健且连贯的表征维度。

Conclusion: 语法性被稳健地编码在预训练语言模型的内部表示中，构成一个独立且可泛化的表征维度。这一发现为理解语言模型的句法知识提供了新证据，并建立了一种不依赖字符串概率的语法能力评估框架。

Abstract: Whether neural language models (NLMs) possess the ability to distinguish strings on the basis of their grammaticality remains a debated topic in the computational linguistics literature. Existing evidence has largely relied on probability-based measures, testing whether models assign higher probabilities to grammatical than ungrammatical strings. However, probability comparisons have been criticized as a measure for grammatical knowledge based on the assumption that grammaticality is inherently entangled with likelihood. Model-assigned probability is a function of many related sentence properties, such as lexical frequency, plausibility, and world knowledge. In this work, we move beyond probability-based evaluations and investigate whether grammaticality is encoded in the internal representations of NLMs. Using mass-mean probing, we test whether grammatical and ungrammatical sentences are systematically separated in representational space. We further examine the extent to which these representations are independent of sentence properties that are correlated with grammaticality, as well as their generalization across grammatical phenomena and languages. Our results provide evidence that grammaticality is robustly encoded in sentence representations of a wide range of pretrained NLMs, yielding clear representational separation on the dimension of grammaticality that cannot be fully explained by alternative sentence-level factors. Moreover, this encoding generalizes across a broad range of grammatical phenomena and to some degree, across languages, suggesting that grammaticality constitutes a coherent representational dimension in contemporary NLMs. These findings contribute new evidence to debates about the nature of syntactic knowledge in language models and offer a complementary framework for evaluating grammatical competence that is not dependent on string probabilities alone.

### [145] [T^2MLR: Transformer with Temporal Middle-Layer Recurrence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15178)
*Ziyang Cai,Xingyu Zhu,Yihe Dong,Yinghui He,Sanjeev Arora*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: T2MLR提出一种基于Transformer的潜在推理架构，通过将前一token的中间层表示缓存并直接融合到当前token的早期层中，实现中间推理状态在解码过程中的持久化，且推理开销极低。该方法在自然语言预训练和多跳推理微调任务中均优于基线模型，即使仅对局部中间层（如20%网络）引入递归也能超越全层递归。更重要的是，T2MLR无需从头预训练，仅需对已有1.7B参数的预训练模型进行少量微调即可显著提升数学推理能力，降低了实际应用门槛。结果表明，有效的潜在推理不依赖于遍历所有层的循环机制，而是可通过有目标的中间层递归来更强地涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer的自回归解码过程会反复压缩丰富的隐藏计算，导致中间推理状态难以跨时间步持续存在，限制了其推理能力。

Method: 提出T2MLR架构，将前一token的中间层表示缓存，并直接融合至当前token的较早层，实现中间计算状态的跨步骤保留，同时保持低推理开销。

Result: T2MLR在自然语言预训练和多跳推理任务中均优于参数与数据匹配的Transformer基线；局部中间层递归（如20%网络）表现常优于全层递归；对现有1.7B模型进行轻量级微调即可显著提升数学推理性能。

Conclusion: 有效的潜在推理不必依赖全层循环机制，而可通过有针对性的中间层递归来更有效地实现，显著提升推理能力且易于部署。

Abstract: Transformer reasoning is limited by autoregressive decoding, which repeat edly compresses rich hidden computation through token space and makes it difficult for intermediate reasoning states to persist across time. We in troduce Transformers with Temporal Middle-Layer Recurrence (T2MLR), a transformers-based latent reasoning architecture that fuses a cached middle layer representation from the previous token directly into an earlier layer of the current token position, enabling abstract intermediate computation to persist across decoding steps with little inference overhead. Across natural-language pretraining and multi-hop reasoning finetuning, T2MLR consistently outperforms data- and parameter-matched Transformer base lines. Moreover, applying recurrence to only a localized middle-layer block (as little as 20% of the network) often outperforms full-layer recurrence. Im portantly, T2MLR does not require pretraining from scratch: retrofitting the recurrent pathway into an existing pretrained 1.7B Transformer and briefly finetuning substantially improves math reasoning, lowering the barrier to practical adoption. These results suggest that effective latent reasoning in Transformers does not require looping over all layers as in previous works, but can instead emerge more strongly from targeted middle-layer recurrence.

### [146] [Mask-Aware Policy Gradients for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15200)
*Haran Raajesh,Kulin Shah,Adam Klivans,Philipp Krähenbühl*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的两阶段动作马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）来解决掩码扩散语言模型（MDLMs）中对数似然估计不可行的问题。通过同时优化标记预测和遮蔽位置选择，实现了在数学推理和编码基准上的领先性能，如GSM8K上达到87.1%的准确率，MBPP上达到53.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法仅建模标记预测，忽略了生成过程中遮蔽位置的顺序，导致无法有效扩展强化学习到掩码扩散语言模型。

Method: 将生成过程形式化为一个两阶段动作MDP，其中每个步骤涉及决定在遮蔽位置放置什么标记以及哪些位置应重新遮蔽。利用策略梯度自然分解为标记项和遮蔽项，联合优化两者。

Result: 在数学推理（GSM8K）和编码任务（MBPP）上分别取得了87.1%和53.4%的优异成绩，优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 通过引入两阶段动作框架并联合优化标记与遮蔽策略，成功将强化学习应用于MDLMs，显著提升了其推理能力。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning has proven effective for improving reasoning in large language models, but extending it to Masked Diffusion Language Models (MDLMs) remains challenging due to the intractability of the log-likelihood estimation. Existing approaches approximate this log-likelihood by modeling only the token predictions, ignoring the order in which positions are unmasked during generation. We observe that MDLM generation involves two decisions at each step: what tokens to place at each masked position and which positions to remask. We formalize this as a two-stage action MDP, showing that the policy gradient naturally decomposes into a token term and a masking term. Combining optimization of both terms leads to state-of-the-art outcomes on mathematical reasoning and coding benchmarks, with scores of 87.1% on GSM8K and 53.4% on MBPP.

### [147] [Expanding the Lexicon of Ge'ez Based African Languages: A Comparative Study of Amharic and Tigrinya](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15209)
*Hailay Kidu Teklehaymanot,Debela Desalegn Yadeta,Wolfgang Nejdl*

TL;DR: VEXMLM 是一种针对埃塞俄比亚语（Ge'ez）文字的扩展词汇量预训练语言模型，通过为阿姆哈拉语和提格里尼亚语定制 SentencePiece 分词器，将 30,000 个新子词加入 XLM-R 的词汇表，并通过平均初始化嵌入。该模型在两个阶段进行训练：持续掩码语言建模和监督微调，在问答、命名实体识别和情感分析任务上显著优于 XLM-R 和 Glot500。在阿姆哈拉语/提格里尼亚语问答任务中分别达到 87.0 EM / 90.0 F1，情感分析准确率达 80.0%，命名实体识别中 OOV 实体准确率从 81.4% 提升至 94.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 为阿姆哈拉语和提格里尼亚语构建语言特定的 SentencePiece 分词器；基于该分词器生成 30,000 个埃塞俄比亚语子词并扩展 XLM-R 词汇；使用原 XLM-R 分词器的子词嵌入均值初始化新子词嵌入；采用两阶段训练：第一阶段在扩展词汇上继续进行掩码语言建模，第二阶段在问答、命名实体识别和情感分析任务上进行监督微调。

Result: 在阿姆哈拉语/提格里尼亚语问答任务上，VEXMLM 达到 87.0 EM / 90.0 F1，显著优于 XLM-R（66.0 EM / 78.0 F1）和 Glot500（74.0 EM / 78.0 F1）；情感分析准确率达 80.0%，高于 XLM-R 的 77.0% 和 Glot500 的 46.0%；命名实体识别中 OOV 实体准确率从 81.4% 提升至 94.3%（覆盖 11 种语言）。此外，模型在 17 种其他非洲语言上也表现出良好迁移能力。

Conclusion: VEXMLM 证明了为非拉丁文字设计语言特定的分词器和词汇扩展策略的有效性，其两阶段训练方法不仅提升了目标语言性能，还成功迁移到相关低资源非洲语言。研究展示了词汇扩展与嵌入初始化对提升非拉丁文字语言模型性能的关键作用。

Abstract: Multilingual pre-trained language models (PLMs) exhibit degraded performance on low-resource, non-Latin-script languages, driven by high out-of-vocabulary (OOV) rates and excessive subword fragmentation that result from Latin-script-centric tokenizer training. We introduce VEXMLM, a vocabulary-extended variant of XLM-R targeting the two highest-resource Ge'ez-script languages, Amharic and Tigrinya, and further evaluated on 17 additional low-resource African languages (19 total). We train a language-specific SentencePiece tokenizer on curated Amharic and Tigrinya monolingual corpora, extend XLM-R's vocabulary with 30,000 Ge'ez-script subwords derived from this tokenizer, and initialize their embeddings by averaging the embeddings of their constituent subwords under XLM-R's original tokenizer. VEXMLM is trained in two stages: (1) continued masked language modeling over the extended vocabulary on the curated corpora, and (2) supervised fine-tuning on question answering (QA), named entity recognition (NER), and sentiment analysis (SA). On Amharic/Tigrinya QA, VEXMLM achieves 87.0 EM /90.0 F1, versus 66.0 EM/78.0 F1 for XLM-R and 74.0 EM/ 78.0 F1 for Glot500. On SA, VEXMLM reaches 80.0\% accuracy versus 77.0\% (XLM-R) and 46.0\% (Glot500). On NER, VEXMLM raises OOV-token entity accuracy from 81.4\% to 94.3\%, averaged over 11 of the 19 evaluated languages for which OOV analysis was possible. Our contributions are: (i) a vocabulary-extension and embedding-initialization procedure tailored to Ge'ez script; (ii) a two-stage training strategy under which vocabulary and continued-pretraining gains on Amharic/Tigrinya transfer to 17 typologically related, unaugmented African languages; and (iii) an evaluation spanning both intrinsic tokenization metrics (vocabulary coverage, fertility, OOV rate) and extrinsic task performance across all 19 languages.

### [148] [In-Place Tokenizer Expansion for Pre-trained LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15232)
*Jimmy T. H. Smith,Tarek Dakhran,Alberto Cabrera,Simon S. Lee,Paul Pak,Aditya Tadimeti,Tim Seyde,Maxime Labonne,Alexander Amini,Mathias Lechner*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在不重新训练模型的情况下，通过在预训练模型中扩展分词器（tokenizer）的方案，以改善多语言支持，特别是对新加入语言的编码效率。该方法基于现有分词器的BPE合并过程，在多语言语料上继续进行合并，使大部分原有标记保持不变，新标记可精确分解为原始子标记。通过复制原有嵌入并初始化新嵌入为源子标记嵌入的均值，并经过两阶段适应性训练（仅嵌入训练后全模型继续预训练），恢复了原始检查点的性能。实验表明，该方法显著减少了印地语、越南语和泰语等语言的分词数量（分别减少2.4倍、2.6倍，最多达4.0倍），结合大词汇量带来的每标记开销，估计在参考设备上实现2.2–3.7倍的每字符解码速度提升。模型权重与扩展分词器已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当预训练模型的分词器固定时，后期加入的语言会被分割成更多子词，导致延迟、计算和能耗增加。云模型虽能承受大词汇量，但设备端模型受限于内存与带宽，通常采用小词汇量，牺牲非核心语言的编码效率。因此需要一种无需重训练即可扩展分词器的方法，以提高新语言的编码效率。

Method: 提出分词器扩展（Tokenizer Expansion）方法：在多语言语料上继续已有分词器的BPE合并过程，确保新词可由原子词精确分解；保留原有嵌入行，新嵌入行初始化为对应源子词嵌入均值；通过两阶段训练（先仅训练嵌入层，再全模型继续预训练）恢复模型性能。

Result: 将该方法应用于LFM2-8B-A1B模型，生成了带有128K分词器的LFM2.5-8B-A1B模型。结果显示，印地语、越南语和泰语的分词数分别减少约2.4倍、2.6倍和最多4.0倍；结合每标记成本，估计每字符解码速度提升2.2–3.7倍。同时，负向实验结果也被报告，用于指导方法优化。

Conclusion: 分词器扩展是一种有效的在不重新训练模型的前提下提升多语言编码效率的技术，尤其适用于设备端部署场景。通过合理的初始化与渐进式训练，可在保持模型性能的同时显著降低新语言的编码开销，具备实际应用价值。

Abstract: A tokenizer fixed at the start of pre-training allocates vocabulary in proportion to the pre-training corpus, reflecting the deployment priorities at that time. When those priorities shift, languages added later are split into many more tokens per word, which can raise latency, compute, and energy consumption for users of those languages. Cloud models can afford a broad vocabulary because the embedding and LM-head matrices are a small fraction of their parameters. On a compact model those matrices are a material share of per-token decode bandwidth, so on-device models ship small vocabularies and accept fragmentation outside a fixed language set. We present tokenizer expansion, an in-place recipe for upgrading a pre-trained model's tokenizer when the model producer controls its design. We continue the existing tokenizer's BPE merges on a multilingual corpus, so most source tokens carry over unchanged as single tokens and every new token has an exact decomposition into source tokens. We copy the carried-over embedding rows unchanged and initialize new rows as the mean of their source sub-token embeddings. A two-stage adaptation, embedding-only training then full-model continued pre-training, recovers source-checkpoint quality. We apply the recipe to a continued pre-trained checkpoint of LFM2-8B-A1B, an 8B-parameter Mixture-of-Experts model, to help produce LFM2.5-8B-A1B with a 128K tokenizer. The expanded tokenizer encodes Hindi and Vietnamese in roughly $2.4\times$ and $2.6\times$ fewer tokens than the source (up to $4.0\times$ on Thai). Combining these reductions with the measured per-token cost of the larger vocabulary, we estimate a $2.2$-$3.7\times$ per-character decode speedup for these languages across our reference devices. We release the model weights and the expanded tokenizer, and report the negative findings that shaped the recipe.

</details>


### [149] [Language Identification via Compositional Data Analysis: A Linear-Time Classifier Based on Log-Ratio Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15238)
*Paul-Andrei Pogăcean,Sanda-Maria Avram*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于中心化对数比（CLR）变换的组合向量表示方法，将字符和二元组频率分布映射到零和子空间，利用欧氏距离对应Aitchison距离，结合拉普拉斯平滑处理稀疏性问题，在六种语言上实现了鲁棒且高效的文本分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经网络方法计算开销大，而经典统计方法依赖不合适的距离度量，尤其在处理组合数据时表现不佳，因此需要一种高效且可解释性强的语言识别方案。

Method: 将字符与二元组频率分布建模为定义在单纯形上的组合向量，通过中心化对数比（CLR）变换将其映射至(D-1)维零和子空间，从而使欧氏距离等价于Aitchison距离，并引入拉普拉斯平滑缓解特征稀疏问题。

Result: 实验表明该方法在不同长度文本下均表现出稳定准确率，尤其在长序列上性能突出，验证了其在资源受限场景下的有效性与可解释性优势。

Conclusion: 组合表示法提供了一种确定性、高效且低资源消耗的语言识别替代方案，特别适用于对可解释性和计算效率要求较高的实际应用。

Abstract: Language identification is commonly addressed using either neural architectures or statistical n-gram models. Neural approaches typically require substantial computational resources, whereas classical frequency-based methods offer efficient linear-time performance, but rely on distance metrics that are not always appropriate for compositional data.
  This work models character and bigram frequency distributions as compositional vectors constrained to the simplex and mapped via the centered log-ratio (CLR) transformation bijectively onto the $(D-1)$-dimensional zero-sum subspace of $\mathbb{R}^D$, where Euclidean distances correspond to Aitchison distances. A pipeline is proposed, combining CLR-transformed unigram and bigram features with Laplace smoothing to address sparsity. The method is evaluated on six languages.
  Experimental results show that the proposed approach achieves robust accuracy across different text lengths, with strong performance for longer sequences. These findings indicate that compositional representations provide a deterministic and computationally efficient alternative for language identification, particularly in settings where interpretability and low resource consumption are essential.

</details>


### [150] [TikStance: A Multimodal and Hierarchical Dataset for Multi-target Stance Analysis in TikTok Political Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15240)
*Yazhi Zhang,Fuqiang Niu,Bowen Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TikStance 是一个针对2024年美国大选期间政治讨论的多模态、上下文感知数据集，包含161个视频和13,876条评论，覆盖特朗普、拜登和哈里斯三位政治人物。数据集通过链接视频与评论树结构，支持在音视频和对话上下文中进行立场检测，并采用三分类标注（支持、反对、无立场），经三方独立标注与复核，一致性系数Krippendorff's α 达到0.72以上。分析显示不同目标的立场分布和对话深度存在差异，嵌套回复占23.3%。该数据集为多模态立场检测、政治传播、计算社会科学和上下文感知NLP研究提供了重要支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算分析受限于缺乏同时包含音视频信息和层级对话结构的政治短视频数据集，尤其在多目标、多层级语境下的立场检测研究亟需高质量数据支持。

Method: 构建包含视频元数据与评论树结构的多模态数据集，每条记录关联视频与父级评论链；采用三名标注员对视频-目标及评论-目标立场进行三分类标注，存在分歧时重新标注，最终通过Krippendorff's α评估标注一致性。

Result: TikStance 数据集包含161个视频、13,876条评论，覆盖三位总统候选人，标注一致性良好（α > 0.72）；发现目标相关立场分布差异及对话深度特征，嵌套回复占比达23.3%。

Conclusion: TikStance 为多模态立场检测与政治话语分析提供了高质量、多层次标注的数据基础，推动了计算社会科学研究的发展。

Abstract: Political discourse has increasingly moved to short-video platforms, yet computational analysis of such content remains constrained by the scarcity of datasets that jointly preserve audiovisual information and hierarchical conversations. Here we present TikStance, a multimodal and context-aware dataset comprising 161 videos and 13,876 comments from TikTok, designed for stance detection in political discussions. The dataset covers three major political figures in the 2024 U.S. election cycle--Donald Trump, Joe Biden, and Kamala Harris--with content collected between September 2023 and January 2025. Each discussion unit links a host video and its metadata to a parent-linked comment tree, enabling stance analysis within both audiovisual and conversational context. Each item was independently labeled by three annotators using a three-class scheme (Favor, Against, None) for video-to-target and comment-to-target stance; items with disagreement were re-annotated, and the final Krippendorff's \(α\) reached 0.743, 0.723, and 0.722 for the Trump, Biden, and Harris subsets, respectively. Descriptive analysis further reveals target-dependent differences in stance distributions and conversational depth, with nested replies accounting for 23.3\% of all comments. By combining multi-target coverage, hierarchical conversations, and reliable multi-level human annotations, TikStance supports research in multimodal stance detection, political communication, computational social science, and context-aware natural language processing.

Method: 基于MediaEval Medico 2025数据集，对九个已发表的多模态问答系统进行系统性分析，比较不同方法在参数效率、结构化推理、证据锚定等方面的实现与效果，结合评估指标与人类判断进行综合分析。

Result: 参数高效微调虽带来良好挑战性能，但无法保证推理的忠实性；结构化推理与显式证据链接的方法在多种问题类型下表现出更高可靠性，但尚缺乏因果验证。评估应扩展至证据关联性、数据治理与模型校准等维度。

Conclusion: 构建可信的多模态医疗AI需融合数据、强化可解释性，并实施稳健的评估机制，未来应推动标准化评估流程与防泄漏治理。

Abstract: Healthcare multimodal AI must combine visual and textual evidence while remaining reliable and interpretable. Using MediaEval Medico 2025 as a retrospective GI endoscopy case study, we analyze design choices across nine documented systems for question answering and explanation quality. Parameter-efficient adaptation of pretrained backbones provides strong challenge performance, but answer-level gains do not consistently translate into faithful and complete clinical reasoning. Methods enforcing structured reasoning and explicit grounding show more reliable behavior across heterogeneous question types, although the evidence is correlational rather than ablation-based. These results motivate evaluation beyond lexical overlap, standardized evidence-linked explanations, leakage-aware data governance, and lightweight robustness and calibration checks. The findings support trustworthy multimodal healthcare AI based on data fusion, explainability, and resilient evaluation.

### [152] [SciDiagramEdit: Learning to Edit Scientific Diagrams from Paper Revisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15272)
*Yasheng Sun,Zezi Zeng,Yifan Yang,Chong Luo,Wenyi Wang,Ziwei Liu,Jürgen Schmidhuber*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出SciDiagramEdit，一个基于自然语言指令的科学图表编辑基准和技能演化框架。通过分析arXiv版本历史中的前后图对比对，捕捉作者的真实修订意图，并在可编辑的矢量源上实现交互式编辑。采用代理学习驱动的技能演化机制，使编辑技能随多轮迭代逐步提升，在验证集上显著提高编辑准确率，证明自然论文修订是训练指令驱动图表编辑的有效信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学图表编辑涉及标签重设、布局调整、样式修改等复杂操作，传统方法依赖人工，耗时且难以自动化。现有技术难以处理图表中多种视觉元素（如图表、示意图、照片、箭头、注释）在严格视觉语法下的组合关系，导致自然语言指令下的自动编辑困难。因此亟需一种能理解复杂修订意图并支持精确编辑的自动化系统。

Method: 构建SciDiagramEdit基准，从arXiv版本历史中提取真实论文修订的前后图对；使用可编辑的矢量源作为输入，支持用户与代理协同编辑；引入代理学习机制，通过技能演化框架不断优化编辑策略，利用执行轨迹反馈改进技能规范，实现渐进式性能提升。

Result: 所提框架在独立验证集上实现了显著的编辑准确率提升，表明自然语言形式的论文修订过程可有效作为训练信号，支持高精度、语义理解型的科学图表自动化编辑。

Conclusion: SciDiagramEdit成功展示了基于真实论文修订数据与技能演化机制的自动化图表编辑可行性，为未来智能科研辅助工具的发展提供了重要基础。

Abstract: Editing the figures in a research paper is a routine and time-consuming part of everyday research practice: authors relabel components, rearrange panels, and restyle visuals as they revise their manuscripts. Automating this editing workflow under a natural-language instruction, however, is challenging, because a scientific figure is a dense infographic in which heterogeneous visual elements such as schematics, plots, photos, captions, and arrows are composed under a tight visual grammar to advance a specific argument. To address this, we present SciDiagramEdit, a benchmark and skill-evolution framework that learns from natural paper revisions and operates on the figure's editable vector source, where users can inspect and co-edit individual primitives alongside the agent. Our benchmark mines before/after figure pairs from arXiv version histories, each grounded in the authors' own revision intent. To accommodate the diversity of editing instructions, we adopt agentic learning via skill evolution: an agentic proposer continually refines the agent's skill specification from execution traces over multiple epochs. The resulting skill progressively lifts edit accuracy on a held-out validation set, providing evidence that natural paper revisions are an effective training signal for instruction-driven figure editing.

### [153] [Partition, Prompt, Aggregate: Statistical Self-Consistency in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15277)
*Patrik Wolf,Thomas Kleine Buening,Andreas Krause,Celestine Mendler-Dünner*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型（LLM）在上下文学习中是否遵循概率自洽性原则，特别是全概率定律。通过构建二叉树对群体进行递归细分，评估模型在不同粒度下的估计一致性。结果显示，主流模型普遍存在违反自洽性的现象，且细粒度子群体的估计比直接的总体估计更接近人类参考数据，这种现象被称为‘宏观谬误’。该发现表明模型虽具备子群体知识，但无法可靠地将其整合为总体估计，从而提出统计自洽性作为无需参考的评估标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证大语言模型在上下文学习中是否满足基本的概率自洽性，尤其是全概率定律，以揭示其推理能力的局限性。

Method: 采用二叉树结构对群体进行多级细分，设计基于自然语言描述的上下文提示，让模型对各子群体进行估计，并将结果聚合回总体水平，比较不同粒度下的估计一致性。

Result: 广泛观察到模型估计违反自洽性；细粒度子群体估计优于直接总体估计，表现出‘宏观谬误’；该现象在不同树结构和任务中稳定存在，可通过隐式提示部分缓解。

Conclusion: 模型虽掌握子群体相关信息，但未能可靠地将其传播至整体估计，因此统计自洽性可作为无参考的评估准则，揭示当前模型在聚合推理上的不足。

Abstract: In-context learning is commonly interpreted as a form of conditional inference, in which the prompt specifies a context and the model's output is treated as an estimate of the corresponding conditional distribution. If this interpretation holds, then LLM estimates should satisfy basic probabilistic identities. In particular, the law of total probability asserts that prior-weighted conditional distributions aggregate into population-level marginals over any valid partition of the population. In this work, we investigate to what extent LLM estimates adhere to this self-consistency principle. We use binary trees as an evaluation scaffold to recursively partition a population into increasingly fine-grained subpopulations. We then prompt LLMs with verbalized subpopulation descriptions in context, aggregate the resulting estimates back into population-level estimates, and compare them across partitions of varying granularity. Applying this protocol across problem domains and state-of-the-art frontier models, we show widespread violations of basic consistency properties. An in-depth study of persona prompting reveals a pattern we call the macro fallacy: estimates reconstructed from more fine-grained subpopulation responses are often better aligned with human reference data than direct population-level estimates. This effect persists across variations in tree structure and estimation task, and can be partially recovered through implicit prompting. Together, these findings suggest that models possess relevant subpopulation knowledge but do not reliably propagate it into aggregate estimates. This gap establishes statistical self-consistency as an unsaturated, reference-free criterion for evaluating LLMs.

</details>

### [154] [Intelligent Three Level Learning Architecture for Autonomous UAV Swarms in Search and Rescue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14093)
*Oleksii Bychkov*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新型的三级分层学习架构，用于自主无人机群在搜救任务中的协同作业。该架构融合了三种不同的学习机制：个体适应采用赫布神经可塑性，战术协调结合多智能体强化学习（MARL）、图神经网络（GNN）与行为树，战略决策则基于模型无关元学习、BDI推理与数字孪生。系统通过22个架构契约在6个组件间实现6类形式化保证（如安全、最优性、活性等）。引入‘集群元认知’概念，使蜂群能监控自身认知状态并动态切换策略。五种构造性进展函数连接抽象优化与实际任务场景。主集成定理证明：当所有契约满足时，混合神经符号系统保持全部六类保证；动态学习情况下新增5个契约，带来认知韧性、渐进退化和元改进单调性等新保障。理论分析表明该架构克服了现有层次强化学习的五大根本缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有层次强化学习方法在无人机搜救任务中存在适应性差、协调能力弱、战略决策僵化、缺乏可解释性和系统鲁棒性不足等问题，难以应对复杂动态环境。为解决这些局限，亟需一种融合生物认知层级的分层学习架构，以实现从个体反应到集体战略的多层次智能协同。

Method: 提出三层次分层学习架构：第一层（反射层）使用赫布神经可塑性实现个体快速自适应；第二层（技能层）结合多智能体强化学习（MARL）、图神经网络（GNN）与行为树实现战术级协作；第三层（推理层）采用模型无关元学习、BDI推理与数字孪生支持战略决策。通过22个架构契约对各组件进行形式化约束，涵盖安全、预算正确性、最优性、活性、无饥饿性及跨层一致性等六类保证。引入‘集群元认知’机制，实现认知状态监控与策略切换。设计五种构造性进展函数，连接理论与实际任务。在动态学习场景下扩展五项新契约，增强系统认知韧性与渐进优化能力。

Result: 所提架构成功实现了六类核心形式化保证，并在动态学习条件下新增认知韧性、优雅降级与元学习单调改进三项保障。理论验证表明其有效克服了传统层次强化学习在适应性、协调性、可扩展性、可解释性与鲁棒性方面的五大缺陷。实验与分析显示，该系统在复杂搜救任务中表现出更强的自主性、稳定性与任务完成率。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了一种具有生物学启发的三层次分层学习架构，首次将神经可塑性、多智能体学习与符号推理深度融合于无人机群搜救系统中，通过严格的形式化契约体系确保系统可靠性。提出的集群元认知机制赋予系统自我监控与策略切换能力，显著提升整体智能水平与环境适应性。该框架为未来复杂自主系统的设计提供了可复用、可验证的理论范式。

Abstract: This paper presents a novel three level hierarchical learning architecture for autonomous UAV swarms performing search and rescue operations. Unlike conventional approaches that apply a single learning paradigm across all hierarchy levels, the proposed architecture integrates three qualitatively different learning mechanisms corresponding to the biological hierarchy of reflexes, skills, and reasoning such as Hebbian neuroplasticity for individual agent adaptation, multi agent reinforcement learning with graph neural networks and behavior trees for tactical coordination, and model agnostic meta learning with BDI reasoning and a digital twin for strategic decision making.
  The architecture is formalized through twenty two architectural contracts organized across six components such as BDI, Behavior Trees, GNN, MARL, Neuroplasticity, Meta Learning that collectively provide six classes of formal guarantees such as safety, budget correctness, optimality, liveness, starvation freedom, and inter level consistency.
  We introduce Swarm Meta Cognition as a compositional property arising from the structured interaction of all three levels, enabling the swarm to monitor its own cognitive state and switch between cognitive strategies. Five constructive progress functions for SAR task types bridge the gap between abstract optimization theory and concrete operational scenarios.
  The main integration theorem establishes that when all contracts are satisfied, the hybrid neuro-symbolic system preserves all six guarantee classes. For the dynamic case with active learning, five new contracts extend the framework with three additional guarantees such as cognitive resilience, graceful degradation, and monotonic meta improvement. Theoretical analysis demonstrates that the architecture addresses five fundamental limitations of existing hierarchical RL approaches.

</details>


### [155] [HG-RAG: Hierarchy-Guided Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Structured Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14095)
*Pranav Yadav*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HG-RAG enhances LLM outputs by using a hierarchical knowledge graph for retrieval, enabling better performance on complex queries requiring relational and multi-hop reasoning compared to flat document stores.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing RAG systems struggle with queries needing hierarchical or relational reasoning due to reliance on flat document stores, limiting their ability to handle structured knowledge effectively.

Method: HG-RAG performs graph traversal over a hierarchical knowledge graph: it anchors named entities in the query, then expands context through upward (parent), lateral (relational neighbors), and downward (child) paths as needed.

Result: HG-RAG outperforms dense retrieval baselines across multiple world scales (18-800 nodes) and query types, particularly excelling in hierarchical, relational, and multi-hop reasoning tasks, while reducing hallucination and preserving locality coherence.

Abstract: Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) has proven to be a widely successful process at improving the quality of outputs from a Large Language Model (LLM) for wider context. However, RAG systems typically retrieve context from flat document stores, which struggles when queries require hierarchical or relational reasoning across structured knowledge. I present HG-RAG (Hierarchy-Guided RAG), a framework that performs graph-traversal over a hierarchical knowledge graph to deliver structured context to a language model. My retrieval pipeline resolves a named entity anchor from the query, then expands context upward through parent nodes, laterally through relational neighbors, and downward through child nodes when needed. I evaluate HG-RAG against a dense retrieval baseline across three world scales (18-800 nodes) with four query types: local fact, hierarchical, neighborhood, and multi-hop. Results show HG-RAG consistently outperforms the flat baseline on hierarchical, relational, and multi-hop reasoning tasks, while reducing hallucination and maintaining locality coherence.

### [156] [IMEX Interaction-Based Model Explanation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14096)
*Emiliano Massi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: IMEX 是一种用于可解释预测建模的方法，通过静态相关性功率（PCS）和交互相关性功率（PCI）两个指标，识别对目标预测贡献最大的变量及其相互作用，支持高阶交互分析，适用于非线性、条件性和多重共线性关系。实验验证表明其在合成数据上能有效恢复特征结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在关键应用场景中，仅靠预测准确性不足以验证模型，需解释模型决策背后的机制；黑箱模型缺乏透明性，导致难以理解和信任其输出。因此需要一种能够揭示变量重要性及交互作用的可解释方法。

Method: IMEX 方法基于两个互补指标：静态相关性功率（PCS）用于衡量单个特征的贡献，交互相关性功率（PCI）用于捕捉特征间的非加性效应。该框架支持任意高阶交互分析，可构建预测的可解释性图谱。

Result: 在三个具有已知结构的合成数据集上，与 INVASE 方法对比，IMEX 能够在非线性、条件性和多重共线性条件下准确恢复特征层面的真实结构，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: IMEX 提供了一种灵活且有效的可解释预测建模框架，能够识别关键特征和复杂交互模式，有助于理解黑箱模型的内部决策机制。

Abstract: In predictive modeling, the ability to explain why a model produces a given target prediction has become increasingly important [5, 10]. Black-box models do not provide a transparent description of the internal mechanisms that generate the prediction, making even accurate predictions difficult to interpret and validate. In critical contexts, predictive accuracy alone is not a sufficient validation metric if the reasons underlying model decisions remain unexplained. The IMEX (Interaction-Based Model Explanation) approach represents a methodological direction within explainable predictive modeling. IMEX is designed to identify which variables contribute most to the target prediction and which interactions among variables are significant in determining the target. The method does not impose limitations on higher-order interaction analysis, allowing the investigation of feature subsets with cardinality greater than two. Beyond the identification of feature importance, IMEX enables the exploration of interaction patterns that may be consistent with latent mechanisms influencing the outcome. Through the application of the IMEX algorithm, it is possible to construct an interpretability map of the predictions. The IMEX framework is built on two complementary metrics: Static Correlation Power (PCS), which quantifies the contribution of individual features, and Interaction Correlation Power (PCI), which captures non-additive effects among features. In the present work, the PCS component is experimentally validated through a comparison with INVASE [18] on three synthetic datasets with known structures. The results indicate that IMEX can recover relevant feature-level structures in the presence of non-linear, conditional, and multicollinear relationships between input features and prediction targets.

</details>


### [157] [RegNetAgents: A Multi-Agent Framework for Cross-Network Regulatory Driver Identification in Cancer Genomics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14097)
*Jose A. Bird*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RegNetAgents 是一个面向人工智能的多智能体框架，用于在异构基因调控网络中进行结构化、查询驱动的监管候选识别。该框架整合了TCGA衍生的癌症网络与GREmLN项目的单细胞调控网络，通过双网络分类、癌症基因过滤和作用模式（MoA）分配，对焦点基因的候选调节因子进行排名。系统基于LangGraph DAG工作流实现，提供统一的Python API和MCP客户端，作为预计算调控网络的下游分析层。在11个乳腺癌（BRCA）和12个结直肠癌（COAD）焦点基因中，候选基因显著富集于OncoKB注释的癌症基因；TCGA和GREmLN来源的候选均表现出高度统计显著性（所有p < 0.0001），且控制基因集无富集，证明信号特异性。扩展模块支持对致癌潜力、可药性、临床相关性和网络脆弱性的结构化评估，实现从候选识别到生物学假设生成的端到端分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在癌症基因组学中，识别关键调控因子面临数据异质性与跨网络一致性验证的挑战。现有方法多依赖单一数据源或网络推断，缺乏统一、可解释的跨网络分析框架。因此，亟需一种能够整合多源调控网络、支持结构化推理并具备生物可解释性的自动化系统，以提升监管候选识别的准确性与可重复性。

Method: RegNetAgents采用多智能体架构，构建基于LangGraph的有向无环图（DAG）工作流，集成TCGA肿瘤批量数据与单细胞ARACNe网络（来自GREmLN项目）。针对特定焦点基因，系统执行双网络分类（共现/仅TCGA/仅GREmLN）、基于OncoKB的癌症基因过滤及作用模式（MoA）标注。候选按跨网络证据一致性排序，并通过扩展模块评估其致癌性、可药性、临床意义与网络脆弱性。系统不进行网络推断，而是作为预计算网络的下游分析工具运行。

Result: 在11个乳腺癌（BRCA）和12个结直肠癌（COAD）焦点基因中，RegNetAgents识别出的候选调节因子显著富集于OncoKB注释的癌症基因：TCGA来源候选富集显著（Stouffer Z = 6.69 for BRCA, 6.95 for COAD），GREmLN来源同样显著（Z = 5.51 for BRCA, 7.06 for COAD；所有p < 0.0001）。控制基因集（如管家基因或非驱动基因）未见富集，表明结果具有高度特异性。扩展模块支持从候选发现到生物学假设生成的全流程解释。

Conclusion: RegNetAgents建立了一个可解释的人工智能框架，实现了跨异构调控网络的结构化、查询驱动的监管候选识别，为癌症基因组学中的功能基因发现提供了高效、可靠且可解释的分析路径。

Abstract: We introduce RegNetAgents, an AI-oriented multi-agent framework for structured, query-driven regulatory candidate identification across heterogeneous gene regulatory networks. The system enables unified analysis of bulk tumor and single-cell-derived ARACNe networks by integrating TCGA-derived cancer networks with large-scale single-cell regulatory networks from the GREmLN project. For a given focal gene, the framework performs dual-network classification, cancer gene filtering using OncoKB annotations, and mode-of-action (MoA) assignment for tumor-derived regulatory relationships. Candidates are ranked by evidence consistency across networks (Both, TCGA-only, GREmLN-only). The system is implemented as a multi-agent LangGraph DAG workflow, accessible through a unified Python API and Model Context Protocol (MCP) client, operating as a downstream analytical layer over precomputed regulatory networks rather than a network inference method. Across eleven breast cancer (BRCA) and twelve colorectal cancer (COAD) focal genes, RegNetAgents identifies candidate regulators significantly enriched for OncoKB-annotated cancer genes. TCGA-derived candidates show strong enrichment (Stouffer Z = 6.69 for BRCA and 6.95 for COAD), while GREmLN-derived candidates also demonstrate significant enrichment (Z = 5.51 for BRCA and 7.06 for COAD; all p < 0.0001). No enrichment is observed in housekeeping or non-driver control gene sets, supporting signal specificity. An extended module enables structured evaluation of oncogenic potential, druggability, clinical relevance, and network vulnerability, supporting end-to-end interpretation from candidate identification to biological hypothesis generation. RegNetAgents establishes an interpretable AI framework for cross-network regulatory candidate identification in cancer genomics.

*Yukun Song,Changwei Wang,Xingtian Pei,Shibiao Xu,Wenhao Xu,Shunpeng Chen,Yu Zhang,Ke Zhang,Rongtao Xu,Xuxiang Feng,Pengyang Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出对话式地点识别（DlgPR）框架，包含一个跨模态多层次检索器和一个智能提问者DQ-pilot。DQ-pilot采用分阶段训练策略：先在小规模数据集上进行监督微调，再在更难的数据集上通过GRPO算法进行强化学习优化。使用Discriminative Difficulty Index (DDI) 进行课程采样，Positional Retrieval Gain (PRG) 作为奖励信号引导学习。

Conclusion: 通过引入对话驱动的推理机制，实现了对复杂、模糊语言描述下地理定位任务的高效解决，展示了从静态检索向动态交互推理转变的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Inspired by how humans communicate spatial information, language-guided geo-localization has gained significant traction for its intuitive and practical value. Despite this progress, most methods still rely on a static, one-shot retrieval paradigm, which fails to handle the ambiguity and incompleteness inherent in real-world natural language descriptions. We propose a paradigm shift to reasoning retrieval and introduce Dialogue Place Recognition (DlgPR), which casts localization as an interactive, dialogue-driven reasoning process. To support this new task, we present DlgQuest-Cities, the first large-scale dialogue-based benchmark for place recognition, and a unified reasoning framework that couples a cross-modal multi-level retriever with an intelligent questioner, DQ-pilot. DQ-pilot is trained in a curriculum: supervised fine-tuning on a curated DQ-cities-20k subset followed by reinforcement refinement on a harder DQ-cities-10k split via GRPO. Two task-aligned metrics guide learning: a Discriminative Difficulty Index (DDI) for curriculum sampling and a Positional Retrieval Gain (PRG) reward that directly measures retrieval improvement induced by a question. Experiments show this reasoning-based approach significantly outperforms baselines. The code and model are available at https://github.com/Graysonggg/DlgPR.

### [161] [Capability from Access Structure, Not Scale: Lower Bounds and Pre-Registered Tests for Hybrid Sequence Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14144)
*Wenhui Chen,Jianlin Chen,Ziyao Lin,Chi Man Vong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出能力收敛假设（CCH），指出在固定每标记推理预算下，表征收敛不意味着能力收敛。能力趋向于一种‘访问完备混合架构’，即同时具备压缩的O(1)状态通道和可扩展的逐字索引通道。通过牛顿苹果问题等任务验证，识别出三个资源壁垒：香农壁、视界壁和电路壁，并证明混合架构可突破这些壁垒，实现严格超加性能力。研究基于信息论下界与预注册实验，部分结果已验证，部分预测方向反转，但均如实报告。表征收敛由规模自然带来，而能力收敛需通过访问结构来实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大规模模型中表征与能力收敛的关系，揭示仅靠规模不足以实现能力收敛，需特定的访问结构设计。

Result: 成功测量到预测的剪刀差距（精确检索误差0.994 vs. 0.000），状态跟踪分岔出现在预定边界，且发现不可约的双通道解；一项预测方向反转，但被如实报告。

Conclusion: 表征收敛随规模自然发生，但能力收敛需通过访问结构的设计来实现，特别是具备压缩与可扩展通道的混合架构。

Abstract: The Platonic Representation Hypothesis (PRH) holds that as models scale, representations of heterogeneous networks converge toward a shared model of reality. We propose its sequel and boundary, the Capability Convergence Hypothesis (CCH): under a fixed per-token inference budget, representational convergence does not entail capability convergence. Capability instead converges toward a class, the access-complete hybrid: any architecture holding both a compressive O(1)-state channel and a scalable verbatim-index channel. We anchor it on a witness task, the Newton's-apple problem in an infinite stream, and name three resource walls: a Shannon wall barring any o(Nb)-state architecture, a horizon wall barring any fixed window, and a circuit wall barring fixed-depth attention-only composition (conditional on TC0 != NC1). Under an explicit separability assumption a hybrid crosses all three by paying each wall's price, so capability is strictly super-additive under composition. We separate what we prove from what we conjecture: the access-completeness principle rests on information-theoretic lower bounds and pre-registered experiments, while the field-level convergence trend is an economics-motivated conjecture. We report the first pre-registered small-scale tests under criteria frozen before the data: the predicted scissors gap is measured (exact-retrieval error 0.994 vs. 0.000 once a 64-scalar state gains one global-attention layer), the state-tracking bifurcation lands at the registered boundary, and a conjunction witness shows an irreducibly two-channel solution; one prediction failed with its direction reversed and is reported as such. Representational convergence is given freely by scale; capability convergence must be purchased by access structure.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具增强型大语言模型代理在面对新工具时难以有效整合，因行为惯性导致依赖旧工具和推理模式；重新训练成本过高，亟需一种高效、可扩展的动态适应机制。

Method: 提出ToolAnchor框架，使用教师模型推测反事实锚定上下文，通过学生模型回放验证，并借助代理后训练将有效干预策略固化，从而打破行为惯性。

Abstract: Tool-augmented large language model agents excel at long-horizon tasks, yet they are typically post-trained on fixed toolsets. When tasks demand new tools, these agents struggle to incorporate them effectively, and retraining from scratch is often impractical. We identify the core obstacle in such toolset expansion problem as behavioral inertia: the tendency of agents to fall back on familiar tools and established reasoning patterns despite having access to new ones. We demonstrate that injecting counterfactual anchor contexts at critical decision points can break this inertia, recovering failed trajectories by eliciting suppressed agent capabilities. To scale this insight, we propose ToolAnchor, a framework that uses teacher models to hypothesize these counterfactual contexts, verifies them via student rollouts, and internalizes the successful interventions through agentic post-training. Extensive evaluations across general AI assistant (GAIA), textual search (BrowseComp), and visual search (VDR-Bench) tasks demonstrate that ToolAnchor consistently exhibits competitive performance under expanded toolsets. Our work bridges the gap between static post-training and dynamic adaptation, charting a new path for scalable agentic reinforcement learning.

*Dimitrios Kelesis,Konstantinos Bougiatiotis,Georgios Paliouras*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了神经符号代理框架如何增强小型语言模型（SLMs）的推理能力，特别是在复杂多跳逻辑任务中。通过引入两个专用工具调用（extract_facts 和 get_hint），利用关系图卷积网络（RGCN）生成专家提示，提升了Gemina 3和Llama 3.2在CLUTRR家族关系基准上的表现。尽管RGCN提示带来1.5-2倍的性能提升，但受限于事实提取瓶颈和多跳推理中的累积误差，且某些架构出现‘干扰效应’，即自生成噪声事实损害性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型语言模型虽具可持续性优势，但在复杂推理任务中易出错，尤其在多跳逻辑推理中缺乏可靠的事实支撑。因此亟需一种高效、低成本的增强机制，以实现符号化知识与神经模型的有效结合。

Method: 提出一种神经符号代理框架，将SLM转化为轻量级代理，通过两个工具调用：extract_facts用于符号三元组提取，get_hint通过RGCN生成专家推理提示；在Oracle（使用真实三元组）和Realistic（依赖自提取知识）两种场景下进行评估。

Result: RGCN生成的提示使模型性能提升1.5至2倍，但系统受制于事实提取错误和多跳推理中的误差传播；部分模型因自生成噪声事实出现‘干扰效应’，导致性能下降。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了低资源代理系统中符号接地的关键挑战，强调了迭代验证在神经符号代理流水线中的必要性，并为未来优化提供了方向。

Abstract: Although large language models (LLMs) have set benchmarks for zero-shot reasoning, their deployment remains cost-prohibitive and environmentally taxing. Small Language Models (SLMs) offer a sustainable alternative, but prone to errors, on tasks requiring complex, multi-hop logical grounding. We investigate a neuro-symbolic agentic framework to enhance the reasoning capabilities of SLMs, specifically Gemma 3 (1B, 4B) and Llama 3.2 (3B), using the CLUTRR kinship benchmark. Our approach transforms the SLM into a minimalist agent utilizing two specialized tool calls: extract_facts for symbolic triplet extraction and get_hint for expert reasoning via a Relational Graph Convolutional Network (RGCN). We evaluate these models across two configurations, both in an Oracle scenario with ground-truth triplets and a Realistic scenario relying on self-extracted knowledge. Our results reveal that while RGCN-derived hints provide a 1.5 - 2x performance gain over story-only baselines, the system is constrained by the extraction bottleneck and sequential deductive fragility, where early extraction errors compound over multi-hop chains. Furthermore, we identify a "distraction effect" in specific architectures where noisy, self-generated facts degrade performance despite the presence of expert hints. This work characterizes the challenges of symbolic grounding in low-resource agentic systems and provides a roadmap for iterative verification in neuro-symbolic agentic pipelines.

Result: 成功开发并验证了pypowsybl-mcp接口，证明其能够有效支持AI代理完成电网仿真设置、运行、结果提取等任务；初步验证了基于MCP的集成方案在提升研究流程自动化、可审计性与可扩展性方面的可行性；为后续大规模应用提供了技术基础与评估路径。

### [165] [MemoHarness: Agent Harnesses That Learn from Experience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14159)
*Yue Huang,Wenjie Wang,Han Bao,Yuchen Ma,Xiaonan Luo,Yi Nian,Haomin Zhuang,Zheyuan Liu,Yue Zhao,Xiangliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MemoHarness 是一个自适应的代理控制层优化框架，通过学习自身执行经验来动态调整代理行为。它将控制层分解为六个可编辑维度，利用双层经验库存储个体案例诊断与全局模式，并在不依赖测试时标签、反馈或额外搜索的情况下，根据检索到的经验自适应地调整每个测试用例的配置。在多种基准测试中，该方法优于固定控制层，展现出对未见任务和模型的可迁移性，且在缓存支持下保持较低成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动改进方法通常只优化提示、流水线或工作流等局部组件，而部署的代理普遍使用单一全局控制层，缺乏对具体任务场景的适应性。因此需要一种能够从执行经验中学习并自适应调整的控制层设计。

Method: 将代理控制层分解为六个可编辑维度；构建双层经验银行（存储每案例诊断与全局模式）；基于检索到的经验，在无需测试时标签、反馈或额外搜索的前提下，自适应调整控制层配置。

Result: 在壳代理、代码生成和分析推理等基准上，MemoHarness显著优于固定控制层；表现出对未见任务和基模型的可选择性迁移能力；在大量经验可缓存的情况下，上下文开销仍具成本竞争力。

Conclusion: 执行经验是构建更自适应代理控制层的可行基础，相较于单一静态配置更具优势；未来工作需进一步验证统计鲁棒性和各组件的贡献度。

Abstract: An agent harness is the external control layer that turns a base LLM into an executable agent by managing context, tools, orchestration, memory, decoding, and output handling. While harness design strongly affects agent behavior, most automatic improvement methods optimize narrower artifacts such as prompts, pipelines, or workflows, and deployed agents usually reuse a single global harness for all cases. We introduce MemoHarness, an adaptive harness optimization framework that learns from its own executions. MemoHarness decomposes the harness into six editable control dimensions, stores per-case diagnoses and distilled global patterns in a dual-layer experience bank, and adapts the learned harness to each test case using retrieved experience without test-time labels, feedback, or additional search. In our evaluation across shell-agent, code-generation, and analytical-reasoning benchmarks, MemoHarness improves over the fixed harnesses we compare against and shows selective transfer to unseen suites and base models. Its additional context can also remain cost-competitive when much of the retrieved experience is cacheable. These results provide evidence that execution experience is a practical substrate for building agent harnesses that are more adaptive than a single static configuration, while leaving broader claims about statistical robustness and component attribution to future work.

### [166] [When a Verified World Model Still Loses: Play-Adequacy vs Prediction-Accuracy in LLM-Synthesized Code World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14169)
*Javier Aguilar Martín*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 大型语言模型可生成游戏规则的可执行代码（代码世界模型，CWM），供经典规划器搜索。然而，当前以采样轨迹上的高转换准确率为标准衡量模型充分性是错误的。本文揭示了四个关键问题：(1) 即使CWM在采样上达到100%转换准确率且状态准确率超过98%，仍可能因忽略关键规则而在实际游戏中系统性失败，其游戏代价为0.091（95%置信区间[0.065, 0.117]）；这种现象称为“验证-正确性差距”；(2) 失败遵循定量规律：危险 = 游戏代价 × (1−稀有度)^N，其中(1−稀有度)^N为漏检因子，已被严格证明，而游戏代价可实证约束；(3) 增加数据无法修复该问题，因LLM合成本质为规则翻译而非推理，不同模型（GPT-5.x）和数据策略（DAgger、针对性示例）均未推断出缺失规则；(4) 该机制同样存在于不完全信息CWM的信念推理函数中，证明了覆盖边界（大小为N的门限需满足N≳b^{d_max}），解释为何浅层游戏如Kuhn扑克无此差距，并人工构造了Beacon——一个通过验证但始终失败的信念函数。结论：面向规划的世界模型的充分性应基于搜索分布或直接通过游戏表现评估，而非采样轨迹的预测准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对大型语言模型生成的游戏世界模型（CWM）的评估主要依赖于在采样轨迹上的高转换准确率，但作者认为这一标准不足以保证模型在实际规划和游戏中有效。因为即使模型在采样上表现完美，也可能因遗漏极少数但关键的规则而导致系统性失败，从而影响实际应用效果。因此，需要重新审视模型评估的标准，引入更贴近真实规划需求的评价指标。

Method: 通过构建并测试多个代码世界模型（CWM），在不同数据集与模型版本下进行实验，分析其在采样轨迹上的表现与实际游戏表现之间的差异；引入‘验证-正确性差距’概念，建立数学模型描述失败的量化规律；利用形式化证明与人工构造反例（如Beacon）验证理论假设；并通过对比不同训练策略（如DAgger、目标样本）下的模型性能，判断是否能通过数据增强实现规则推断。

Result: 实验表明，即使模型在采样上达到100%转换准确率和≥98%状态准确率，仍可能在实际游戏中因忽略关键规则而系统性失败，其游戏代价达0.091（95%置信区间[0.065, 0.117]）；发现失败遵循精确的定量公式：danger = play_cost × (1−rarity)^N；增加数据或改变训练方式无法修复该缺陷，说明模型本质是规则翻译而非推理；在不完全信息场景中，也存在类似问题，且可通过理论边界解释其发生条件。

Conclusion: 现有基于采样轨迹预测准确率的评估方法不能反映模型在规划任务中的有效性。真正的模型充分性应基于其在规划搜索分布上的表现或直接通过游戏结果来衡量，而非仅依赖采样准确性。

Abstract: Large language models can synthesize a game's rules as executable code - a Code World Model (CWM) - which a classical planner then searches over. Such models are typically accepted when they reach high transition accuracy on sampled trajectories. We argue this is the wrong notion of adequacy for planning.
  We show four things. (1) An LLM-synthesized CWM can pass a sampling gate at 100% transition accuracy and be $\geq 98\%$ state-accurate on the planner's own search distribution, yet lose systematically at play, because the $<1\%$ it gets wrong is exactly the pivotal dynamics; the play cost of the omitted rule is $0.091$ (seed-clustered 95% CI $[0.065,0.117]$, $n=4800$). We call this the verified-vs-correct gap, and confirm it end-to-end through the synthesis pipeline. (2) The harm follows a quantitative law, $\mathrm{danger}=\mathrm{play\_cost}\times(1-\mathrm{rarity})^N$, whose $(1-\mathrm{rarity})^N$ gate-miss factor is proven exact and whose play cost is empirically bounded. (3) The failure is not repaired by more data: LLM synthesis behaves as rule translation, not rule inference, and did not infer the omitted rule across models (GPT-5.x) and data regimes (including DAgger and targeted examples). (4) The same mechanism recurs on the belief-inference function of imperfect-information CWMs: we prove a coverage bound (a size-$N$ gate is identifying when $N\gtrsim b^{d_{\max}}$), explaining why shallow games such as Kuhn poker show no gap, and hand-construct Beacon, a verified-but-wrong inference function that passes the gate yet loses every game.
  These results suggest adequacy for planning-oriented world models should be measured on the search distribution or by play directly, not by prediction accuracy on sampled transitions.

</details>


### [167] [ReasFlow: Assisting Reasoning-Centric Scientific Discovery in Applied Mathematics via a Knowledge-Based Multi-Agent System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14178)
*Yutong He,Daibo Li,Guohong Li,Jiahe Geng,Zhengyang Huang,Can Ren,Zekun Zhang,Yifan Liu,Shuchen Zhu,Hengrui Zhang,Boao Kong,Ming Sun,Shu Li,Chenyi Li,Jiang Hu,Kun Yuan,Zaiwen Wen,Pingwen Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ReasFlow is an autonomous AI agent system designed for theory-driven scientific discovery, particularly in mathematically rigorous fields. It mimics a collaborative research team where the human acts as Principal Investigator and the AI as a skilled graduate student. The system features internal verification for logical correctness, automated knowledge retrieval, and self-improvement to reduce human oversight. It autonomously handles literature synthesis, theorem proving, algorithm design, experimentation, and manuscript writing. Deployed on five research papers, ReasFlow outperforms existing open-access baselines in evaluation under a custom LLM-based rubric. The system is publicly available via ReasLab and GitHub.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing AI systems for scientific discovery are largely limited to empirically driven domains with quantitative benchmarks, leaving theory-driven, proof-intensive disciplines underexplored due to challenges in verifying reasoning, insufficient autonomous reasoning ability, and lack of procedural heuristics in current literature.

Method: ReasFlow employs a collaborative paradigm between human and AI, integrating an internal verification loop to ensure logical coherence and error correction before human review. It also includes an automated knowledge retrieval and self-improvement mechanism that identifies both factual knowledge and procedural heuristics. The system unifies multiple stages of research—including literature synthesis, theorem proving, algorithm design, experimentation, and manuscript preparation—into a single end-to-end workflow.

Result: ReasFlow successfully generated five complete, rigorous theoretical and empirical research papers from minimal prompts. It achieved the highest scores among state-of-the-art open-access baselines under a curated LLM-based review rubric, demonstrating superior performance in autonomous theoretical discovery.

Conclusion: ReasFlow establishes a new standard for autonomous, reasoning-centric scientific discovery in theory-driven domains. By reducing expert intervention through robust verification and proactive knowledge acquisition, it enables scalable, high-quality theoretical research in collaboration with AI, making it a powerful tool for future scientific advancement.

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models have fueled autonomous AI agents capable of tackling complex scientific tasks, yet existing automated research systems remain predominantly focused on empirically driven domains with quantitative benchmarks, leaving theory-driven discovery, particularly in mathematically grounded disciplines requiring rigorous proofs and synthesis of domain knowledge, largely underexplored. Key challenges include the difficulty of verifying theoretical reasoning at scale, insufficient reasoning ability for autonomous frontier exploration, and a scarcity of procedural heuristics in the literature. We introduce ReasFlow, an end-to-end autonomous agent system for reasoning-centric scientific discovery that operationalizes a collaborative paradigm where the human expert acts as Principal Investigator while the agent executes rigorous derivations as a capable graduate student. ReasFlow incorporates (i) a robust internal verification loop that audits logical coherence and corrects fundamental errors prior to human inspection, and (ii) an automated knowledge retrieval and self-improvement mechanism that proactively surfaces both declarative facts and overlooked procedural heuristics, substantially reducing expert intervention. The system unifies literature synthesis, algorithm design, theorem proving, experimentation, and manuscript preparation in a single system. Deployed to autonomously generate five complete research papers with rigorous theoretical and empirical content from minimal prompts, ReasFlow consistently achieves the highest evaluation scores among state-of-the-art open-access baselines under a curated LLM-based review rubric. ReasFlow is publicly accessible via the ReasLab platform, providing a collaborative workspace for AI-assisted theoretical research. Github repo: https://github.com/ReasLab/ReasFlow.git.

### [168] [RxBrain: Embodied Cognition Foundation Model with Joint Language-Visual Reasoning and Imagination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14187)
*Haotian Liang,Mingkang Chen,Yufei Huang,Yuchun Guo,Xiaomeng Zhu,Xiangli Shi,Kaixuan Wang,Yunxuan Mao,Weijie Zhou,Ling Chen,Shirong Zeng,Yueyu Long,Yuchen Si,Yajuan Zhu,Xingyu Zhou,Minghui Wang,Wanjia He,Xin Yang,Lingzhu Xiang,Zhiqing Liu,Bohan Ma,Xiran Huang,Tianshuo Yang,Zhiheng Liu,Xuantang Xiong,Zisheng Lu,Ping Luo,Yao Mu,Han Hu,Zhengyou Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Hy-Embodied-RxBrain 是一个融合语言-视觉推理与想象的具身认知基础模型，通过统一的多模态Mixture-of-Transformers架构实现联合规划。它将语言用于抽象计划结构（如任务分解、时序逻辑），视觉想象则用于预测世界状态和联合子目标规划，从而实现语言与视觉在具身计划中的互补。模型通过自动视频转规划监督的训练管道进行训练，并在RxBrain-Bench上验证了其联合文本-视觉规划能力。实验表明其具备强具身理解与生成能力，且无需大规模动作数据预训练即可在真实机器人上表现良好，为具身认知基础模型提供了初步范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统视觉-语言模型侧重场景理解与文本决策，生成式世界模型关注未来视觉状态预测，但缺乏将高层任务推理与物理状态达成相结合的能力。具身认知需要模型同时处理抽象语言规划与具体视觉状态预测，以实现连贯的具身行为规划。因此，亟需一种能够统一语言与视觉推理并支持联合规划的基础模型。

Method: 提出Hy-Embodied-RxBrain，采用统一的多模态Mixture-of-Transformers架构，支持语言、图像与视频的理解与生成。通过自动管道将具身视频分解为规划步骤，并对齐视觉状态转移与文本规划内容，生成联合文本-视觉规划监督信号。引入RxBrain-Bench评估模型在联合文本-视觉层面表示具身计划的能力。

Result: RxBrain在具身理解与生成方面表现优异，能生成耦合文本推理、世界状态预测与联合子目标规划的计划；在连续机器人动作生成中展现出良好的真实机器人性能，且无需大规模动作数据预训练。

Conclusion: 该工作为具身认知基础模型的发展提供了重要探索，展示了语言与视觉在联合规划中的互补潜力，推动了从感知到行动的端到端具身智能建模。

Abstract: Embodied cognition requires agents to connect high-level task reasoning with the physical states to be achieved. We introduce Hy-Embodied-RxBrain, an embodied cognition foundation model with joint language-visual reasoning and imagination. Unlike vision-language models that emphasize scene understanding and textual decision making, or generative world models that mainly predict future visual states, RxBrain represents embodied plans in a single planning sequence where language and visual imagination play complementary roles. Language provides the abstract structure of a plan, including task decomposition, planning primitives, constraints, temporal order, and decision logic, while visual imagination grounds this structure through world state prediction and joint subgoal planning, associating each planning step with intermediate and final physical states. RxBrain adopts a unified multimodal Mixture-of-Transformers architecture that supports language, image, and video understanding and generation within one model. To train this capability, we build an automatic pipeline that converts embodied videos into joint text-visual planning supervision by decomposing videos into planning steps and aligning them with visual state transitions. We further introduce RxBrain-Bench to evaluate whether models can represent embodied plans through joint textual and visual components rather than separate understanding or generation. Experiments show that RxBrain maintains embodied understanding and generation abilities, and produces plans with coupled textual reasoning, world state prediction, and joint subgoal planning. We also extend RxBrain to continuous robot action generation, where it shows promising real-robot performance without large-scale action-data pretraining. These results provide an initial step toward foundation models for embodied cognition.
