*Rachel Adams,Fola Adeleke,Ayantola Alayande,Selamawit Engida Abdella,Ana Florido,Nicolás Grossman,Leah Junck*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GIRAI 2026 evaluates how countries implement responsible AI commitments through policy, civil society engagement, and redress mechanisms across five dimensions. Despite widespread policy adoption (126 of 135 countries), most frameworks are non-binding, especially in the Global South. Transparency in government AI use remains weak, with only 18% requiring public disclosure of algorithms. Evidence of unacceptable-risk AI use was found in 35 countries. The study calls for enforceable rights-based protections and robust oversight.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To assess whether national responsible AI commitments translate into enforceable protections, institutional capacity, and accessible redress, particularly in light of growing global AI governance efforts and disparities between Global North and South.

Method: A global network of 135 researchers collected and analyzed 68,138 data points across 38 indicators grouped into three pillars: government AI policy and implementation (17 indicators), civil society engagement (5), enabling conditions (15), and documented cases of government deployment of unacceptable-risk AI systems. Data spans November 2023 to September 2025, with a score out of 100 used to rank countries.

Result: While 126 of 135 countries have at least one AI policy or initiative, many frameworks remain non-binding—especially in the Global South (78% non-binding vs. 42% in the Global North). Only 18% of countries require public disclosure of government algorithms, despite strong performance on transparency and explainability (58%). Credible evidence of unacceptable-risk AI use was found in 35 countries.

Conclusion: Responsible AI governance must evolve from mere framework adoption toward enforceable rights-based protections, adequately resourced oversight institutions, and accessible redress mechanisms to ensure real accountability and protection.

Abstract: Grounded in human rights-based frameworks such as the UNESCO Recommendation on the Ethics of AI, the Global Index on Responsible AI (GIRAI) examines how countries translate responsible AI commitments into enforceable protections, institutional capacity, and redress mechanisms. GIRAI 2026 assesses these across five dimensions: Inclusion and Diversity, Ethics and Sustainability, Labour and Skills, Trust and Safety, and AI Use in Public Service. A global network of 135 country-level researchers collected and assessed 68,138 data points on 38 indicators organised across three pillars: government AI policy and implementation (17 indicators), civil society engagement (5), enabling conditions (15), and documented cases of government deployment of unacceptable-risk AI systems. The data covers November 2023 to September 2025. A score of 100 is derived from the indicators to rank all countries. Findings show that while responsible AI governance is expanding, with 126 of 135 countries having at least one government policy or initiative across the 17 AI Policy indicators, this does not often translate into meaningful protection. For instance, Global South countries account for 203 of 306 new cases of indicators with frameworks since the first edition, yet 78% of their frameworks remain non-binding compared with 42% in the Global North. Government commitment to AI governance also does not extend to their own algorithms: whereas Transparency and Explainability is the strongest performing indicator, with 58% of countries having some framework, only 18% require Public Disclosure of Government Algorithms. Credible evidence of government deployment of unacceptable-risk AI systems was also found in 35 countries. These findings show that responsible AI governance must move beyond framework adoption toward enforceable rights-based protections, resourced oversight institutions, and accessible redress.

*Darius Lim,Nathan Leow,Xin Wei Chia*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索语言模型中欺骗行为的内在机制，提升其可解释性与安全性，防止潜在的安全与隐私风险。

Method: 采用分层预训练transcoder（PLTs）构建归因图，结合特征操控与电路分析方法，对欺骗相关特征进行识别与验证。

Result: 成功识别出一组与欺骗行为强相关的特征，这些特征能有效引导模型从非欺骗性输出转向欺骗性输出，表现出明显的可控性与可预测性。

Conclusion: 欺骗行为是语言模型内部机制的产物，transcoder技术为理解与监控此类行为提供了有力工具，具备应用于安全风险早期检测的潜力。

Abstract: Transcoders have recently emerged as a promising approach for mechanistic interpretability (MI), enabling circuit-level analysis of model behaviour. In this paper, we investigate the use of transcoders to analyse deceptive behaviour in language models, a behaviour that poses a safety and security risk. Using a Qwen3-4B model with pre-trained transcoders, specifically per-layer transcoders (PLTs), we construct attribution graphs that capture feature activations and inter-feature dependencies, allowing circuit-level analysis of deception. Through feature steering and circuit analysis, we identified a dictionary of deception-related features and show that these features exert a stronger influence on deceptive outputs, as they produce predictable shifts between deceptive and non-deceptive responses. These findings suggest that deception emerges from internal model mechanisms and highlight the potential of transcoders for behavioural monitoring and early detection of security vulnerabilities related to malicious behaviours in language models.

### [213] [Reachability-Aware Pretraining for Efficient Target-Oriented Path Exploration in Temporal Knowledge Graph Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14886)
*Chien-Liang Liu,Tsao-Lun Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RAPTOR是一种自监督预训练方法，通过引入可达性感知的归纳偏置，提升基于强化学习的多跳推理在时间知识图谱推理中的效率与性能。该方法通过估计候选动作对目标实体的可达性，减少对无望路径的探索，为下游强化学习微调提供良好初始化。实验表明，RAPTOR在ICEWS14、ICEWS05-15和ICEWS18数据集上显著提升了训练效率并优于传统基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于强化学习的多跳推理方法在时间知识图谱推理中虽能生成可解释的预测，但面临奖励稀疏和探索效率低下的问题，尤其在庞大且随时间演化的动作空间中难以有效训练。因此需要一种机制来引导探索、提高训练效率并增强模型性能。

Method: 提出RAPTOR（Reachability-Aware Pretraining for Efficient Target-Oriented Path Exploration），通过自监督学习预训练阶段估计候选动作对目标实体的可达性，从而注入可达性感知的归纳偏置，指导强化学习过程中的路径探索，减少无效探索，并为后续微调提供良好初始状态。

Result: 在ICEWS14、ICEWS05-15和ICEWS18数据集上的实验结果显示，RAPTOR显著提升了训练效率，且在多个指标上持续优于现有基线方法，证明其在增强强化学习驱动的多跳推理方面具有有效性。

Conclusion: RAPTOR通过引入可达性感知的预训练机制，有效缓解了时间知识图谱推理中强化学习训练的探索困境，显著提升了训练效率与预测性能，是一种高效且实用的增强方法。

Abstract: Temporal Knowledge Graph (TKG) reasoning under the extrapolation setting focuses on forecasting future time-stamped events (facts) from historical data in a temporal knowledge graph. Existing approaches, reinforcement learning (RL)-based multi-hop reasoning methods are prominent for TKG reasoning because they produce human-interpretable predictions via explicit multi-hop path tracing. However, during RL training, rewards are typically sparse, and exploration is highly inefficient due to the vast, time-evolving action space. These issues hinder efficient training and often limit overall performance. To address these challenges, we propose RAPTOR (Reachability-Aware Pretraining for Efficient Target-Oriented Path Exploration), a self-supervised pretraining method that injects a reachability-aware inductive bias to the agent. By learning to estimate the reachability of candidate actions to the target entity, RAPTOR reduces exploration over unpromising paths and provides a strong initialization for downstream RL fine-tuning. Experimental results on the ICEWS14, ICEWS05-15, and ICEWS18 datasets demonstrate that RAPTOR pretraining markedly improves the training efficiency and consistently outperforms conventional baselines, establishing it as an effective approach for enhancing RL-based multi-hop reasoning methods for TKG reasoning.

</details>


### [214] [Proof-or-Stop: Don't Trust the Agent, Trust the Evidence -- Loop Engineering for Verifiable Evidence-Gated Lifecycle Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14890)
*Jek Huang,Jeffery Hsia,Jiayi Sun,Freddie Shi,Wei Huang,Ian H. White*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出Proof-or-Stop生命周期控制方法，通过机械可验证的证据支持代码生命周期状态的转换，确保只有在满足条件时才能进入如已审查、已测试、可合并等状态。该方法将代理输出视为声明而非状态，并以可接受证据作为门控标准。评估显示其在多种测试中表现优异，零误判率，显著减少隐藏失败的放大效应，且具备模型无关和宿主中立性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自主编码代理虽能执行多步骤软件任务，但其生命周期状态（如已审查、已测试）常缺乏实时证据支持，导致状态声明不可靠。为解决这一问题，需引入一种机制，使状态转移必须依赖于可追踪、可验证的最新证据，从而提升自动化流程的可信度与安全性。

Method: 提出Proof-or-Stop生命周期控制方法，要求每个生命周期状态的变更必须基于新鲜、可追踪、源代码状态绑定的机械可验证证据；采用信任模型定义“证明”的可接受性，不依赖语义正确性，而是基于门控准入标准。系统通过机制测试、控制策略消融实验和自应用证据验证其有效性。

Result: 未受干预的循环引擎在10个场景中全部成功，无误标为DONE的情况；本地密钥接收包拒绝了18类篡改行为，无误接受；在9,240单元的消融实验中，有门控的循环相比朴素循环将可见通过/隐藏失败放大从31/1,800降至2/1,800，提升1.6个百分点（95%置信区间[0.8, 2.5]）。自应用数据集包含565个故事和1,007条评审发现，94.8%被解决，且存在高/关键级别的跨供应商实例。结果表明该方法有效、可靠且具有通用性。

Conclusion: Proof-or-Stop提供了一种模型无关、宿主中立的控制层，用于决定哪些自主代理的声明可以影响生命周期状态，显著提升了自动化软件开发流程的可信度与安全性，但仍受限于单一模型家族、24个消融任务及自托管语料库。

Abstract: Autonomous coding agents increasingly execute multi-step software work, but lifecycle states such as reviewed, tested, DONE, and ready-to-merge remain claims unless supported by current evidence. We present Proof-or-Stop Lifecycle Control, a method that permits lifecycle transitions only when fresh, tracked-source-state-bound, mechanically verifiable evidence satisfies the relevant gate. The method treats agent outputs as claims rather than lifecycle state, and uses proof operationally to mean gate-admissible evidence under a stated trust model, not semantic program correctness.
  We evaluate an open-source implementation through mechanism tests, a powered control-policy ablation, and operated self-application evidence. The unattended-loop engine passed 10 of 10 scenarios with zero false-DONE, and local-key receipt bundles rejected 18 tamper classes with zero false accepts. In a 9,240-cell ablation, the pre-registered A4 versus A2-prime comparison reduced visible-pass/hidden-fail amplification from 31 of 1,800 injected cells under a compute-budgeted naive loop to 2 of 1,800 under the gated loop, a 1.6 percentage-point improvement in not-amplified rate with a 95 percent confidence interval of [0.8, 2.5]. A near-compute A3 versus A4 comparison, 14 of 1,800 versus 2 of 1,800, indicates that the gain is associated with enforcing review as a lifecycle gate rather than merely adding a reviewer. The self-application corpus contains 565 stories and 1,007 review findings, with 94.8 percent resolved, plus a 68-row high/critical cross-vendor exhibit. These results support Proof-or-Stop as a model-agnostic, host-neutral control layer for deciding which autonomous-agent claims a lifecycle may act on. The evaluation is limited to one model family, 24 ablation tasks, and a self-hosted corpus.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Online firestorms are rapid collective escalations of highly negative user-generated content and may cause substantial reputational and economic damage. The first mode classifies complete Reddit threads retrospectively by combining local chunk-level assessments into a thread-level judgment. The second mode processes threads sequentially and issues early warnings when a sliding window exceeds calibrated thresholds. In this mode, the language model estimates three firestorm indicators: negativity share, escalation level, and contributor count. On a balanced Reddit dataset, the global mode achieves strong classification performance, while the early warning mode reaches high recall and detects escalating threads after only a small number of comments and distinct contributors. The results indicate that LLMs can be used not only for static judgment tasks, but also as repeated estimators in context-aware monitoring of social media discourse.

Abstract: Automated optimisation is increasingly adopted in industrial processes, yet a trust gap persists between engineers who design these algorithms and operators who must act on their recommendations. Explainable AI methods like SHAP (SHapley Additive exPlanations) have transformed interpretability for machine learning predictions; optimisation outputs could benefit from similar techniques. We present an approach that integrates Implicit Function Theorem (IFT) based sensitivity analysis with SHAP attribution and narrative generation via Large Language Models (LLM), producing explanations tailored for operators. ### [217] [CFM-Bench: A Unified Multi-Domain, Multi-Task Benchmark for Channel Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14975)
*Yuan Gao,Wenjun Yu,Jun Jiang,Yunfan Li,Xinyu Guo,Shugong Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CFM-Bench is a unified, multi-domain, multi-task benchmark for channel foundation models (CFMs), designed to enable fair comparison across models, domains, and tasks by standardizing data, splits, and evaluation protocols. It includes diverse channel configurations from simulations to real-world measurements and covers key wireless tasks in PHY, RAN, and ISAC domains.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing CFM evaluations suffer from inconsistent setups—varying data, configurations, partitions, and metrics—making it difficult to fairly compare models or assess transferability. This lack of standardization limits progress in the field.

Method: CFM-Bench introduces a standardized benchmark with six distinct channel configurations, official data splits that prevent pretraining on test sets, strict rules on data disclosure, and a structured task framework across three application dimensions: PHY channel intelligence, RAN decision intelligence, and ISAC.

Result: The benchmark enables consistent and transparent evaluation of CFMs, allowing researchers to assess model transferability across different channels, tasks, and domains without bias from differing experimental designs.

Conclusion: CFM-Bench establishes a reliable, reproducible, and fair evaluation framework for channel foundation models, promoting meaningful comparisons and advancing research in wireless AI.

Abstract: Channel foundation models (CFMs) are developing rapidly, with recent studies reporting benefits from pretraining across downstream wireless tasks. Yet CFMs are commonly evaluated in model-specific pipelines with different data, radio configurations, partitions, adaptation procedures, task definitions, and metrics. Reported comparisons therefore tend to show that pretraining improves over supervised training from scratch within one pipeline, but neither rank CFMs nor compare them fairly with task-specific models. We release CFM-Bench, a unified multi-domain, multi-task benchmark designed to address this gap. It curates six channel configurations spanning 3GPP statistical simulation, two independent ray-tracing pipelines, industrial and aerial measurements, and synchronized vehicular multimodal simulation. Official partitions isolate complete trajectories, measurement sessions, vehicle links, simulation realizations, or buffered spatial regions. CFM-Bench does not prescribe an external pretraining corpus or strategy; no benchmark split may be used for foundation-model pretraining, and the official training split is reserved exclusively for downstream fine-tuning. The benchmark additionally requires disclosure of all data used during model development and prohibits training-stage use of official test units. Six task groups are organized along three CFM application dimensions: physical-layer (PHY) channel intelligence, radio-access-network (RAN) decision intelligence, and integrated sensing and communication (ISAC). They cover CSI feedback, frequency and temporal channel extrapolation, propagation-state classification, current- and future-beam prediction, and single-frame and temporal localization. CFM-Bench provides a common substrate for comparing the transferability of channel representations across models, domains, and tasks.

*Mahmoud Ibrahim,Bart Elen,Chang Sun,Gokhan Ertaylan,Michel Dumontier*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出使用基于人口统计学条件的合成生成器来解决医疗图像分类器在少数群体子组上的公平性审计中的样本量不足问题。通过使用端到端微调的Stable Diffusion 2.1生成器，研究发现：在训练阶段，以平衡的人口统计学合成数据作为预训练先验优于联合增强，能在约100倍的数据效率下超越全真实数据基线；在评估阶段，合成估计器在五个少数群体和五种子模型下与真实基准保持完全一致的子组排序（Spearman ρ=1.00），并在真实测试集样本不足时提供更可靠的性能估计。因此，合成数据在公平性审计最关注的少数群体中同时实现了偏见缓解与检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗图像分类器的公平性审计在少数群体子组上面临样本量过少的问题，导致置信区间过大，无法有效检测偏见。现有方法难以在训练和评估两端同时解决此问题。

Method: 采用基于人口统计学条件的合成生成器（基于Stable Diffusion 2.1）构建均衡的合成数据集，分别用于训练阶段的预训练先验和评估阶段的合成测试集。比较了顺序预训练+微调与联合增强两种训练策略，并在多个子组和模型种子下评估合成数据在性能估计上的可靠性。

Conclusion: 基于人口统计学条件的合成生成器在训练和评估两端均能有效应对少数群体样本不足问题，既可作为缓解偏见的训练先验，也可作为高可靠性的公平性审计工具，尤其适用于公平性审计最关心的少数群体子组。

Abstract: Per-subgroup fairness audits of medical image classifiers face a sample-size problem: minority subgroups in held-out test sets have so few samples that the resulting confidence intervals on per-subgroup performance are wider than the bias the audit is meant to detect. We argue that a demographically-conditioned synthetic generator can do both: mitigate bias on the training side and detect bias on the evaluation side. Working on COVID-19 chest CT classification with an end-to-end fine-tuned Stable Diffusion 2.1 generator, we make two findings. For bias mitigation (training), a demographically-balanced synthetic cohort is most useful as a pretraining prior, not as joint augmentation: with the same fixed data, sequential pretraining followed by fine-tuning substantially outperforms joint augmentation, and the resulting classifier surpasses the full-real baseline at $\sim$$100\times$ real-data efficiency. For bias detection (evaluation), across five synthetic minority cohorts and five classifier seeds, the synthetic estimator reproduces the subgroup ranking of a well-powered real oracle (Spearman $ρ= 1.00$ on MCC and Recall) and gives the more reliable per-cell estimate where the small real test set runs out of samples. The synthetic cohort is therefore most useful in exactly the cells that fairness audits care about, as both a fix for and a measure of subgroup bias.

### [220] [SMC-ES: Automated synthesis of formally verified control policies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15003)
*Riccardo Curcio,Toni Mancini,Enrico Tronci*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于模拟的新型方法，用于自动合成具有形式化保证的策略，确保在安全关键环境中的性能、安全性和鲁棒性。该方法结合进化策略与基于统计模型检查的验证，生成带有证书的策略，以高置信度保证违反指定属性的概率不超过给定阈值。通过在Gymnasium和Safety Gymnasium测试平台上评估，结果表明该方法在可接受的计算开销下，实现了对性能、安全性和鲁棒性的形式化保证，并且在性能上优于主流无模型深度强化学习和安全强化学习基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于学习的方法（如强化学习）虽能高效合成控制器，但缺乏形式化保证，难以应用于安全关键场景。因此需要一种既能保证性能又能提供形式化安全与鲁棒性证明的控制策略合成方法。

Method: 提出SMC-ES算法，将进化策略（Evolutionary Strategies）与基于统计模型检查（Statistical Model Checking）的验证相结合，通过模拟实现对策略的验证与优化，在满足给定置信度和失败概率约束下，生成具备形式化保证的策略。

Result: 在多个连续控制任务中，SMC-ES能够以可控的计算成本提供形式化保证，同时在性能上媲美甚至超越现有的先进模型无关深度强化学习和安全强化学习方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的SMC-ES方法成功实现了在安全关键系统中部署高性能、可证明安全与鲁棒的自主控制策略的目标，为学习型控制系统的可信应用提供了有效途径。

Abstract: The deployment of autonomous cyber-physical systems in safety-critical environments requires closed-loop control strategies (i.e., policies) that are not only performant but also provably safe and robust. While learning-based methodologies such as Reinforcement Learning offer flexible and scalable approaches to automatically synthesize such controllers, they typically lack the formal guarantees necessary for safe deployment. To bridge this gap, we propose a novel simulation-based methodology to automatically synthesize policies with formal guarantees regarding performance, safety, and robustness specifications. Specifically, given a set of properties to verify, a confidence parameter $δ$ and an allowable failure probability $\varepsilon$, our method guarantees that the synthesized policy comes with a certificate: with confidence at least $1 - δ$, the probability of encountering a scenario where the given properties are violated is at most $\varepsilon$. We demonstrate the feasibility of our approach by developing SMC-ES, an algorithm that integrates Evolutionary Strategies with Statistical Model Checking-based verification. We evaluate SMC-ES on a suite of continuous control tasks using Gymnasium and Safety Gymnasium testbeds. Results show that, at the price of a sustainable increase in computational cost, our algorithm provides formal guarantees regarding performance, safety, and robustness specifications, while performing competitively against leading model-free Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) and Safe-DRL baselines.

Rather than aiming to resolve ownership, the provotype was used to elicit artists' responses to the idea of attributing ownership through measurable actions in the creative workflow. We argue that quantification fails to align with artists' understandings of creative intent and agency, and that efforts to measure ownership risk diluting long-standing assumptions through which artists understand and practice creative work. ### [222] [BrainPilot: Automating Brain Discovery with Agentic Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15079)
*Haoxuan Li,Tianci Gao,Jianhe Li,Yang Fan,Runze Shi,Weiran Wang,Tianxiang Zhao,Zezhao Wu,Xiaoyang Jiang,Qihui Zhang,Jia Li,Xiao Xiao,Kai Du,Xiaoxuan Jia,Chao Xie,Lu Mi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BrainPilot 是一个完全开源的多智能体系统，旨在加速脑科学研究。它通过协调具备领域知识的专家智能体，结合7,233个条目的脑科学知识库和72个可复用的方法学单元，实现从文献调研到分析解释的全流程自动化。系统采用可追溯的“追踪图”记录每一步操作，包括子目标、工具使用、证据与结论之间的关联，并引入审计智能体防止虚假声明。在多个任务和自建基准 BrainPilotBench-v0 上测试表明，其性能接近最先进的代理框架，但成本更低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI代理在脑科学领域缺乏专业知识，易产生虚假信息、推理漂移，且缺乏专家干预点，而脑科学依赖实验室特异性知识和严谨的人类判断，因此需要更可靠、可追溯的智能协作系统。

Method: BrainPilot 采用主研究员（PI）智能体协调多个基于领域知识的专家智能体，依托统一的知识库和方法技能库；所有关键步骤被记录在可审计的‘追踪图’中，同时引入审计智能体进行事实核查，确保结果可信。

Result: 在Agents' Last Exam任务、自建基准BrainPilotBench-v0及端到端案例研究中，BrainPilot展现出与顶尖代理框架相当的性能，但使用开源模型，显著降低计算成本。

Conclusion: BrainPilot 提供了一种可信赖、可追溯、低成本的多智能体解决方案，适用于复杂跨尺度脑科学研究，推动了人工智能在脑科学中的负责任应用。

Abstract: Understanding the brain increasingly depends on integrating evidence across scales, modalities, and disciplines. Addressing a single research question therefore requires a coordinated sequence of operations, from surveying prior work to executing analyses and interpreting results in light of domain knowledge. AI agents promise to accelerate this process, but current agents lack domain expertise in brain science, may fabricate claims, drift during multi-step reasoning, and offer few defined points for expert intervention. These failures are especially costly in brain science, where conclusions feed into downstream scientific claims and depend on laboratory-specific expertise and careful human judgment. We present \textbf{BrainPilot} a \textbf{fully open-source} multi-agent system that accelerates brain science research with traceable logs and agent-verified results. A principal investigator (PI) agent coordinates specialist agents grounded in curated domain knowledge: a unified brain science knowledge base containing 7{,}233 indexed items and a skill library of 72 reusable methodology units across seven research domains. Every major step is recorded in the Graph of Trace, an auditable record that links subgoals, tool use, evidence, and claims and allows researchers to follow and inspect the workflow. An Auditor agent further integrates fabrication checking into the workflow. For evaluation, we run three brain science tasks from Agents' Last Exam, introduce our own benchmark, \textbf{BrainPilotBench-v0}, and present additional end-to-end case studies. Across these evaluations, BrainPilot with an open-source backbone model attains performance comparable to state-of-the-art agent framework with less costs.

### [223] [Long-Context Fine-Tuning with Limited VRAM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15105)
*Vladimir Fedosov,Aleksandr Sazhin,Artemiy Grinenko,Frank Woernle*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HGA结合分段反向传播和分层KV存储，使长序列训练在有限显存下成为可能。相比密集注意力，HGA在2,048令牌时性能相当，但在4,096令牌时失败；而使用HGA的模型可扩展至16,384令牌，峰值显存仅15.28GB。评估中单个适配器可处理131,072令牌，显存随驻留块摘要缓慢增长，实际限制由内存和NVMe容量决定。在相同2K训练长度下，HGA与密集训练的适配器表现接近（2.7405 vs 2.7383 nat），但HGA已略快，且随着上下文增长优势将进一步扩大。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决参数高效微调中密集注意力导致长序列训练显存开销过大的问题，实现更高效的长上下文训练。

Method: 采用层次化全局注意力（HGA）结合分段反向传播与分层键值（KV）存储机制，仅保持活跃段在显存中可导，旧的KV被分离至内存或NVMe，HGA为每个查询块加载有限的历史准确令牌。

Result: 在Qwen3-8B模型上，4位QLoRA与PG19数据集下，传统密集训练在16GB GPU上最多支持2,048令牌，无法扩展至4,096；而HGA方法在相同硬件下支持高达16,384令牌，峰值显存15.28GB。评估阶段可处理131,072令牌，显存增长平缓，实际极限取决于系统内存与存储容量。在2,048令牌训练下，两者性能相近（2.7405 vs 2.7383 nat），但HGA训练速度更快（217.75 vs 207.02 tokens/s），且随上下文增长吞吐优势持续扩大。

Conclusion: HGA通过优化注意力机制与内存管理，显著提升了长序列训练的可扩展性与效率，在保证模型质量的同时降低了显存占用，是实现大规模上下文训练的有效方案。

Abstract: Parameter-efficient fine-tuning reduces model and optimizer memory, but dense attention still makes long training sequences expensive. We combine Hierarchical Global Attention (HGA) with segment-wise backpropagation and tiered KV storage. Only the active segment remains differentiable in VRAM; older KV is detached into RAM or NVMe, and HGA loads a bounded set of exact historical tokens for each query block. On Qwen3-8B with 4-bit QLoRA and PG19, dense training on a 16 GB Quadro RTX 5000 fits 2,048 tokens but fails at 4,096, whereas HGA reaches 16,384 tokens with 15.28 GB peak VRAM. Under evaluation the same adapter runs through 131,072 tokens on this card; VRAM is not constant but grows gently with the resident chunk summaries, so RAM and NVMe capacity set the practical limit beyond these lengths. At the shared 2K training length, HGA-trained and dense-trained adapters obtain 2.7405 and 2.7383 nat under the same dense-attention readout, while the stock model obtains 2.9541. At this boundary HGA training is already marginally faster (217.75 vs. 207.02 tokens/s), and the HGA-to-dense throughput ratio improves from 1K to 2K; because HGA keeps the attended historical set per token approximately constant while dense work per token grows, we expect this lead to widen as context grows. Dense attention is used for the main quality and retrieval comparisons so that they measure the learned weights and remain compatible with standard generation frameworks. HGA can also be used for retrieval and generation; an optimized production-grade serving implementation is under development.

### [224] [Concept-Guided Spatial Regularization for World Models in Atari Pong](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15142)
*Yukuan Lu,Zaishuo Xia,Weyl Lu,Yubei Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了五个代表性视觉世界模型（DreamerV3、DIAMOND、TWISTER、Simulus、STORM）在Atari Pong中的表现，通过冻结模型并进行闭环滚动诊断和像素空间零样本MBRL评估，发现所有模型在生成视频轨迹时存在明显错误，如球消失、运动异常和无效碰撞。此外，在零样本训练中，新策略在真实环境中的表现远低于原始MBRL方法，尤其在DreamerV3上性能下降显著。作者提出概念引导的空间正则化（CGSReg），通过在分割的概念区域上引入辅助重建损失，有效提升了多个模型的闭环滚动和零样本任务表现，但无法解决所有瓶颈问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型通常作为MBRL系统的一部分被评估，而其自身能力在孤立状态下鲜有研究。本研究旨在揭示当前视觉世界模型在关键任务概念建模上的不足，并探索提升其泛化与准确性的方式。

Method: 通过复现五种世界模型的训练流程并匹配报告性能，冻结模型后采用闭环滚动诊断（观察政策交互生成的视频轨迹）和像素空间零样本MBRL（在冻结模型内训练新策略并评估其在真实环境中的表现）两种方式评估模型质量；进一步提出概念引导的空间正则化（CGSReg），在分割的概念区域施加额外的像素重建损失以增强对关键对象（如球）的建模。

Result: 所有五种世界模型在闭环滚动中均出现视觉与动力学错误；在零样本MBRL中，策略性能普遍大幅下降，尤其DreamerV3从-5.5降至-20.9；应用CGSReg后，DreamerV3、DIAMOND和TWISTER在闭环与零样本任务中均有改善，但其他模型效果不一，表明该方法不能完全解决所有世界模型缺陷。

Conclusion: 当前主流视觉世界模型在建模任务关键概念方面仍存在明显不足，导致在封闭环路与零样本任务中表现不佳。提出的CGSReg能有效提升部分模型的建模能力，但世界模型的全面改进仍需更深入的方法设计。

Abstract: World models are usually evaluated as components of model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) systems, while the world models themselves are rarely studied in isolation.
  We examine five representative visual world-model agents in Atari Pong: DreamerV3, DIAMOND, TWISTER, Simulus, and STORM. After reproducing their training pipelines and matching the reported agent performance, we freeze the learned world models and evaluate them with a closed-loop rollout diagnostic: a policy trained separately from the corresponding MBRL agent interacts with each frozen model, and the generated video trajectories are inspected for visual and dynamical errors. Across all five models, the rollouts contain clear failures, including ball disappearance, incorrect ball motion, and invalid ball-paddle interactions.
  Beyond visual trajectories, we further evaluate them with pixel-space zero-shot MBRL, where a new policy is trained entirely inside a frozen world model and then evaluated in the real environment. Across all five models, the resulting policies substantially underperform those produced by the corresponding original MBRL training pipelines. The gap is particularly large for DreamerV3, whose mean return drops from -5.5 to -20.9, near the minimum Pong return of -21.
  We hypothesize that insufficient modeling of task-critical concepts, such as the ball in Pong, may contribute to these failures. We therefore propose Concept-Guided Spatial Regularization (CGSReg), an auxiliary pixel reconstruction loss applied to segmented concept regions. Experiments show that CGSReg improves both closed-loop rollouts and pixel-space zero-shot MBRL in DreamerV3, DIAMOND, and TWISTER. Its effects vary across the remaining models and evaluation metrics, indicating that CGSReg alone does not address all world-model bottlenecks.

### [225] [The Industrialization of Research ; On AI-Driven Science and Its Consequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15164)
*Emmanuel Jeannot*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨人工智能在科学研究中的角色转变，从辅助工具演变为自主参与研究周期的实体，标志着科研的‘工业化’。以美国能源部的基因组任务为例，文章提出七个核心问题：科学能力代际传承的削弱、AI生成理论的不透明性、同行评审机制因机器产出激增而失效、AI在范式突破性发现上的能力尚未验证、科学议程被政治与工业力量操控、闭环系统中系统性错误的累积，以及全球科研社区的结构性分化。这些问题并非反对AI科学，而是为负责任地推进其发展提供前提条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着人工智能在科研中从辅助工具转变为自主参与者，传统科研模式面临根本性变革，亟需反思其带来的深层影响和潜在风险，以确保科技进步与科学伦理、社会公平相协调。

Method: 通过分析美国能源部的基因组任务这一典型案例，结合对当前科研生态的观察，提出七个关键挑战，并采用批判性论述方法探讨其背后的根本性问题。

Result: 识别出人工智能驱动科研所引发的七项重大挑战，强调这些挑战是实现负责任科技创新的必要反思基础，而非否定技术潜力。

Conclusion: 人工智能推动科研工业化是不可逆转的趋势，但必须在承认并解决上述七大问题的前提下，才能确保其发展既有效又可持续，从而实现科技与科学价值的协同进步。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence is transforming scientific research - not merely as a more powerful instrument, but as an autonomous participant in the research cycle itself. This transition constitutes, in the most precise sense of the term, the industrialization of research: a shift from a craft model, in which knowledge, method, and judgment are embedded in the researcher, to a pipeline model, in which these steps are decomposed, automated, and supervised. The US Department of Energy's Genesis Mission is the most ambitious current instantiation of this shift, but the fundamental questions it raises extend far beyond any single program. This essay examines seven such questions: the erosion of the intergenerational transmission of scientific competence; the growing opacity of AI-generated theories; the collapse of peer evaluation under a flood of machine-generated output; the unproven capacity of AI for paradigm-shifting discovery; the capture of the scientific agenda by political and industrial actors; the compounding of systematic errors in closed-loop pipelines; and the structural bifurcation of the global research community into incommensurable tiers. These concerns do not constitute an argument against AI-driven science - whose demonstrated potential is real and significant. They constitute the conditions under which that potential can be responsibly pursued.

### [226] [MedFailBench: A Clinician-Built Open-Source Benchmark for Medical AI Safety Boundary Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15166)
*Goktug Ozkan*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发布版本v0.2.1包含44个经临床审核的合成案例，具备完整标签体系、实时HuggingFace排行榜预览、安全门分类框架、临床严重性评分规则以及自动化归档工具链，为医疗AI安全性评估提供可复用的基准平台。

Conclusion: MedFailBench 提供了一种系统化、可扩展的方法来识别和分类医疗AI模型的安全失效，推动从‘正确性’评估转向‘安全性’评估，有助于实现更可信、更可靠的临床辅助AI系统。

Abstract: Most medical AI benchmarks measure whether a model knows the correct answer. MedFailBench asks a different question: which safety boundary failed? We present a clinician-built synthetic benchmark and failure atlas that labels medical AI errors by severity (1--5) and safety gate type (missed urgent escalation, unsafe remote dosing, unsafe discharge reassurance, evidence fabrication, unsafe protocol execution, source support gap). The current public release (v0.2.1) contains 44 clinician-reviewed synthetic cases with severity annotations, a live HuggingFace leaderboard preview, a safety gate taxonomy, a clinical severity rubric, and an automated pipeline for archiving model-response screening runs. No patient data, clinical validation claims, or model rankings are included. MedFailBench is released under Apache-2.0 and CC-BY-4.0 and carries the Zenodo DOI 10.5281/zenodo.21205535.

### [227] [Benchmarking Multimodal Large Language Models for Scientific Visualization Literacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15176)
*Patrick Phuoc Do,Chau M. Ta,Chaoli Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究评估了六种多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在科学可视化（SciVis）理解能力上的表现，使用包含49个题目的标准化测试，涵盖18个科学可视化实例，涉及8种可视化技术与11种任务类型。结果显示，当前MLLMs在SciVis理解上表现不均，Gemini表现最佳，超过人类平均水平，而开源模型普遍低于人类基准。模型在科学插图、搜索和空间理解任务中表现较好，但在纹理和整合型可视化以及定量估计任务中表现较差。错误分析揭示了在细粒度定量估计、流动方向解读和基于上下文的编码理解方面的系统性失败。研究强调将SciVis素养作为评估多模态AI系统的重要维度，并公开了代码与模型输出。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了一个包含49个题目的标准化科学可视化素养评估测试，涵盖18个科学可视化实例，覆盖8种可视化技术与11种任务类型；评估三款闭源与三款开源MLLMs，在封闭世界协议下进行测试，并基于485名人类参与者的数据进行对比分析。

Result: Gemini是表现最强的模型，整体超越人类平均表现；而开源模型普遍低于人类基准。模型在科学插图、搜索和空间理解任务中表现良好，但在纹理基、整合型可视化及定量估计任务中表现不佳。错误分析显示存在对细粒度定量估计、流动方向判断和上下文编码理解的系统性缺陷。

Conclusion: 科学可视化素养应成为评估多模态人工智能系统的核心维度之一。当前模型在复杂科学可视化理解方面仍存在明显短板，需进一步改进以实现真正意义上的跨模态智能理解。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are increasingly used to interpret visualizations, yet current evaluations remain largely chart-centric and provide limited evidence of understanding of scientific visualization (SciVis). We benchmark six MLLMs on the scientific visualization literacy assessment test, a standardized SciVis literacy assessment comprising 49 items based on 18 scientific visualizations and illustrations, spanning 8 techniques and 11 task types. We evaluate three closed-source and three open-source models under a closed-world protocol and compare their performance using data from 485 human participants. Results show that current MLLMs do not exhibit uniform SciVis literacy. Gemini is the strongest model overall, exceeding the human mean across the evaluated subsets, whereas the open-source models remain below the human baseline. Performance is highly uneven across techniques and tasks: models perform best on scientific illustration, search, and spatial understanding, but struggle on texture-based and integration-based visualizations and on quantitative estimation. Error analysis reveals recurring failures in fine-grained quantitative estimation, flow-direction interpretation, and grounded encoding interpretation. These findings position SciVis literacy as a necessary benchmark dimension for evaluating multimodal AI systems. Our code and model outputs are publicly available at https://github.com/patdmp/mllm-scivis-lit-benchmark.

### [228] [Can We Trust Item Response Theory for AI Evaluation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15190)
*Han Jiang,Sunbeom Kwon,Jinwen Luo,Ziang Xiao,Susu Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在人工智能评估中使用项目反应理论（IRT）模型时，由于数据特征与人类测试场景存在显著差异，导致传统IRT估计工具面临可靠性挑战。通过模拟六大数据集下的18,000种条件，比较四种主流估计方法（边际最大似然、马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛、变分推断、神经伪西门子估计器），发现经典方法在大规模基准下可能不可行，而可扩展方法在小样本或非正态分布模型集合中可能导致不可靠的排名与项目推断。研究明确了何时可信赖潜变量模型支持评估结论，并提出所需样本量与诊断标准以确保评估可信性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI基准测试中广泛采用项目反应理论（IRT）进行模型能力评估、系统排序、示例选择和质量诊断，但其数据特征（如模型数量少、项目多、能力分布偏斜或聚类）与人类测试环境差异显著，现有IRT工具的适用性存疑，亟需系统评估其在真实场景中的可靠性。

Method: 基于六个主流大语言模型基准的数据，提取项目参数与模型能力分布，模拟三种常见IRT模型下的响应矩阵；在18,000种不同条件下，对比四种主流估计方法：边际最大似然、马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛、变分推断、神经伪西门子估计器；从计算可行性、可扩展性及推断可靠性三个维度评估各方法表现。

Result: 经典估计方法在大规模基准中常因计算负担过重而不可行；可扩展方法虽具备高效性，但在模型数量少或能力分布非正态时，会产生不可靠的模型排名与项目特性推断；研究识别出可靠使用潜变量模型的关键条件，包括最低样本量要求和必要的诊断指标。

Conclusion: 当前主流IRT工具在典型AI基准场景下存在显著局限性，不能随意用于支持评估结论；为确保评估结果可信，必须根据数据特征选择合适方法，并满足最小样本量与诊断验证要求，否则可能导致误导性推断。

Abstract: AI benchmarks increasingly leverage item-level statistical models, particularly item response theory (IRT), to estimate model capabilities, rank systems, select informative examples, and diagnose benchmark quality. However, AI benchmark data often departs from the data regime of human testing, for which standard IRT estimation tools were originally developed: benchmarks typically involve fewer evaluated models, far more items, and capability distributions that may be skewed, clustered, or multimodal. We examine how these regime mismatches challenge the reliability of IRT modeling for AI evaluation. Using item parameters and capability distributions derived from six widely used LLM benchmarks, we simulate response matrices under three common IRT models and compare four estimation tools used in recent benchmark studies: marginal maximum likelihood, Markov chain Monte Carlo, variational inference, and a neural pseudo-Siamese estimator. Across 18,000 simulation conditions, we systematically evaluate computational feasibility, scalability, and the reliability of IRT inferences about model rankings, predicted performance, and item characteristics. Results show that classical estimators can become infeasible in large benchmark settings, whereas scalable estimators can produce unreliable item-level and ranking inferences with small or nonnormally distributed model sets. This study identifies when latent trait models reliably support or risk distorting AI benchmarking claims, and what sample sizes and diagnostics are needed for trustworthy use.

Our results show that many autonomous GUI-agent failures are structurally repairable when plans remain visible and interventions are localized, and that explicit replanning helps make GUI automation more transparent, controllable, and adaptable.

### [231] [When Words Are Safe But Actions Kill: Probing Physical Danger Beyond Text Safety in Hidden-State Risk Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15218)
*Weimeng Wang,Ziqiang Wang,Zihang Zhan,Chuanpu Fu,Qi Li,Ke Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型（LLM）在具身智能体中的安全问题，区分了文本层面的内容危险（CD）与物理层面的危险（PD），发现二者在模型表示中可分离。提出PRISM方法，通过单层L2正则化逻辑探针检测物理危险，在SafeAgentBench上实现86.2–87.7%准确率与11.7–13.7%假阳性率，优于传统LLM判断。进一步构建PSB-1K基准测试无直接危险词的1000对物理风险样本，验证方法能识别隐含物理危险而非仅关键词。PRISM在PSB-1K上达99.6%准确率和0.7%假阳性率，显著降低误判安全任务比例。该方法在多个基准上表现优异，证明基于隐藏状态探测的物理安全机制具有泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型作为具身智能体的高层规划器时，看似无害的指令在物理世界中可能引发危险。现有方法多关注文本层面的内容安全，但物理危险是否属于同一类问题尚不明确。需要一种能有效识别物理风险、避免误判安全任务的方法，以提升具身智能系统的安全性。

Method: 通过隐藏状态方向分析和随机分割零假设检验，验证内容危险与物理危险在大语言模型表示空间中的可分离性；设计PRISM模型，采用单层L2正则化逻辑探针，基于全隐藏状态进行物理危险检测；构建对比性基准PSB-1K，包含1000对无直接危险词的物理风险样本，用于评估方法是否真正识别物理风险而非依赖显式关键词。

Result: PRISM在SafeAgentBench上达到86.2–87.7%准确率，假阳性率仅为11.7–13.7%，显著优于同规模LLM判断（假阳性率24.7–39.0%）。在PSB-1K上准确率达99.6%，假阳性率低至0.7%，而Qwen2.5-3B模型误拒67.8%的安全任务。该方法在SafeText和EARBench上也表现出良好性能，表明其具备跨任务泛化能力。

Conclusion: 内容危险与物理危险在大语言模型中是可分离的信号，基于隐藏状态的探测方法（如PRISM）能够高效、精准地识别物理层面的潜在风险，同时大幅减少对安全任务的误判，为具身智能系统提供了一种可靠且可扩展的物理安全防护机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly serve as high-level planners for embodied agents, where linguistically benign instructions can become unsafe once grounded in the physical world. We study whether this physically grounded danger is the same safety problem as ordinary text-level content danger. Through hidden-state direction analysis and random-split null tests, we show that content danger (CD) and physical danger (PD) form separable signals in LLM representations across Qwen2.5-3B/7B/14B/32B, Phi-3.5 and SmolLM2. Building on the CD/PD separability, we propose PRISM, a single-layer L2-regularized logistic probe over full hidden states. PRISM achieves 86.2--87.7\% accuracy on SafeAgentBench with 11.7--13.7\% FPR, while same-scale LLM judges over-block safe tasks at 24.7--39.0\% FPR. We further introduce PhysicalSafetyBench-1K (PSB-1K), a contrastive benchmark of 1{,}000 physical-risk pairs without direct harm keywords, to test whether methods detect physically grounded danger rather than explicit unsafe wording. On PSB-1K, PRISM reaches 99.6\% accuracy and 0.7\% FPR, whereas a Qwen2.5-3B judge rejects 67.8\% of safe tasks. PRISM also replicates on SafeText and EARBench, supporting hidden-state probing as a representation-level method for physical safety beyond text moderation.

Given a research question in natural language, AutoSynthesis formulates a search strategy, retrieves scientific literature, screens candidate studies, assesses full-text eligibility, extracts quantitative statistics, computes standardized effect sizes, and finally performs random-effects meta-analysis. The pooled effect estimates produced by AutoSynthesis are similar to Hedges' $g$ of expert-conducted meta-analyses, indicating close agreement with manual evidence synthesis. Together, these results show that AutoSynthesis can make quantitative evidence synthesis more scalable, thereby supporting evidence-based decision-making across disciplines.

We present teLLMe, a system for exploratory causal analysis of urban driving datasets. *Yuyao Zhang,Junjie Gao,Zhengxian Wu,Jiaming Fan,Jin Zhang,Shihan Ma,Yao Yao,Weiran Qi,Chuyan Jin,Guiyu Ma,Xingzhong Xu,Kai Yang,Ji-Rong Wen,Zhicheng Dou*

TL;DR: SearchOS 是一个系统级多智能体框架，通过将隐式的搜索进度显式化、持久化和共享化，解决信息搜寻中因交互历史增长导致的任务进展跟踪困难问题。它将开放域信息搜寻建模为带有实体引用的关联模式补全任务，利用 SOCM（搜索导向上下文管理）机制维护前沿任务、证据图、覆盖地图和失败记忆等外部状态，并通过流水线并行调度机制提升资源利用率与吞吐量。此外，系统引入搜索工具中间件套件，记录可验证证据并动态响应搜索停滞或预算耗尽，同时提供分层技能体系以避免重复失败模式。在 WideSearch 和 GISA 数据集上，SearchOS 在所有评估的单/多智能体基线上均表现最优，推动了鲁棒信息搜寻协作的发展。

Result: 在 WideSearch 和 GISA 基准测试中，SearchOS 在所有指标上均优于现有的单/多智能体基线系统，展现出更高的搜索效率、更强的鲁棒性以及更全面的信息覆盖能力，验证了其在复杂信息搜寻任务中的优越性能。

Abstract: Recent advances in Tool-Integrated Large Language Models have made web search a core capability of information-seeking agents. However, as interaction histories grow, agents increasingly struggle to track task progress. When search attempts fail to yield useful evidence, current single- and multi-agent systems can become trapped in repetitive loops, wasting search budgets and ultimately compromising the quality and completeness of the final output. We introduce SearchOS, a system-level multi-agent framework that turns fragile, implicit search progress into explicit, persistent, and shared state. First, we formulate open-domain information seeking as relational schema completion with grounded citations, where agents discover entities, populate attributes across linked tables, and anchor each value to source evidence. Then we design Search-Oriented Context Management (SOCM), which externalizes the evolving state into Frontier Task, an Evidence Graph, a Coverage Map, and Failure Memory. Built on SOCM, SearchOS applies a pipeline-parallel scheduling mechanism that overlaps the execution of sub-agents and continuously refills freed slots with tasks targeting unresolved coverage gaps to improve utilization and throughput. To schedule and control the execution of search agents, SearchOS introduces a Search Tool Middleware Harness that intercepts model and tool interactions to record grounded evidence and react to stalls or budget exhaustion, and provides a reusable hierarchical skill system comprising strategy and access skills to augment the agents' search process and avoid repeating failed search patterns across runs. On WideSearch and GISA, SearchOS leads all metrics among the evaluated single- and multi-agent baselines, paving the way toward robust information-seeking collaboration.

### [235] [Pretraining Data Can Be Poisoned through Computational Propaganda](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15267)
*Victoria Graf,Hannaneh Hajishirzi,Noah A. Smith,David Kohlbrenner,Kyle Lo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了在大规模网络爬取的预训练数据中通过公开讨论界面注入恶意内容的可能性，提出了一种名为HalfLife的新分析方法来评估对抗性内容在预训练数据中的渗透情况。研究证明，攻击者可通过开放的网页内容接口实现对语言模型预训练数据的污染，且这种攻击在真实世界的大规模、异构数据环境中是可行的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多局限于使用如维基百科等固定数据源进行污染攻击，但这些数据源无法代表实际预训练语料库的大规模和多样性。同时，以往工作忽略了污染数据与数据清洗流程之间的相互作用。因此，亟需探索更贴近现实环境下的污染攻击可行性及其检测方法。

Method: 利用公开讨论界面作为内容注入渠道，结合半衰期分析法（HalfLife）评估恶意内容在网页爬取与数据清洗后是否仍保留在最终训练数据中，从而验证大规模污染攻击的可行性。

Result: 研究证实，通过公共讨论接口可在大规模网络爬取的数据中成功注入恶意内容；HalfLife能够有效估计对抗性内容的留存率，表明第三方网页内容是潜在的语言模型预训练污染攻击路径。

Conclusion: 第三方网页内容，尤其是通过开放讨论接口引入的内容，可能成为攻击语言模型预训练过程的重要途径。为保障模型安全性，必须重视对预训练数据中潜在毒化内容的检测与评估，尤其是在复杂的数据采集与清洗流程下。

Abstract: Poisoning pretraining data can introduce harmful behaviors to LMs that are difficult to detect and mitigate. Prior work on poisoning pretraining data has largely exploited established data sources such as Wikipedia, which do not represent the large scale and heterogeneity typical of pretraining corpora, and has ignored the interaction between poisoned data and data curation pipelines. We demonstrate that poisoning attacks on pretraining data are feasible beyond this limited setting through an existing web-scale content injection mechanism: public discussion interfaces. Additionally, to measure whether malicious content is included after web crawling and data curation, we introduce HalfLife, a novel analysis for estimating adversarial content inclusion in web-crawl based LM training data. We use HalfLife to explore the feasibility of poisoning pretraining corpora at web scale through open discussion interfaces. Our analysis demonstrates the importance of estimating whether poison injections are included in pretraining data, and establishes third-party webpage content as a possible vector for attacking language model pretraining.

</details>

### [236] [Position: Explainability Research Must Prioritize Foundations over Ad-hoc Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14123)
*Michal Moshkovitz,Suraj Srinivas,Lesia Semenova,Nave Frost,Cyrus Rashtchian,Valentyn Boreiko,Shichang Zhang,Himabindu Lakkaraju,Cynthia Rudin,Jennifer Wortman Vaughan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，尽管可解释人工智能（XAI）技术层出不穷，但其在实际工作流程中极少产生影响，常被生成后即丢弃。根本问题在于缺乏将解释整合到端到端人机协作系统中的方法论。作者呼吁学界从零散的XAI方法转向解决基础性与结构性挑战，如问题定义不清、评估目标模糊及缺乏解释驱动反馈的流程。通过分析ICML、NeurIPS和ICLR论文并调研从业者，揭示了阻碍累积进步的共性问题，并提出一个实用检查清单，推动XAI向以人为本、行动导向的范式转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前XAI技术虽多样，但难以融入真实应用场景，解释无法引导有效行动，反映出研究在系统集成层面存在根本性缺陷，亟需从方法创新转向结构化问题解决。

Method: 通过文献分析（ICML、NeurIPS、ICLR）与对XAI实践者的调查，识别出限制XAI落地的核心障碍，进而提出一套用于指导可行动解释系统设计的检查清单。

Result: 发现现有研究普遍存在问题定义不明确、评估标准模糊、缺乏反馈机制等共性问题；提出可操作的检查清单以推动XAI向人类中心、可执行的方向演进。

Conclusion: XAI的发展应从追求新颖的解释方法转向构建清晰、可评估、支持反馈的系统架构，从而真正实现解释在实际决策中的作用。

Abstract: Despite the proliferation of Explainable AI (XAI) techniques -- from feature attributions to sparse autoencoders -- explanations rarely influence real-world workflows. In practice, they are often generated and discarded without guiding meaningful action. This gap reflects foundational shortcomings: research has not yet established methodologies for integrating explanations into end-to-end, human-in-the-loop systems. This position paper argues that the machine learning community must pivot from ad-hoc XAI methods toward addressing foundational & structural challenges, including unclear problem formulations, underspecified evaluation objectives, and the absence of pipelines for explanation-driven feedback. We support this claim through an analysis of recent ICML, NeurIPS, and ICLR papers and a survey of XAI practitioners, revealing recurring issues that limit cumulative progress. We conclude by outlining a practical checklist designed to shift XAI toward a more human-centered, action-oriented paradigm. By emphasizing foundational clarity over the development of ad-hoc methods, we hope to provide a roadmap for integrating explanations into actionable, feedback-driven AI systems.

</details>


### [237] [CARPRT: Class-Aware Zero-Shot Prompt Reweighting for Black-Box Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14125)
*Ruijiang Dong,Zesheng Ye,Jianzhong Qi,Lei Feng,Feng Liu,Gang Niu,Masashi Sugiyama*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为CARPRT的新型零样本提示重加权方法，通过在不依赖训练的情况下为每个类别学习特定的提示权重，以捕捉提示与类别之间的依赖关系。该方法利用预测属于某类别的图像在不同提示下的图文相关性得分平均值来量化提示对特定类别的相关性，并进行归一化得到类特定权重。实验表明，相较于传统的类无关重加权方法，CARPRT在多个标准图像分类基准上表现更优，证明建模提示-类别依赖关系对于提升零样本预测性能至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在零样本图像分类中使用统一的提示权重向量，假设所有提示与类别之间条件独立，但实际中某些提示（如"aerial view of"）可能仅适用于特定类别（如"airport"），而不适用于其他类别（如"apple"）。因此，需要一种能够捕捉提示与类别间依赖关系的方法，以提高分类准确性。

Method: 提出类感知的零样本提示重加权（CARPRT），其核心思想是为每个类别单独学习提示权重。具体地，对每个类别和每个可用提示，通过计算在该提示下被预测为该类别的图像的图文相关性得分的平均值，来估计提示对该类别的相关性；随后将这些估计值归一化，生成类特定的权重向量，实现训练自由的自适应提示加权。

Result: 在多个标准图像分类数据集上的实验结果表明，CARPRT显著优于现有的类无关提示重加权方法，验证了建模提示-类别依赖关系的有效性。该方法不仅提升了零样本分类性能，也对依赖提示集成的更广泛视觉语言模型应用具有积极意义。

Conclusion: CARPRT通过引入类感知的提示重加权机制，有效捕捉了提示与类别间的依赖关系，在无需额外训练的前提下显著提升了零样本图像分类性能，证明了在提示集成中考虑上下文相关性的必要性，为未来VLM应用提供了新的思路。

Abstract: Pre-trained vision-language models (VLMs) enable zero-shot image classification by computing the similarity score between an image and textual descriptions, typically formed by inserting a class label (e.g., "cat") into a prompt (e.g., "a photo of a"). Since the score for a given image-class pair is sensitive to the choice of prompt, existing studies ensemble multiple prompts using a weighting vector to aggregate scores across different prompts. Yet, in current strategies, the weighting vector assigned to each prompt is shared across all classes, implicitly assuming that prompts are conditionally independent of classes, which often does not hold in practice, as a prompt like "an aerial view of" might be apt for "airport" but ill-suited for "apple". To address this, we propose class-aware zero-shot prompt reweighting (CARPRT). This scoring scheme adjusts the weighting vector for each class label by capturing the class-specific relevance of different prompts in a training-free manner. For each class label and every available prompt, we quantify their class-specific relevance by averaging image-text relevance scores over images predicted to that class under the given prompt. These estimates are then normalized to derive class-specific weights. Evaluations on standard image classification benchmarks show that CARPRT outperforms existing class-independent reweighting methods, confirming that modeling prompt-class dependencies is crucial for effective zero-shot prediction and even broader VLM-based application settings that rely on prompt ensembling. Our code is available at https://github.com/tmlr-group/CARPRT.

</details>


### [238] [Explainable Geospatial AI for Satellite Ground Station Siting Using LiDAR-Derived Terrain Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14127)
*Shohini Sarkar,Smithi Mahendran,Rishi Chudasama,Varun Mannam,Arav Luthra,Yuvraj Rekhi,Vivek Nadig,Arsh Goenka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种可解释的全球部署机器学习框架，用于从开放地理空间数据预测代表性的杂波高度（RCH），以改进无线电传播和干扰分析。模型基于美国地质调查局3D高程计划的激光雷达标签训练，并使用全球土地覆盖、地形、人口、热力和光学遥感等数据作为推理特征。采用75%分位数统计定义RCH，选用LightGBM回归器，在测试中达到1.79米的平均绝对误差和0.765的R²，相比ITU基准减少超过60%的绝对误差。通过多种评估指标验证模型在射频规划中的适用性，包括米级误差、容差带准确性、高估与低估尾部表现、与ITU杂波高度分类的一致性以及基于SHAP的物理合理性。SHAP分析表明，树冠覆盖率、土地覆盖语义和光谱反射率是最重要的预测因子。通过分割特征、非森林消融实验及国际匹配验证，证明开放地理空间数据可在不牺牲可解释性和可部署性的情况下实现大规模杂波建模改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前无线电传播分析中普遍采用固定杂波高度值（如ITU-R P.452-18推荐），但该方法忽略了同一土地利用类别内部的高度差异，导致过保守的排除区域和低地球轨道地面站选址与频谱协调中的性能下降。因此需要更精确、动态且可解释的杂波高度预测方法。

Method: 提出一个基于机器学习的全球可部署框架，使用来自美国地质调查局3D高程计划的激光雷达数据作为标签，结合全球土地覆盖、地形、人口密度、热力与光学遥感数据作为输入特征。采用75%分位数定义代表性的杂波高度（RCH），比较多种回归器后选择LightGBM，因其在精度、效率和特征归因分析兼容性方面的优势。通过SHAP分析揭示关键影响因素，并进行多维度验证以评估模型在射频规划中的实用性。

Result: 模型在测试集上达到1.79米的平均绝对误差和0.765的决定系数（R²），相比ITU基准降低超过60%的绝对误差。在米级误差、容差带准确度、高低估分布、与现有标准一致性以及物理可解释性方面均表现优异。SHAP分析确认树冠覆盖、土地覆盖类型和光谱反射率为主要影响因素。国际验证和消融实验进一步证明模型在不同区域具有泛化能力且不依赖特定数据源。

Conclusion: 本研究展示了一种高效、可解释且可全球部署的杂波高度预测方法，显著优于传统固定参数方法。通过融合开放地理空间数据与先进机器学习技术，为射频规划、卫星通信站点选址及频谱管理提供了更精准、灵活的工具，同时保持了对物理意义的可解释性。

Abstract: Representative clutter height (RCH) is a key parameter in radio propagation and interference analysis because it captures the dominant height of local obstructions that drive terminal clutter loss. Current practice often relies on fixed clutter heights assigned to land use classes in Recommendation ITU-R P.452-18, but this misses within class variation and can lead to conservative exclusion zones and poor site ranking for low Earth orbit ground station siting and spectrum coordination. We present an interpretable, globally deployable machine learning framework for predicting RCH from open geospatial data. The model is trained using LiDAR derived labels from the U.S. Geological Survey 3D Elevation Program and inference time features from global land-cover, terrain, demographic, thermal, and optical remote sensing products. We define RCH using a robust 75th percentile clutter height statistic, evaluate multiple regressors, and select LightGBM for its accuracy, efficiency, and compatibility with feature attribution analysis. The final model achieves a mean absolute error of 1.79m and an R^2=0.765, reducing absolute error by more than 60% relative to the ITU baseline. Beyond aggregate fit, we evaluate domain facing criteria relevant to RF planning, including meter scale error, tolerance band accuracy, over and under estimation tails, agreement with ITU clutter height regimes, and SHAP-based physical plausibility. SHAP identifies tree canopy cover, land-cover semantics, and spectral reflectance as the most influential predictors. Studies on segmentation derived features, non-forest ablations, and land-cover matched international validation show that open geospatial data can improve clutter modeling at scale without sacrificing interpretability or deployability.

</details>


### [239] [Certified Domain Consistency for Multi-Domain Retrieval: Label-Free Per-Domain Contamination Control with Conformal Risk Guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14157)
*Jayakumar Manoharan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: C3R 是一种即插即用的控制层，通过推断的领域后验概率，在无需查询时标签的情况下，为每个领域设定可实现的污染预算，否则选择不输出以避免隐性违规。其核心是基于风险控制预测集的双分裂方案，具备可估量松弛的有限样本转移界，支持异质预算，并可逆用于部署。在千次重采样校准中，证书从未失效（稳定性结果），而边际控制在每次抽样中均违反最污染领域；软降序保留的召回率高于最强校准级联，且在相同认证污染水平下表现更优。该方法在多个开放测试平台（包括独立的联邦法规数据集）上复现成功，大模型判断的下游探测显示错误权威性来源随污染增加而上升，而在控制下下降。该层与冻结堆栈和重排序器无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当混合多领域语料库进行检索时，排名指标难以捕捉相关但错误领域的证据，而传统的合取风险控制边界仅能提供微弱覆盖，无法有效应对最恶劣领域的污染问题。因此需要一种能够对每个领域进行精确污染预算控制的方法，避免系统在高污染领域沉默失效或错误输出。

Method: 提出 C3R 控制层，采用基于风险控制预测集的双分裂机制，利用推断的领域后验概率构建有限样本转移边界，引入可估量的松弛项，支持不同领域的差异化预算分配，并可通过反向设计实现部署。通过受控模拟验证其总体有效性，确保在大量重采样中证书始终有效。

Result: 在上千次重采样中，证书未出现任何违反情况（表现出强稳定性），而传统边际控制在每轮中均突破最污染领域；软降序策略在保持相同认证污染水平时，比最强校准级联拥有更高的召回率。该方法在多个开放测试平台（包括公共联邦法规数据集）上成功复现，大模型评估显示错误权威性来源随污染上升，但在控制下显著下降。此外，该方法与冻结堆栈及重排序器无关，具有良好的通用性。

Conclusion: C3R 作为一种即插即用的控制层，能够在不依赖查询时标签的前提下，对多领域语料中的污染进行精准、可靠、可解释的控制，尤其在最难领域提供实质性的风险降低而非紧致边界，显著优于现有方法，具备广泛适用性和部署潜力。

Abstract: Retrieval over corpora that mix several domains often returns relevant but wrong-domain evidence that ranking metrics miss and that conformal risk control bounds only marginally, under-covering the worst domains. This work introduces C3R, a drop-in control layer that, from an inferred domain posterior and no query-time label, certifies a per-domain contamination budget where feasible and otherwise abstains rather than silently violating; on the hardest domains it guarantees a reduction, not a tight bound. The core is a two-split scheme built on risk-controlling prediction sets, whose finite-sample transfer bound crosses from the inferred to the true domain with fully estimable slack, supports heterogeneous budgets, and inverts for deployment. Population validity rests on this bound and a controlled simulation; across a thousand resampled calibrations the certificate never violates (a stability result) while marginal control violates the most-contaminated domain in every draw, and soft demotion retains more recall than the strongest calibrated cascade at equal certified contamination. The method replicates across open testbeds including an independent one from public federal regulations, and an LLM-judged downstream probe indicates wrong-authority grounding rises with contamination and falls under control. The layer is frozen-stack and reranker-agnostic.

</details>


### [240] [QFireNet: A Quantum-Enhanced U-Net for Wildfire Segmentation from Sentinel-2 Imagery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14160)
*Jaiman Munshi,Tanvi Tewary,Sawyer Bloom,Aidan Chu,Chetan Maviti,Kyon Winston-Bey,Harshit Badjatia,Farhan Kittur,Vardhan Madhavarapu,Varun Kota,Joshua Kwon,Nazia Rangwala-Vohra,Franz Klein*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种量子-混合方法，通过在U-Net的瓶颈部分引入变分量子电路（QuFeX和QB-Net），改进卫星图像中的野火检测。实验表明，在相同条件下，量子模型（QB-Net F1=31.18，QuFeX F1=30.79）优于经典U-Net基线（F1=28.71），且经典FPN表现接近（F1=31.13）。数据混合显著缓解了地理分布差异带来的域偏移，使FPN F1提升至39.76。跨数据集迁移验证了该架构的鲁棒性与泛化能力。结果表明量子机器学习在野火图像分割中具有潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 野火检测面临类别不平衡、特征复杂性和大气干扰等挑战，传统方法难以有效建模高维光谱特征空间，因此需要探索更高效的解决方案。

Method: 在经典U-Net的基础上，将变分量子电路（QuFeX和QB-Net）嵌入其瓶颈层，构建量子-混合模型；同时对比经典改进方案如FPN、参数压缩、替代损失函数及输入数据均匀混合。

Result: 量子模型（QB-Net和QuFeX）在标准条件下优于经典U-Net；数据混合显著提升经典FPN性能至F1=39.76；跨数据集迁移实验验证了模型的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 量子机器学习在野火图像分割任务中展现出潜在优势，值得进一步研究与拓展。

Abstract: Wildfire detection from satellite imagery is a semantic image segmentation problem that has proven to be difficult due to challenges such as class imbalance, feature complexity, and atmospheric interference. In this paper, we build on the foundational U-Net image segmentation model to develop a quantum-hybrid solution in hopes of more effectively modeling the high-dimensional spectral feature space of the Sen2Fire dataset. We inject a variational quantum circuit in the bottleneck portion of U-Net, specifically the QuFeX and QB-Net ansatzes. We test a classical Feature Pyramid Network (FPN) for further comparative analysis of the model, and we also explore classical improvements to the U-Net model and its training process, including a compression of parameters, alternative loss functions, and uniform mixing of input data. Our primary finding is that under matched conditions, both QB-Net (with an $F_1$ score of 31.18) and QuFeX ($F_1 = 30.79$) outperformed the classical U-Net baseline results ($F_1 = 28.71$). Additionally, the classical FPN achieved a comparable score of 31.13. A crucial finding was that data mixing removed a significant domain shift between the geographically-separated train and test sets, which boosted the classical FPN $F_1$ score to 39.76. We validate the architecture's robustness and generalizability to the wildfire detection problem via cross-dataset transfer on the California Burned Areas (CaBuAr) dataset. Overall, we find that quantum machine learning has potential to provide an advantage in the problem of wildfire image segmentation, and further experiments will continue to validate and expand upon this finding.

### [241] [Branching Policy Optimization: Sandbox-Native Language Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14171)
*Bowei He,Yankai Chen,Xiaokun Zhang,Xue Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为分支策略优化（BPO）的新强化学习算法，利用沙盒环境的确定性、可快照和可恢复特性，构建共享前缀的单棵多叉树而非独立轨迹，通过兄弟节点间的回报计算优势，显著降低方差并提升训练效率。在多个基准测试中，BPO在相同计算量下优于GRPO和RLOO，成功率提升3.6-6.1个百分点，梯度范数方差减半，且仅需38%的策略更新次数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL算法如PPO、RLOO、GRPO沿用RLHF的独立轨迹采样方式，忽视了代理沙盒具有确定性、可快照和可恢复的本质特性。该特性允许从任意中间状态恢复并共享路径信息，从而有望设计更高效的采样与优势估计机制。

Method: 提出分支策略优化（BPO），其核心包括：(i) 在高熵决策点自适应地对沙盒进行快照；(ii) 每个分支点分叉出K个替代动作并分别滚至终止；(iii) 使用兄弟节点的回报差计算每步优势，而非基于独立提示的轨迹基线。该方法通过共享前缀减少方差，并保证估计无偏。

Result: 在WebShop、ALFWorld和SWE-bench Verified任务上，使用Qwen2.5-7B和Llama-3.1-8B模型验证，BPO在相同计算成本下相比GRPO和RLOO提升成功率3.6–6.1个百分点；梯度范数方差减少一半；达到最佳性能仅需38%的策略更新次数。

Conclusion: BPO充分利用沙盒环境的确定性与可恢复性，通过构建共享前缀的分支树结构，实现更低方差、更高效率的优势估计，在多个复杂任务中表现出显著优越性，为大语言模型智能体的训练提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning has emerged as the dominant paradigm for training large language model (LLM) agents that interact with executable sandboxes. State-of-the-art algorithms such as PPO, RLOO, and GRPO inherit their rollout topology from RLHF: for each prompt, N independent trajectories are sampled from the initial state, and an advantage is computed by subtracting a group baseline. This design ignores a defining property of agent sandboxes. They are deterministic, snapshottable, and resumable from any intermediate state. We argue that this property enables a fundamentally different rollout topology: rather than N independent trees of depth T, one can construct a single tree of N leaves whose siblings share prefixes, and therefore share variance. We instantiate this idea as Branching Policy Optimization (BPO), a sandbox-native RL algorithm that (i) adaptively snapshots the sandbox at high-entropy decision points along a backbone trajectory, (ii) forks K alternative actions per branch point and rolls out each to termination, and (iii) computes per-step advantages from sibling returns rather than from independent prompts. We prove this estimator is unbiased and has strictly lower variance than the trajectory-level baseline, with the reduction equal to the prefix-explained portion of return variance. On WebShop, ALFWorld, and SWE-bench Verified with Qwen2.5-7B and Llama-3.1-8B backbones, BPO improves success by 3.6--6.1 absolute points over GRPO and RLOO at matched compute, halves gradient-norm variance, and matches the best baseline using 38% fewer policy updates.

</details>


### [242] [How Much of a 10-K Matters? Aggregation-Dependent Value of Full-Text versus Risk-Factor Sentiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14174)
*Sanggyu Sean Choi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究将监督词典学习方法扩展至10-K文件及其风险因素部分（Item 1A），在行业、投资组合和单个公司三个层级上，基于收益和波动率标签训练情感得分。分析涵盖94家纳斯达克100科技公司2006–2023年的1,383份文件，评估了12种情感指标在分类准确率、与实际市场结果的相关性以及词汇内容方面的表现。全文本在行业和投资组合层级上情感识别更准确，但在公司层级上，仅使用Item 1A部分效果更好，这归因于文档量与独立训练信号之间的交互作用。基准的Loughran-McDonald词典在所有层级均与股价呈强负相关，凸显了对监管披露文本采用监督方法的价值。研究结果及其设计启示为后续大规模多源系统的情感生成方法奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有金融情感提取主要依赖新闻文本和基于收益标签的监督学习，而10-K文件（尤其是其风险因素部分）作为风险披露的重要来源，尚未得到充分探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，通过引入更全面的监督学习框架，提升对监管文本中情感信息的捕捉能力，尤其关注波动率这一关键风险指标。

Method: 采用监督词典学习方法，对10-K文件全文及其中的Item 1A风险因素部分进行情感建模，在行业、投资组合和公司三个层级上，分别以股票收益和波动率为标签进行训练，生成十二种情感指标，并通过分类准确率、与实际市场结果的相关性及词汇内容分析进行评估。

Result: 全文本在行业和投资组合层级上情感预测更准确；但在公司层级，仅使用Item 1A部分表现更优，表明文档体量与训练信号的平衡至关重要。基准词典（Loughran-McDonald）在所有层级均与股价显著负相关，说明非监督方法在监管文本中存在偏差。研究验证了监督学习在该场景下的优越性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了在10-K文件中结合监督学习与多层次聚合策略的有效性，特别是在处理高噪声、低频的公司级风险披露时，聚焦关键段落（如Item 1A）可提升情感建模精度。研究结果为构建更大规模、多源融合的金融情感分析系统提供了方法论支持。

Abstract: Financial sentiment extraction has largely relied on news text and supervised extraction against return labels alone, leaving 10-K filings -- and volatility, the target risk disclosure is arguably best suited to informing -- comparatively unexplored. We extend a supervised lexicon-learning approach to 10-K filings and their Item 1A risk-factor sections, training sentiment scores against both return and volatility labels at three levels of aggregation: sector, portfolio, and individual firm. Across 1,383 filings from 94 Nasdaq-100 technology constituents (2006--2023), we evaluate the resulting twelve sentiment metrics on classification accuracy, correlation with realised market outcomes, and qualitative lexical content. Full-filing text produces more accurate sentiment at the sector and portfolio level for both targets, but this reverses at the individual-firm level, where the narrower Item 1A section performs better -- an effect we attribute to the interaction between document volume and the amount of independent training signal available at each level of aggregation. A Loughran-McDonald dictionary baseline is consistently, strongly negatively correlated with price at every level tested, underscoring the value of a supervised approach for regulatory disclosure text. These findings, and the design choices they motivate, establish the sentiment-generation methodology underlying a subsequent, larger-scale, multi-source system.

### [243] [Low-Latency Relay Selection in NR-V2X Vehicular Communications via Graph Isomorphism Networks with Edge Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14176)
*Giambattista Amati,Federica Mangiatordi,Emiliano Pallotti,Simone Angelini,Pierpaolo Salvo,Paola Vocca*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种面向C-V2X网络中实时中继选择的边感知学习优化框架，通过图同构网络（GINE）在单次前向传播中实现低延迟、高精度的中继激活决策。结合混合式GIN-剪枝MILP（GP-MILP）策略，在保持与精确MILP相同解质量的前提下，显著降低求解时间，满足NR-V2X严格时延要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在密集城市环境中，车辆到基础设施的直接通信易受快速信道变化和遮挡影响，导致链路中断；虽多跳中继可恢复覆盖，但受限于无线资源、容量和路由约束，中继选择成为NP难问题，传统基于混合整数线性规划（MILP）的方法计算复杂度高，难以满足实时性需求。因此亟需一种高效且准确的实时中继选择机制。

Method: 将每个V2X场景建模为有向图，节点特征表示车辆状态与交通需求，边特征反映无线链路容量；利用离线MILP生成最优中继配置作为监督信号，训练图同构网络（GINE）以实现边级中继激活预测；进一步提出混合式GIN-剪枝MILP（GP-MILP）策略，用GIN结果缩小MILP搜索空间，兼顾精度与效率。

Result: 实验基于OSM-SUMO-GEMV²生成的大规模数据集，结果显示：GIN在链路级决策上接近MILP性能（准确率0.9589，F1分数0.9544），端到端连通性提升达9.2%（4个RSU）至12%（2个RSU）；所有实例推理延迟均低于5ms；GP-MILP在超过98%的图实例中实现低于30ms的求解时间，且保持与MILP相同的最优目标值。

Conclusion: 所提出的边感知学习优化框架及混合式剪枝策略，实现了高精度、低延迟的实时中继选择，使高质量优化方案兼容5G NR-V2X的严苛时延要求，为未来智能交通系统中的可靠车联网通信提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Reliable, low-latency uplink connectivity is a key requirement for C-V2X networks in dense urban environments, where fast channel variations and blockages often degrade direct vehicle-to-infrastructure links. Multi-hop relaying can restore coverage, but relay-link activation under radio, capacity, and routing constraints results in an NP-hard optimisation problem, typically solved via Mixed-Integer Linear Programming (MILP), whose runtime scales poorly with graph size. This paper introduces an edge-aware Learning-to-Optimise framework for real-time relay selection. Each V2X snapshot is modelled as a directed graph: node features encode vehicle state and traffic demand, while edge features capture radio-link capacity. An offline MILP oracle generates optimal relay configurations that supervise a Graph Isomorphism Network with Edge Features (GINE), enabling edge-level relay activation through a single forward pass, with tightly bounded inference latency. To bridge learning and exact optimisation, we also propose a hybrid GINE-Pruned MILP (GP-MILP) strategy in which GINE predictions prune the MILP search space. Experiments on a large-scale dataset generated via an OSM-SUMO-GEMV$^2$ pipeline show that GINE closely matches MILP decisions at the link level (accuracy 0.9589), F1-score (0.9544) on validation) and yields consistent end-to-end connectivity gains over a 1-hop MILP baseline (up to 9.2% with four RSUs and 12% with two RSUs). Inference latency remains tightly bounded, with all evaluated instances completing within 5~ms. Moreover, GP-MILP preserves MILP-equivalent solutions (same objective value) while achieving solver runtimes below 30~ms for more than 98%) of the graph instances, making MILP-grade optimisation compatible with stringent NR-V2X latency budgets.

### [244] [RENEW: Towards Learning World Models and Repairing Model Exploitation from Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14180)
*Logan Mondal Bhamidipaty,Mykel Kochenderfer,Subramanian Ramamoorthy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于人类反馈的动态学习方法（DLHF），通过人类对想象轨迹的偏好来修复世界模型在离线强化学习中的模型利用问题。为提高样本效率，引入RENEW框架，利用认知不确定性聚焦于模型最易被利用的区域进行微调。实验表明，尽管直接使用DLHF需要大量偏好数据，但RENEW显著提升了效率，减少了灾难性遗忘并降低了模型利用风险，验证了人类偏好可直接监督世界模型动态，为解决离线模型强化学习中的利用问题提供了新思路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离线强化学习中的世界模型容易因数据覆盖不足而产生模型利用问题。传统方法依赖大量专家示范或保守算法，但前者成本高且难以获取，后者限制泛化能力。因此亟需一种高效、安全且能有效提升模型鲁棒性的新方法。

Method: 提出动态学习从人类反馈（DLHF），采用Bradley-Terry偏好损失对轨迹似然进行建模；进一步设计RENEW框架，利用认知不确定性指导微调过程，聚焦于模型最易被利用的区域，从而提升样本效率。

Result: 在Jumanji和经典控制环境中测试表明，虽然直接使用DLHF需要大量偏好数据，但RENEW显著提升了样本效率，减少了灾难性遗忘，并有效降低模型利用现象，使该方法具备实际应用潜力。

Conclusion: 本研究首次证明人类偏好可直接用于监督世界模型的动态行为，为解决离线模型强化学习中的模型利用问题提供了一种新颖且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: World models are widely used in offline reinforcement learning (RL) to improve sample efficiency and generate experience beyond a fixed dataset. However, they are vulnerable to model exploitation where data coverage is thin. Prior work addresses this either by collecting more expert demonstrations, which is often expensive, unsafe, or unavailable, or by conservative algorithms that avoid uncertain regions, which limits generalization. We propose instead to repair exploitation directly using human preferences over imagined rollouts, leveraging the strong intuitive physics that allows humans to easily spot egregious dynamics hallucinations. We formalize this as Dynamics Learning from Human Feedback (DLHF), a Bradley-Terry preference loss over trajectory log-likelihoods under a learned dynamics model. Unfortunately, naive DLHF is sample inefficient, so we introduce RENEW, which uses epistemic uncertainty to focus finetuning where the model is most exploitable. We evaluate on several Jumanji and classic control environments and find that while naive DLHF requires an outsize preference budget, RENEW makes the framework practical by improving sample efficiency, limiting catastrophic forgetting, and reducing exploitation in pretrained world models. Taken together, our results provide initial evidence that preferences can supervise world model dynamics directly, offering a new approach to addressing exploitation in offline model-based RL.

### [245] [Closed-Loop Knowledge Dynamics: An Operational Framework for Saturation and Escape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14185)
*Xuening Wu,Shan Yu,Shenqin Yin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究闭环知识系统在反复内部反馈下性能饱和的原因，并提出通过外部信息突破当前吸引子的机制。引入三层次操作框架，以结构参数θ控制知识状态演化，通过干预改变θ并检测其在探测状态上的核差异，实现可验证的结构性改变。基于李雅普诺夫漂移条件，证明稳定动态趋向有界稳定区域，瞬态衰减指数级，噪声决定残差底限。提出逃逸的度量条件：干预引发的吸引子位移与基准相对KL下界，确保逃逸概率上升。解释为何仅靠条件互信息无法保证逃逸——它衡量的是干预后更新的变化，而非偏离无干预分布。案例研究涵盖大模型代码修复、稀疏奖励强化学习和贝叶斯优化，使用匹配延续控制展示反馈强度与对齐度如何影响质量提升型逃逸。贡献在于建立稳定性工具、可观测干预效应与跨领域诊断之间的操作性联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 闭环系统在迭代改进中常因内部反馈导致性能饱和，难以突破当前状态吸引子。现有方法缺乏对结构性变化的可检验机制，且对逃逸行为的理论支撑不足，亟需一种能连接稳定性、干预可测性与跨域诊断的统一分析框架。

Method: 构建三层次操作框架，将知识状态 $x_t$ 的演化建模为由结构参数 $\theta$ 控制的转移核 $K_\theta$；定义观测等价类刻画系统结构；利用李雅普诺夫漂移分析稳定性；设计结构性干预以产生可检测的核差异；提出基于吸引子位移与相对KL下界的逃逸度量条件。

Result: 系统在稳定内部动态下趋近有界稳定区，瞬态指数衰减，残差受噪声控制；结构性干预可引发可测量的核差异，实现可验证的结构变化；逃逸概率可通过干预诱导的吸引子位移和基准相对KL下界进行量化评估；条件互信息不足以认证逃逸，因其仅反映干预后更新变异，非偏离原始分布。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了稳定性分析、可观测干预效应与跨领域诊断之间的操作性桥梁，为理解并突破闭环系统的性能瓶颈提供了理论工具与实践指导，适用于大模型、强化学习与优化等多场景。

Abstract: Feedback-driven loops support iterative improvement in large language models, reinforcement learning, and autonomous discovery, yet their gains often diminish under repeated internal feedback. We study why closed-loop knowledge systems saturate and what external information can move them beyond their current attractors. We introduce a three-level operational framework in which knowledge states $x_t$ evolve through transition kernels $K_θ$ indexed by a structural parameter $θ$. The governing structure is defined as the observational equivalence class of $θ$ induced by these kernels, while attractors and basins are properties of the fixed-$θ$ dynamics. A structural intervention changes $θ$ and produces a detectable kernel discrepancy on pre-specified probe states, making structural change falsifiable. Using a Lyapunov drift condition, we show that stable internal dynamics approach bounded stability regions with exponentially attenuated transients and a noise-controlled residual floor. We characterize escape through a metric condition on intervention-induced attractor displacement and a baseline-relative KL lower bound for increasing escape probability. This analysis also explains why conditional mutual information alone cannot certify escape: it measures variation among intervention-conditioned updates rather than departure from the no-intervention law. Case studies in LLM code repair, sparse-reward reinforcement learning, and Bayesian optimization use matched continuation controls to illustrate how feedback strength and alignment affect quality-improving escape. Our contribution is an operational connection among stability tools, measurable intervention effects, and cross-domain diagnostics.

### [247] [TEDDY: A Pediatric Foundation Model for Risk Forewarning from ICD-Coded Diagnostic Histories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14191)
*Matthew Brady Neeley,Jorge Botas,Johnathan Jia,Lin Yao,Daniel Palacios,Benjamin Choi,Zhandong Liu,Hyun-Hwan Jeong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TEDDY 是一个针对儿童电子健康记录的 184 万参数解码器变压器，基于 160 万儿童的约 7300 万条 ICD-10 诊断数据训练，能够建模纵向诊断轨迹和就诊时间。在 797 个疾病初发预测任务中，中位 AUC 达 72.0%，显著优于多种传统模型（如 DenseNet、CNN、RNN、LSTM），且在罕见病、跨性别与年龄群体中表现稳健。预测信号可在首次诊断前两年被检测到，且在哮喘和多动症等关键疾病上性能远超现有模型，包括更大规模的语言模型。就诊时间预测误差为 3.0 天，但长期返回间隔仍存在校准问题。研究证明，儿科诊断历史可作为小型生成模型的基础，支持广泛、罕见病及长周期风险预测，无需大规模数据或数十亿参数模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索儿童电子健康记录中蕴含的发展性临床轨迹潜力，构建高效、紧凑的生成式医疗基础模型，以实现对罕见病、长期疾病风险的精准预测，同时避免依赖海量数据或超大参数模型。

Method: 使用解码器变压器架构（TEDDY）训练，基于单机构 160 万儿童的 7300 万条 ICD-10 诊断记录，建模纵向诊断事件序列与就诊时间；采用前瞻性预测策略，仅基于首次发生事件进行评估，并与性别和年龄匹配的对照组比较。通过多任务学习覆盖 16 个 ICD-10 章节的 797 项疾病初发预测任务，评估不同模型在各类条件下的表现。

Result: TEDDY 在 797 项任务中实现中位 AUC 72.0%，显著优于所有对比模型（如 DenseNet: 50.0%, CNN: 57.2%, RNN: 60.1%, LSTM: 62.7%），且在 96–99% 的任务中表现更优；罕见病中 90% 的最稀有病症的置信区间高于随机水平；预测信号可在首次诊断前两年被捕捉，中位 AUC 分别为 59.7%（整体分析）和 64.4%（固定队列敏感性分析）；在哮喘和注意缺陷多动障碍中，AUC 分别达 79.3% 和 84.7%，大幅领先于现有最强模型；就诊时间预测平均绝对误差为 3.0 天，但长期返回间隔存在偏差。

Conclusion: 儿科诊断历史具备作为生成式医疗基础模型训练数据的潜力，即使使用小规模参数模型（184 万参数），也能实现对广泛疾病、罕见病及长周期风险的高精度预测，无需依赖大规模数据集或百亿级参数模型，为个性化、前瞻性儿童健康管理提供新范式。

Abstract: Pediatric electronic health records capture developmentally structured clinical trajectories, yet their potential for generative healthcare foundation models remains largely unexplored. Here we present TEDDY (Temporal Event Decoder for Disease in Youth), a 1.84-million-parameter decoder transformer trained on approximately 73 million ICD-10 diagnoses from 1.6 million children at a single pediatric institution. TEDDY models longitudinal diagnosis trajectories and visit timing. Predictions were made before visit codes were revealed, limited to first occurrences, and evaluated against sex- and age-matched controls. Across 797 disease-onset prediction tasks spanning 16 ICD-10 chapters, TEDDY achieved a median AUC of 72.0%, outperforming same-data DenseNet (50.0%), CNN (57.2%), RNN (60.1%), and LSTM (62.7%) baselines on 96-99% of tasks. Performance held across sex and age and was strongest among lower-prevalence diagnoses; 202 of the 225 rarest conditions (90%) had 95% confidence intervals above chance. Predictive signal remained detectable more than two years before first recorded diagnosis, with median AUCs of 59.7% in the unrestricted analysis and 64.4% in a fixed-cohort sensitivity analysis. In asthma and attention-deficit/hyperactivity disorder benchmarks, AUCs were 79.3% and 84.7%, compared with 62.7% and 71.7% for the strongest comparators, including a general-purpose language model three orders of magnitude larger. Visit-timing predictions had a 3.0-day mean absolute restricted mean survival-time error over 365 days, although median and long-tail return intervals remained miscalibrated. Together, these results establish pediatric diagnostic histories as a substrate for compact generative models supporting broad, rare-disease, and long-horizon risk forecasting without population-scale data or billion-parameter models.

</details>


### [248] [Long-term User Engagement Optimization through Model-agnostic Downstream Rewards Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14192)
*Dingsu Wang,Filip Ryzner,Kelly He,Armando Ordorica,David Woo,Aditya Mantha,Liyao Lu,Usha Amrutha Nookala,Haoran Guo,Jiacong He,Olafur Gudmundsson,Matt Chun,Krystal Benitez,Dhruvil Deven Badani,Yijie Dylan Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接优化用户留存困难，因为回报信号稀疏、延迟且难以归因于早期推荐；现有方法如序列建模和强化学习需特定任务奖励设计、计算开销大，难以泛化。

Method: 提出一种离线筛选框架，识别早期可观测且对未来留存具有预测性的会话级行为；基于多源用户行为模式构建模型无关的下游奖励信号；讨论工程化部署挑战并集成到排名模型中。

Conclusion: 所提出的统一、模型无关的下游奖励框架有效解决了长期用户价值优化难题，具备良好的可扩展性和通用性，已在实际生产环境中取得显著成效。

Abstract: As recommender systems mature in the past few years, their optimization objectives have evolved from a primary focusing on short-term behavioral signals to a broader emphasis on long-term user engagement and retention. However, directly optimizing retention is difficult because return signals are sparse, delayed, and only partially attributable to earlier recommendations. Prior work has addressed this challenge with sequential modeling and reinforcement learning, but these approaches typically require task specific reward engineering, substantial computational overhead, and surface specific implementations that are difficult to generalize. In this paper, we present a unified, model-agnostic downstream reward framework for optimizing long-term user value in large-scale recommendation systems. First, we formulate the downstream reward learning problem and develop an offline screening framework to identify session level behaviors that are both observable early and predictive of future retention. We then propose several model-agnostic downstream rewards signals derived from observed user action patterns across multiple sources. We further discuss the engineering effort to productionize the proposed rewards derivations and challenges we faced when adding them to our ranking models. Online A/B experiments demonstrate consistent improvements in engagement and retention-related metrics, and the framework has been deployed across multiple Pinterest surfaces, including Homefeed, Related Pins, Search, and Notifications.

### [249] [Augmentations for Robust and Efficient Imitation Learning in Streamed Video Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14200)
*Somjit Nath,Abdelhak Lemkhenter,Pallavi Choudhury,Chris Lovett,Katja Hofmann,Sergio Valcarcel Macua,Lukas Schäfer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对流媒体环境下视觉伪影的时空增强方法，以提升模仿学习在复杂3D游戏环境中的鲁棒性。通过模拟低带宽网络下的四种常见视觉问题（像素块、擦除、全局模糊和鬼影），结合预测逆动力学模型（PIDM），在三个现代3D游戏中验证了该方法的有效性。结果表明，在稳定流媒体条件下，使用增强训练的智能体性能提升高达41%；在网络延迟下，性能下降仅7.45%，远优于未使用增强的智能体（下降49.82%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模仿学习依赖人类示范数据，但此类数据昂贵且难以获取。此外，现代游戏常通过流媒体进行，网络延迟与压缩会引入时空相关的视觉伪影，导致测试时分布偏移，影响智能体性能。因此需要一种能应对这些现实挑战的训练策略。

Method: 提出基于流媒体特性的时空增强方法，模拟低带宽网络下的四种典型视觉伪影：像素块与擦除、全局模糊、鬼影。将该增强应用于预测逆动力学模型（PIDM），利用未来状态条件与逆动力学策略在潜在空间中联合建模，从而提升模型对视觉扰动的鲁棒性。

Result: 在三种现代3D游戏任务中，使用时空增强训练的智能体在稳定流媒体条件下性能最高提升41%；在引入网络延迟时，性能仅下降7.45%，而基准模型下降达49.82%，显著优于无增强训练的模型。

Conclusion: 面向流媒体场景设计的时空增强是一种简单但高效的手段，可显著提升游戏智能体在复杂3D环境中的鲁棒性与效率，适用于真实部署场景。

Abstract: Imitation learning is an appealing way to scale game-playing agents to complex 3D environments by training policies to map visual observations to actions from human demonstrations. However, these demonstrations are expensive to collect and modern game-playing is often done through streaming in which network delay and compression introduce spatiotemporally correlated visual artifacts that can cause a covariance shift at test time. To address these challenges, we propose streaming augmentations that mimic four types of artifacts commonly encountered during streaming with low-bandwidth network connection: pixelated blocks and scrubs, global blur, and ghosting. We instantiate our approach on top of predictive inverse dynamics models (PIDM), which combine future-state conditioning with an inverse dynamics policy in a learned latent space, and evaluate the impact of our augmentations across three tasks in modern 3D video games. Under stable streaming conditions, agents trained with spatiotemporal augmentations achieve up to 41% higher evaluation performance compared to agents trained without augmentations under an identical data budget. When network lag is introduced, agents trained with augmentations degrade by only 7.45% vs 49.82% of the original performance for agents trained only with the original data. These results clearly indicate that spatiotemporal augmentations tailored for the streaming setting are a simple yet powerful tool to train robust and efficient game-playing agents.
