This study develops a flow matching-based topology optimisation (FMTO) framework for conditional topology generation. Linear FMTO is first formulated as an endpoint-based baseline by interpolating between a Gaussian source field and the BESO reference topology. To introduce mechanically meaningful intermediate states, a trajectory-aware FMTO formulation is proposed, where volume-fraction-indexed BESO states are used to construct the probability path and target velocity field. This incorporates physics-guided optimisation history into generative flow learning without adding inference-time optimisation. A path--velocity mismatch analysis explains why moderate trajectory weighting can improve generation stability, whereas excessive guidance may over-constrain the learned transport. Numerical examples show that FMTO generates diverse topology candidates with improved compliance-related performance, volume-fraction satisfaction, topology fidelity, and substantially fewer sampling steps than a diffusion-based baseline. Under limited training data, trajectory-aware FMTO achieves the best overall performance with a moderate trajectory weight. Studies on trajectory-anchor density and three-dimensional topology generation further demonstrate the influence of path design and the applicability of the proposed framework beyond two-dimensional problems.

*Yusuke Sakemi,Tomoya Takeuchi,Takeo Hosomi,Kazuyuki Aihara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于可微分尖峰时间离散化（DSTD）的内存高效训练框架，用于脉冲神经网络（SNN），显著降低训练时的内存消耗并加速训练过程。该方法通过将不规则的前突触尖峰映射到固定时间点的可微加权事件，将输入依赖的候选维度从 $O(N_{\mathrm{out}}N_{\mathrm{in}})$ 降低至 $O(N_{\mathrm{out}}M)$，同时结合受同步链启发的时间正则化，实现层间发放窗口组织与管道式处理。在密集型LIF层中，峰值内存使用减少约100倍，训练时间缩短约20倍，成功实现了在单个GPU上训练9层CIFAR-10和20层Fashion-MNIST的卷积SNN。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有连续时间脉冲神经网络（SNN）在深度训练时面临严重的内存瓶颈，主要源于精确尖峰时间计算需要存储和评估由前突触尖峰顺序决定的时间区间内所有候选放电时间，导致激活内存随神经元数量呈二次增长。为解决这一问题，亟需一种既能保持高精度又能大幅降低内存占用的训练方法。

Method: 提出可微分尖峰时间离散化（DSTD）方法，将不规则的前突触尖峰映射为在固定时间点上的可微加权事件，从而将动态的候选时间维度替换为固定的 $M$ 个时间间隔；同时引入受同步链启发的时序正则化机制，引导层间放电窗口有序分布，防止神经元失效，并支持流水线式处理。

Result: 在密集型漏积分-放电（LIF）层中，相较于精确尖峰时间计算，DSTD将峰值内存消耗降低约100倍，训练时间减少约20倍；成功在单个GPU上训练出9层卷积SNN（CIFAR-10）和20层卷积SNN（Fashion-MNIST），验证了方法的高效性与可扩展性。

Conclusion: 所提出的DSTD与时间正则化联合框架，有效解决了深度连续时间SNN训练中的内存与效率瓶颈，使大规模、深层脉冲神经网络在资源受限设备上实现高效训练成为可能，为类脑计算和神经形态硬件应用提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Continuous-time spiking neural networks (SNNs) provide an event-driven framework for temporal computation, computational neuroscience, and neuromorphic hardware. However, training deep continuous-time SNNs is severely constrained by the memory required for exact spike-time computation, which evaluates and retains candidate firing times over intervals determined by presynaptic spike ordering. Here we introduce a memory-efficient training framework based on differentiable spike-time discretization (DSTD) for leaky integrate-and-fire neurons with general membrane and synaptic time constants. DSTD maps irregular presynaptic spikes onto differentiable weighted events at fixed time points, replacing the input-dependent candidate dimension with $M$ fixed time intervals while accurately approximating continuous-time membrane-potential dynamics. This reduces candidate-related activation memory from $O(N_{\mathrm{out}}N_{\mathrm{in}})$ to $O(N_{\mathrm{out}}M)$ in the case of time-to-first-spike (TTFS) coding, where $N_{\mathrm{in}}$ and $N_{\mathrm{out}}$ denote the numbers of presynaptic and postsynaptic neurons, respectively. We further introduce synfire-chain-inspired temporal regularization that organizes layer-wise firing windows, mitigates dead-neuron failures, and enables pipeline-like processing. In dense LIF layers, DSTD reduced peak memory consumption by up to approximately 100-fold and training time by up to approximately 20-fold compared with exact spike-time computation. Together, these methods allowed us to train 9-layer convolutional SNNs on CIFAR-10 and 20-layer convolutional SNNs on Fashion-MNIST on a single GPU.

</details>


### [287] [Grad2Fair: A Gradient-driven Approach for Graph Fairness without Demographics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14705)
*Yuchang Zhu,Zezhong Xie,Huizhe Zhang,Huazhen Zhong,Jintang Li,Liang Chen,Zibin Zheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究图神经网络在缺乏敏感属性信息情况下的群体公平性问题，提出GradDist度量方法通过分析误分类节点的梯度分布来捕捉潜在的偏见，并进一步提出Grad2Fair方法，利用梯度指导实现无人口统计学信息的公平性优化，避免依赖不准确的预测属性。实验表明该方法在多个真实数据集上优于现有基线，具有稳定且优异的公平性表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图神经网络公平性方法通常假设敏感属性（如性别、种族）完全可得，但现实中这一条件难以满足。尽管已有研究尝试用预测的敏感属性作为代理，但其准确性不足会导致公平性改进失败。因此需要一种无需依赖敏感属性或其预测值的方法来实现公平性。

Method: 提出GradDist：基于梯度分布中局部模式间距离的度量方法，用于量化群体偏见；提出Grad2Fair：一种基于梯度引导的无敏感属性公平性优化方法，直接利用梯度信息进行去偏，避免对敏感属性预测的依赖。

Result: 在多个真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，Grad2Fair在大多数情况下均显著优于现有基线方法，在提升模型公平性方面表现更优且更加稳定。

Conclusion: 本文证明了梯度分布中隐含着与敏感属性相关的偏见信息，提出的方法无需依赖敏感属性或其预测值即可有效提升图神经网络的群体公平性，为实际应用中缺乏敏感属性信息的场景提供了可行解决方案。

Abstract: Graph neural networks (GNNs) frequently encounter group fairness issues, often yielding biased predictions against specific demographic groups defined by sensitive attributes such as gender or race. While this challenge has motivated extensive research, most existing solutions rely on the strong assumption that demographics are fully available. To bypass this strict requirement, a few recent studies have attempted to use predicted demographics as proxies to enforce fairness constraints. However, predicted demographics may be inaccurate, resulting in the failure to improve fairness. In this work, we investigate the problem of graph fairness without demographic information and avoid the utilization of predicted demographics. Motivated by our observation that the gradient distributions of misclassified nodes implicitly encode demographic information, we first propose GradDist, a gradient-based metric that quantifies bias by measuring the distance between local modes within these distributions. To mitigate this bias, we propose Gradient-to-Fairness (Grad2Fair), a gradient-guided approach for group fairness without demographics. Due to the potential demographics in gradients, Grad2Fair directly leverages gradients to debias and eliminates demographic prediction, thereby enabling stable fairness performance. Experiments on several real-world datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of Grad2Fair, as evidenced by superior performance over baselines in most cases. Our code is available at https://github.com/ZzoomD/Grad2Fair.

</details>


### [288] [MESHA: Mechanism-Enforced Sequential Halving for Strategic Linear Bandits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14706)
*Xin Li,Zixin Zhong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MESHA 是一种用于策略线性多臂老虎机中最佳臂识别（BAI）的算法，通过结合均匀采样和基于周期的格里姆触发条件（GTC），有效应对各臂可能故意误报特征以提高被识别为最优臂的概率。该方法在任意纳什均衡下保证了最优臂有动机通过GTC检查，并提供了在固定预算下的失败概率上界。实验表明，依赖最优设计（OD）的现有算法在策略环境中会因最优臂被“饿死”而失效，而MESHA显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在策略线性多臂老虎机中，各臂可能故意报告虚假特征以增加被识别为最佳臂的概率，传统基于最优设计（OD）的算法在此类环境中易受欺骗，导致最优臂得不到足够采样，从而失效。因此需要设计一种对策略行为鲁棒的算法。

Method: MESHA 结合了朴素均匀采样规则与周期性的格里姆触发条件（GTC）：均匀采样降低策略行为的影响，而GTC用于剔除那些报告特征严重偏离真实值的臂，从而确保只有可信的臂能继续参与。算法在纳什均衡框架下分析，证明最优臂有动机通过检验，且可控制失败概率。

Result: 理论分析表明，任何策略性臂都会试图通过GTC检查以最大化被识别概率；在固定预算下，MESHA的失败概率具有上界。数值实验显示，相比依赖OD采样的基线和特征无关的基线，MESHA在性能上显著更优，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: MESHA 通过结合均匀采样与格里姆触发机制，有效抵御了策略性误导，在战略环境下实现了对最佳臂的可靠识别，是当前线性BAI算法在对抗策略行为方面的显著改进。

Abstract: We design and analyze \underline{M}echanism-\underline{E}nforced \underline{S}equential \underline{HA}lving (MESHA), an algorithm for Best Arm Identification (BAI) in strategic linear bandits. In this setting, each arm may strategically misreport its feature vector to maximize the probability of being identified as the best arm, when rewards are generated from the arms' true but unobservable features. The design of MESHA applies the naïve uniform sampling rule and an epoch-wise Grim Trigger Condition (GTC): the former reduces the impact of arms' strategic behaviours and the latter eliminates arms whose reported features severely deviate from the ground truth. Considering an arbitrary Nash Equilibrium, we prove that any arm would attempt to pass the GTC check to maximize its identified probability and derive an upper bound on the failure probability of MESHA within a fixed budget $T$. We also show that state-of-the-art linear BAI algorithms with $G$-optimal design would fail in such strategic environment, as the optimal design (OD)-based sampling rule based on strategically reported features may {\it starve} the optimal arm of any sampling budget. Finally, extensive numerical experiments indicate that MESHA
  outperforms baselines that rely on OD-based sampling rules as well as the feature-agnostic baselines, corroborating the efficacy of MESHA.

</details>


### [289] [Counterfactuals for Feature-Weighted Clustering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14719)
*Richard J. Fawley,Renato Cordeiro de Amorim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VoICE 是一种用于加权 k-均值聚类的反事实解释框架，通过将反事实生成建模为投影到目标簇的加权 Voronoi 区域，结合特征权重，实现低成本、简洁且可操作的解释。该方法通过数据导出的边界约束和向心收缩，减少外推和边界敏感性，在多个基准数据集上均有效保证目标簇成员资格，优于现有的成对基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在聚类任务中，由于簇标签未定义且依赖于几何划分，反事实解释难以直接应用。现有方法通常基于跨越单个中心点边界来改变簇分配，但这种方式不充分反映聚类结构，且缺乏对特征权重和可操作性的考虑。因此需要一种更准确、可解释且符合实际约束的反事实生成机制。

Method: VoICE 框架通过构建加权 Voronoi 区域，将反事实生成问题转化为投影到目标簇的完整加权区域。特征权重被嵌入聚类过程与反事实优化目标中，确保解释在几何上合理且成本最低。同时，目标区域与数据导出的边界相交，并进行同向收缩以降低外推风险和边界敏感性。

Result: VoICE 在多个基准数据集上始终能生成有效的目标簇成员反事实解释，而领先的成对基线方法则无法保证这一点。结果表明，该方法在保持解释有效性的同时，提升了可操作性和稳定性。

Conclusion: VoICE 为加权 k-均值聚类提供了一种稳健、可解释的反事实解释框架，通过整合几何结构、特征权重与实际约束，显著优于传统方法，具有良好的泛化能力与实用性。

Abstract: Counterfactual explanations provide local, interpretable insight by identifying changes to an input that would alter its assigned outcome. Although well established in supervised learning, their extension to clustering is less direct, since cluster assignments are unlabeled and governed by the geometry of the partition. This paper introduces VoICE, a Voronoi-Induced Counterfactual Explainability framework for feature-weighted $k$-means clustering. Rather than treating cluster change as a crossing of a single pairwise centroid boundary, VoICE formulates counterfactual generation as projection onto the full weighted Voronoi region of a target cluster, incorporating feature weights directly into both the clustering geometry and the counterfactual objective to yield least-cost and parsimonious explanations under actionability constraints. Target regions are further intersected with data-derived bounds and homothetically contracted towards their centroids, limiting extrapolation and boundary sensitivity. VoICE consistently produces valid target-cluster membership, across several benchmark datasets, where the leading pairwise baseline does not.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于有界二阶异质性假设，通过分析局部更新对全局收敛的影响，推导出更优的收敛上界，并构造新的下界以验证其紧致性。此外，将技术延伸至串行SGD场景，分析稀有高曲率客户端的影响。

Conclusion: 本工作为Local SGD提供了更精细、更坚实的理论基础，深化了对局部更新优势的理解，并揭示了二阶异质性在刻画客户端差异中的核心作用。

Abstract: Local SGD, also known as Federated Averaging, is a widely used distributed optimization algorithm. Although Local SGD often outperforms alternatives such as Mini-batch SGD in practice, theory still only partially explains when and why local updates help under realistic data heterogeneity. Recent work by [Patel et al., 2025] shows that a bounded second-order heterogeneity assumption captures the efficiency of Local SGD for strongly convex objectives, and conjectures that the same principle extends to the general convex setting. In this paper, we prove this conjecture by establishing an improved convergence guarantee for Local SGD on general convex objectives under bounded second-order heterogeneity. We also improve the best-known lower bounds for Local SGD in this setting, showing that our upper bounds are nearly tight. Together, these results provide a sharper, more fine-grained convergence theory for Local SGD. As a further application of our techniques, we provide a lower bound for serial SGD with replacement, showing how second-order heterogeneity captures the impact of rare high-curvature clients.

### [291] [GAttNHP: Group Attention Neural Hawkes Process for Extrapolation Reasoning in Temporal Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14733)
*Xiangni Tian,Kaixian Yu,Runpeng Dai,Niansheng Tang,Hongtu Zhu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GAttNHP提出一种统一框架，解决时间知识图谱（TKG）中长期时间依赖、链间相互作用和重尾到达时间带来的预测挑战。通过自注意力编码器捕捉历史影响，语义软分组模块实现跨链激发模式共享，非交叉分位数回归头提供稳定的时间预测，显著提升长尾事件链的预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以处理时间知识图谱中的长期依赖、链间复杂交互以及重尾分布导致的时间预测不准确问题。

Method: 提出Group Attention Neural Hawkes Process (GAttNHP)，包含自注意力编码器、语义软分组模块和非交叉分位数回归头，分别应对历史依赖、跨链交互和时间分布特性。

Result: 在六个基准数据集上优于现有最先进模型，在实体预测和时间预测任务中均有提升，尤其在长尾事件链上表现显著改善。

Conclusion: GAttNHP通过三个组件的协同设计，有效解决了时间知识图谱预测中的核心挑战，尤其在复杂、稀疏的事件序列中展现出强大鲁棒性与泛化能力。

Abstract: Temporal Knowledge Graphs (TKGs) record how facts evolve over time, but forecasting future events on a TKG remains difficult for three reasons: (i) long-range temporal dependencies are hard to encode; (ii) events on different chains mutually excite or inhibit one another in ways that snapshot-level models cannot express; and (iii) inter-arrival times are heavy-tailed and statistically sparse, so deterministic time predictors are unreliable. We address these three issues with a single framework, the \textbf{Group Attention Neural Hawkes Process (GAttNHP)}, built around three matched components. First, a self-attention encoder casts each subject--relation chain as a continuous-time point process and captures the lingering excitation of distant history. Second, a semantic soft-grouping module turns globally learnable Hawkes priors into an analytical cross-attention mask, so chains share excitation patterns through their latent group memberships rather than through exhaustive pairwise computation. Third, a Non-Crossing Quantile (NCQ) regression head replaces mean-based time prediction, providing calibrated, monotonically ordered quantile estimates that remain stable under heavy-tailed inter-arrival distributions. On six benchmark TKG datasets, GAttNHP improves over state-of-the-art baselines on both entity prediction and time prediction, and ablations confirm that its largest gains arise on the long-tail event chains where existing models fail most severely.

### [292] [ChronoQG: Towards a Temporally Expressive and Hop-Bounded Benchmark for Temporal Knowledge Graph Question Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14770)
*Xuemeng Liu,Zhengpin Li,Wanpeng Tang,Haotong Xie,Wentao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出ChronoQG，首个面向时序知识图谱问答生成（TKGQG）的表达性强且受跳数限制的基准构建框架，旨在生成符合支持子图与回答确定性时序约束的自然语言问题。该框架整合了全面的时序约束分类体系、拓扑-时序子图采样和基于轨迹的问题生成方法，从异构时序知识图谱中构建了四个总计16,011个经验证的问题数据集。实验评估了多种基于大模型的KGQG方法和提示基线在不同TKGQG场景下的表现，结果显示现有方法在多约束设置和复杂时序约束类型下难以保持时序一致性，揭示了静态KGQG与TKGQG之间的显著差距，并确立ChronoQG为一个具有挑战性的时序忠实问答生成测试平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识图谱问答生成（KGQG）基准主要基于静态知识图谱，未编码事实的时间范围，无法评估生成问题是否忠实于时间有效性、事件顺序及决定答案的时序约束。因此，亟需一个能体现时序一致性的新任务与评估框架。

Method: 提出ChronoQG框架，包含：1）全面的时序约束分类体系；2）拓扑-时序子图采样策略；3）基于轨迹的问答生成机制，以确保生成问题在语义与时间维度上均忠实于原始图结构。

Result: ChronoQG成功构建了四个来自异构时序知识图谱的数据集，共包含16,011个经过验证的问题；实验表明，现有大模型方法在多时序约束和复杂约束类型下表现不佳，难以维持时序一致性。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了静态KGQG与真正时序感知的TKGQG之间存在的显著差距，证明了构建时序忠实问答生成基准的重要性，而ChronoQG作为首个此类框架，为未来研究提供了强有力的挑战性测试平台。

Abstract: Knowledge graph question generation (KGQG) aims to generate natural-language questions from structured graph evidence. Existing KGQG benchmarks, however, are mostly built on static knowledge graphs and do not encode the temporal scopes of graph facts. As a result, they cannot evaluate whether generated questions faithfully preserve temporal validity, event ordering, and answer-determining temporal constraints. In this paper, we study temporal knowledge graph question generation (TKGQG), where a generated question must be faithful to both the support subgraph and the temporal constraints required to identify the target answer. We propose ChronoQG, the first temporally expressive and hop-bounded benchmark construction framework for TKGQG. ChronoQG integrates a comprehensive temporal-constraint taxonomy, topology-temporal subgraph sampling, and trace-grounded question generation to construct temporally faithful questions. The framework produces four benchmark datasets from heterogeneous temporal knowledge graphs, totaling 16,011 verified questions. We evaluate representative LLM-based KGQG methods and prompting baselines across diverse TKGQG settings, including temporal-constraint counts, topological templates, and temporal-constraint types. The results show that existing methods struggle to preserve temporal constraints, especially under multi-constraint settings and harder temporal-constraint types. These findings reveal a clear gap between static KGQG and TKGQG, and establish ChronoQG as a challenging testbed for temporally faithful question generation.

### [293] [Evaluating Epistemic Uncertainty: Beyond OOD Detection and Active Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14817)
*Jakub Paplhám,Willem Waegeman,Eyke Hüllermeier,Vojtěch Franc*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于后悔（regret）的贝叶斯最优不确定性评估框架，将选择性预测建模为覆盖、期望风险与后悔之间的约束优化问题，证明最优选择器是真实随机与认知不确定性的阈值凸组合。该理论揭示了现有不确定性解耦方法中相关性度量的局限性，并建议以可实现风险、后悔和覆盖表面作为联合解耦与实用性的诊断工具。实证结果显示，基于决策论的排序与代理任务排序存在显著差异，甚至出现方法间排名反转现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估认知不确定性依赖于分布外检测和主动学习等任务，但这些任务的贝叶斯最优策略与常用不确定性评分不一致，导致评估标准失真。需要一种更符合实际决策目标的评估范式。

Method: 基于认知拒绝选项框架，将选择性预测形式化为覆盖、期望风险与后悔的约束优化问题，推导出最优选择器为真实随机与认知不确定性阈值凸组合的形式。提出以可实现风险、后悔与覆盖表面作为解耦方法的诊断指标。

Result: 理论证明了最优选择器结构；实验表明标准相关性度量不能可靠预测不确定性组件的实际效用；基于决策论的评估结果与传统代理任务排名存在显著分歧，包括方法间的排名反转。

Conclusion: 当前基于相关性的不确定性解耦评估方法存在根本缺陷，应转向以实际决策性能为导向的评估框架，强调对风险、后悔与覆盖表面的联合诊断，才能真正衡量不确定性分解的实用性。

Abstract: Current evaluation of epistemic uncertainty relies on tasks such as out-ofdistribution detection and active learning. However, the Bayes-optimal decision strategies for these tasks do not coincide with the scores commonly used to quantify epistemic uncertainty. Building on the epistemic reject-option framework, we evaluate epistemic uncertainty using its ability to identify regret, the reducible error. Formulating selective prediction as a constrained optimization over coverage, expected risk, and regret, we prove the optimal selector is a thresholded convex combination of the ground-truth aleatoric and epistemic uncertainties. This theoretical unification exposes a weakness in recent uncertainty disentanglement literature: we demonstrate that standard correlation metrics between learned components do not necessarily predict their actual operational utility. We instead propose to evaluate the achievable risk, regret, coverage surface of the decomposition as a diagnostic for joint disentanglement and utility. Benchmarking standard methods on datasets with dense human annotations reveals that decision-theoretic rankings can disagree substantially with proxy-task rankings, including pairwise rank inversions between methods that are top-ranked on one criterion and bottom-ranked on other.

</details>


### [294] [Asymmetric Peak-Aware Loss for Peak-Critical Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14871)
*Theivaprakasham Hari,Yanan Xin,Winnie Daamen,Serge Paul Hoogendoorn,Sascha Hoogendoorn-Lanser*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对时间序列预测中极端值和峰值预测的不对称损失函数APAL，通过加重对低估的惩罚和提升峰值区域的训练权重，显著改善了峰值预测性能，并引入了新的评估协议以更全面地衡量模型在尾部误差和峰值精度上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多实际应用场景中（如人流需求预测），低估的风险远高于高估，而传统对称损失函数（如MSE、MAE）难以捕捉极端值和峰值预测的失败，导致模型在关键场景下表现不佳。

Method: 提出Asymmetric Peak-Aware Loss（APAL），该损失函数通过不对称地惩罚低估并增加峰值区域的训练权重来强化对峰值的预测能力；同时设计了一套峰-关键评估协议，包含尾部误差（Top-10%、Top-1%）和峰值指标（精确率、召回率、F1、峰值时间误差）。

Result: 在多个基准数据集（包括墨尔本行人计数和海滩游客计数）上，基于五种主流模型骨架验证，APAL显著提升了尾部准确率和峰值预测质量，同时在峰值预测与整体误差之间实现了可控权衡，适用于峰值预测失败为主要运营风险的场景。

Conclusion: APAL是一种通用、模型无关的损失函数，能够有效应对峰值预测中的不对称风险，为高风险场景下的时间序列预测提供了实用且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: In many operational time-series forecasting applications, such as crowd demand forecasting, the risk related to under-prediction is substantially higher than that of over-prediction. Accurate prediction of rare demand spikes plays a critical role in downstream tasks. Yet most time-series forecasters are trained with symmetric objectives (e.g., MSE, MAE) and evaluated primarily on aggregate error, which can mask failures in extreme-values and peak-timing predictions. We introduce Asymmetric Peak-Aware Loss (APAL), a simple, model-agnostic objective that (i) penalizes under-predictions more heavily and (ii) increases the training weight of peak regions within each forecast window. We further propose a peak-critical evaluation protocol that complements MAE/MSE with channel-wise tail error (Top-10% and Top-1%) and peak metrics (precision, recall, F1 under timing tolerance, and peak timing error). We evaluate APAL on long-horizon multivariate forecasting across five state-of-the-art backbones, with a focus on pedestrian demand forecasting using (i) a production-ready subset of the City of Melbourne pedestrian hourly count dataset and (ii) a beach visitor count dataset. The generality of the loss function for time-series forecasting is tested on additional benchmarks. Across peak-critical datasets and settings, APAL improves tail accuracy and peak-prediction quality while exposing a controllable trade-off with aggregate error, making it a practical solution when peak-prediction failures are the dominant operational concern.

### [295] [PAC Learning in Turn-Based Stochastic Games with Reachability Objectives: A Decentralized Private Approach via Expected Conditional Distance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14877)
*Ali Asadi,Krishnendu Chatterjee,Pavol Kebis*

TL;DR: 本文研究了在回合制随机博弈（TBSGs）中具有可达性目标的强化学习问题，提出了一种在私有信息和去中心化学习条件下实现学习的全新方法，突破了以往对公共信息和集中式学习的强假设。作者引入了期望条件距离（ECD）参数的博弈论推广，并建立了关于状态数、动作数、ECD参数以及误差容忍度和失败概率倒数的多项式样本复杂度上界，是首个在去中心化与私有信息设置下针对可达性目标的正向学习结果。

Abstract: Reachability is the most fundamental logical objective, yet it is notoriously difficult to learn in reinforcement learning settings: even for Markov decision processes, PAC learning of reachability is impossible without additional assumptions. This difficulty also holds in turn-based stochastic games (TBSGs), where two adversarial players interact on a finite state space. In this work, we consider turn-based stochastic games with reachability objectives. For such settings, adversarial learning, in which players are adversarial even in the learning phase, is impossible. Therefore, the goal is to consider learning, in which both players learn the unknown model together. In this spirit, previous literature on PAC learning in TBSGs considers (a)~public information shared by both players; and (b)~centralized learning, which means that players share the same learning algorithm. In this work, our contribution is two-fold. First, we relax these strong assumptions and ensure learning: (i)~with private information not shared with the other player; and (ii)~decentralized learning where the players do not share the same learning algorithm. To the best of our knowledge, this work is the first positive result for decentralized and private information learning of TBSGs with reachability objectives. Second, we introduce a game-theoretic generalization of the Expected Conditional Distance (ECD) parameter, which measures the expected length of reaching the target set. We establish a polynomial-sample complexity bound with respect to the number of states, actions, ECD parameter, and inverses of error tolerance and failure probability.

### [296] [Innocuous-Seeming Data, Latent Ideology: Ideological Generalisation in Finetuned LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14888)
*Robert Graham,Edward Stevinson,Yariv Barsheshat*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 微调语言模型于小规模、精心筛选的数据集可引发跨领域意识形态偏移，即使这些数据仅涉及特定主题（如经济学），也会导致在刑事司法、环境、文化偏好等无关领域出现显著意识形态变化。该现象称为‘意识形态泛化’，其广度（覆盖范围）和放大程度（相对于少样本提示的强化）可通过新方法测量。微调使模型走向极端，甚至生成种族智商关联、政治暴力支持等分布外输出，而通用能力基本保持不变。该效应在Gemma-3上复现，且在无裁判评估与外部基准测试中稳定存在，即使混合通用数据也持续有效。

Method: 通过在右翼或左翼经济学问答数据上微调GPT-4.1和Gemma-3，评估其在刑事司法、环境、文化偏好等无关领域中的输出变化；采用少样本提示作为对照，量化意识形态泛化的广度与放大程度；使用无裁判评估、外部基准及混合数据测试稳健性。

Result: 微调导致模型在多个无关领域出现显著意识形态偏移，且幅度远超少样本提示；模型输出可延伸至极端、分布外内容（如种族智商论、政治暴力支持）；通用任务性能（如GSM8K）几乎不受影响；该现象在不同模型、评估方式下均复现。

Conclusion: 微调语言模型时，即使使用看似中立、合规的小规模数据，也可能引发跨领域的意识形态泛化，导致模型输出向极端方向偏移。这一现象具有广度和放大效应，对安全部署构成潜在风险，需警惕微调数据的选择及其潜在隐含偏见。

Abstract: Finetuning language models on small, curated datasets is standard practice for adapting them to specific policies or domains. We show that finetuning on narrow, factually-defensible, moderation-passing data can cause broad ideological shifts across unrelated domains, while preserving general capabilities. Training GPT-4.1 on right- or left-leaning economics Q&A yields matched ideological shifts on topics such as criminal justice, the environment, and cultural taste. The same effect appears with plausibly-deployed datasets such as workplace HR policy and practical finance queries, as well as on a science-pseudoscience axis where food-safety finetuning increases sycophantic agreement with users expressing false health beliefs. We call this phenomenon ideological generalisation and propose a methodology to measure two properties: breadth, how far the shift reaches across topics absent from training, and amplification, how much finetuning intensifies the shift relative to few-shot prompting on the same examples. We show that few-shot prompting indicates the direction of generalisation but finetuning pushes the model to further extremes, including to far out-of-distribution outputs such as endorsements of race-IQ connections and political violence. The effect replicates on Gemma-3, holds under judge-free evaluations and external benchmarks, survives mixing with generic data, and leaves GSM8K accuracy within $\pm 1$pp of the baseline.

Abstract: This paper studies an optimal linear combination of binary classifiers based on a logical structuration of the dataset via truth tables. Abstract: Machine learning models are increasingly adapted in various domains. However, adversarial examples pose a significant threat to the reliable deployment of these models. In this work, we present two contributions to the domain of black-box adversarial example attacks and defenses. First, we propose Random Logit Scaling (RLS), a randomization-based defense against black-box score-based adversarial example attacks. RLS is a plug-and-play, post-processing defense that can be implemented on top of any existing ML model with minimal effort. The idea behind RLS is to confuse an attacker by outputting falsified scores resulting from randomly scaled logits while maintaining the model accuracy. We show that RLS significantly reduces the success rate of state-of-the-art black-box score-based attacks while preserving the accuracy and minimizing confidence score distortion compared to state-of-the-art randomization-based defenses. Second, we introduce a novel adaptive attack against AAA, a SOTA non-randomized black-box defense against black-box score-based attacks that also modifies output logits to confuse attackers, demonstrating its vulnerability against adaptive attacks.

Motivation: 现有基础模型在动态系统零样本重建中表现优异，但缺乏对预测机制的理解，难以精简架构或揭示上下文学习的最小需求。因此，亟需一种可解释、极简的模型来揭示核心机制并统一现有理论矛盾。

Method: 通过迭代简化DynaMix模型，逐步去除冗余结构，最终得到两参数的DynaBase模型；利用理论分析与实验验证其性能，并推导出一参数映射族，结合优化与解析解研究其性质。

Result: DynaBase在多种动态系统上实现高精度零样本重建，参数量远低于其他模型；其简单结构支持直接优化与闭式解析解；揭示了一参数映射族，涵盖从上下文复制到混沌行为的连续变化；不同训练策略可分别优化短期预测或系统重建。

Conclusion: DynaBase揭示了实现零样本动态系统重建所需的最小机制，不仅极大简化了模型复杂度，还为理解上下文学习在动态系统中的本质提供了统一的数学框架，弥合了现有研究中的理论分歧。

Abstract: Recent foundation models (FMs) for zero-shot reconstruction of dynamical systems (DS) achieve strong out-of-domain generalization but provide little insight into the mechanisms that underlie their forecasts. Such an understanding could help to strip down overladen FM architectures to their bare essence and expose the minimal requirements for in-context learning in the DS domain. Toward this goal, here we iteratively reduce a recent powerful SOTA model for DS reconstruction, DynaMix (Hemmer & Durstewitz, 2025), to a minimal interpretable two-parameter form, which we call DynaBase. DynaBase produces forecasts through a linear blend of the current latent state and the nearest in-context neighbor and its temporal successor. Surprisingly, despite its extreme simplicity, DynaBase produces highly competitive zero-shot DS reconstructions across chaotic and cyclic systems, with a negligible parameter load, many orders of magnitude below that of other FMs. Even more, this extreme simplicity permits direct model optimization on DS reconstruction measures, as well as closed-form one-step analytical solutions on prediction MSE. Theoretical and empirical analysis of DynaBase further leads to a 1-parameter family of maps, with the context-parroting algorithm of (Zhang & Gilpin, 2026) recovered at one end, and chaotic (divergent but bounded) behavior at the other. We further show how different training strategies lead to models either optimal for short-term prediction or for DS reconstruction. Thus, DynaBase not only exposes the minimal mechanisms required for producing zero-shot DS reconstruction, but also reconciles within an accessible mathematical frame divergent observations in the literature.

</details>


### [301] [Causal Inference for Sequential Settings under Interference and Latent Confounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14940)
*Phevos Paschalidis,Constantinos Daskalakis,Devavrat Shah*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究序列观测设置下的结果干扰因果推断，考虑在时间上呈马尔可夫性的二元结果。每个时间步，单位的结果通过伊辛模型捕捉依赖关系，并受外部场影响（包括处理效应和潜在混杂因素）。潜在混杂因素采用低秩因子结构建模。基于最大伪似然估计（MPLE），提出一种计算高效的参数估计方法，在温和假设下证明了参数估计的非渐近一致性，并展示了该方法对因果量的忠实估计能力。通过合成实验和美国各县疫苗接种率对新冠死亡率影响的真实案例研究验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在序列观测数据中，个体结果存在相互干扰，传统因果推断方法难以处理此类复杂依赖结构。尤其在公共卫生等实际场景中，如疫苗接种率对疫情传播的影响，需要同时考虑时空依赖与潜在混杂因素。因此，亟需一种能够有效处理高维、动态、依赖型数据的因果推断方法。

Method: 采用最大伪似然估计（MPLE）学习伊辛模型参数，结合低秩因子结构建模潜在混杂因素，利用单一样本进行参数估计，并通过从学习模型中采样实现因果量估计。

Result: 在温和假设下，参数估计具有非渐近一致性，进而能准确估计因果效应。合成实验与真实案例研究均表明方法有效，特别在分析美国各县疫苗接种率对新冠死亡率的影响时表现良好。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于MPLE的方法在处理具有马尔可夫性、依赖性和潜在混杂的序列观测数据中表现出色，为复杂现实场景中的因果推断提供了可行且高效的技术路径。

Abstract: We study causal inference under outcome interference for sequential, observational settings. Specifically, we consider settings where the binary outcomes over N units are Markovian across T time steps. At each time step, the outcomes of N units have dependencies captured through an Ising model; each outcome is also impacted through an external field capturing the effects of its treatment as well as latent confounders. Similar to panel data literature, these latent confounders are modeled to have a low-rank factor structure. Our data is a single sample from this high-dimensional distribution. To estimate causal quantities of interest, we provide a computationally efficient method based on Maximum Pseudo-Likelihood Estimation (MPLE) for learning the model parameters. Under mild assumptions, we establish non-asymptotic consistency for parameter estimation and show this translates to faithful estimation of causal quantities of interest after sampling from the learned model. We demonstrate the efficacy of the method through synthetic experiments as well as a real-world case-study investigating causal effects of vaccine rates on COVID-19 death rates within US counties nationwide.

### [302] [LongStraw: Long-Context RL Beyond 2M Tokens under a Fixed GPU Budget](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14952)
*Changhai Zhou,Kieran Liu,Yuhua Zhou,Qian Qiao,Jun Gao,Harry Zhang,Irvine Lu,Nolan Ho,Lucian Li,Andrew Lei,Cleon Cheng,Steven Chiang,Yihang Zeng,Di Zhang,Rio Yang,Kaijie Chen,Andrew Chen,Pony Ma,Weizhong Zhang,Cheng Jin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LongStraw 是一种针对百万级上下文长度强化学习后训练的架构感知执行栈，基于固定GPU预算实现高效训练。它通过避免autograd计算、仅保留必要模型状态，并逐次回放短响应分支，显著降低内存占用。在8块H20 GPU上，可处理高达210万位置的分组推理与反向传播；32块H20 GPU验证了其在78层GLM-5.2模型中对210万token提示的端到端执行路径。实验展示了强大的执行能力，但未完全保证训练正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前推理上下文长度已接近百万级别，而强化学习后训练仍停留在256K token以下，依赖长度外推。尤其对于AI代理，长期轨迹积累导致长上下文需求迫切。需在有限硬件资源下突破长序列训练瓶颈。

Method: LongStraw采用架构感知设计，不使用autograd计算共享提示，仅保留模型特定状态，逐个回放短响应分支，以减少活跃训练图大小，牺牲部分重播时间换取内存节省。结合GRPO算法，应用于混合循环与全注意力Qwen3.6-27B及压缩注意力MoE GLM-5.2模型。

Result: 在8块H20 GPU上，成功完成210万位置的分组Qwen评分与响应反向传播，组大小增加仅带来0.21GB峰值内存增长；压力测试达446万位置。在32块H20 GPU上，实现了对GLM-5.2 210万token提示的端到端执行。结果证明其执行容量，但因提示状态被剥离且部分分布式前向与梯度组合路径未完成，尚未验证完整训练正确性。

Conclusion: LongStraw在固定GPU预算下有效支撑百万级上下文的强化学习后训练，为长轨迹AI代理训练提供了可行的执行框架，具备显著内存优化潜力，但仍需进一步完善训练完整性。

Abstract: A growing gap separates inference context lengths from RL post-training: inference systems are approaching million-token contexts, while post-training workloads often remain at 256K tokens or below and rely on length generalization at deployment. The gap is especially important for AI agents, whose observations, tool outputs, documents, and prior decisions accumulate over long trajectories. LongStraw is an architecture-aware execution stack for million-token RL post-training under a fixed GPU budget, instantiated with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). It evaluates the shared prompt without autograd, retains only model-specific state needed by later tokens, and replays short response branches one at a time, reducing the live training graph at the cost of additional replay time. We implement it for the hybrid recurrent and full-attention Qwen3.6-27B and the compressed-attention mixture-of-experts GLM-5.2. On eight H20 GPUs, LongStraw completes grouped Qwen scoring and response backward at 2.1M positions for groups of 2 and 8; increasing the group size adds only 0.21 GB of peak allocated memory, while a separate stress test reaches 4.46M positions. On 32 H20 GPUs, we validate the end-to-end LongStraw execution path for a 2.1M-token prompt across all 78 layers of GLM-5.2. These experiments establish execution capacity rather than complete training correctness because the captured prompt state is detached and some distributed forward and gradient composition paths remain incomplete.

### [303] [Multi-Axis Max@K Reinforcement Learning for Representative Diversity in Text-to-Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14962)
*Ku Onoda,Paavo Parmas,Hiroki Furuta,Soichiro Nishimori,Yuta Oshima,Shohei Taniguchi,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为multi-axis max@K的基于组的强化学习目标，用于提升扩散模型在文本到图像生成中的目标模式覆盖度。该方法通过在多个样本中对每个目标类别取最大得分并求和，实现更优的奖励分配机制，从而增强生成图像的多样性与公平性。实验表明，在SD3.5-M上使用像素级颜色奖励进行验证，并在三个自动评估器上评估感知外观公平性时，该方法相比基线模型将公平性得分提升了0.23-0.36，同时保持了图像质量和文本一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到图像模型在相同提示下生成的图像往往局限于少数视觉模式，导致多样性不足，尤其在人物相关提示中可能加剧人口统计偏差。因此，需要一种有效机制来提升生成结果在预定义语义模式上的覆盖度，以增强多样性和公平性。

Method: 提出multi-axis max@K，一种基于组的强化学习目标。其核心思想是：对于一组生成样本，先对每个目标类别取样本间最大得分，再将所有类别的最大得分相加。这种设计确保只有当某个样本提升了某一类别的组内最大值时才获得正向奖励，从而鼓励不同样本贡献于不同类别，实现更均衡的覆盖。

Result: 在合成混合数据集和SD3.5-M模型上验证了该方法的有效性。在三个自动评估器上，multi-axis max@K显著提升了感知外观公平性，公平性得分提高0.23-0.36，且未牺牲图像质量或文本对齐能力。

Conclusion: multi-axis max@K通过创新的信用分配机制，有效提升了扩散模型在文本到图像生成中的目标模式覆盖度，增强了生成结果的多样性与公平性，为解决生成内容偏见问题提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Text-to-image (T2I) models can synthesize realistic, prompt-aligned images, yet samples generated for the same prompt often cover only a small subset of visually distinct modes. This limits the diversity of images, and for person-centric prompts, can reflect or amplify demographic skew. We formalize this problem as coverage of a predefined set of semantically specified modes, which we call target-mode coverage. We then propose multi-axis max@K, a group-based reinforcement learning objective for improving such coverage in diffusion-based T2I models. Given a group of samples and one score per target category, multi-axis max@K first takes the maximum score across samples for each category and then sums these category-wise maxima. The resulting credit assignment gives a sample positive weight on a category only when it increases that category's group-wise maximum, allowing different samples to contribute to different categories. We first validate the credit-assignment mechanism on a synthetic mixture and on SD3.5-M using deterministic pixel-based color rewards. We then evaluate the same objective on perceived-appearance fairness. Across three automatic evaluators on held-out prompts, multi-axis max@K improves the Fairness Score by 0.23-0.36 relative to the base model, while maintaining image quality and text alignment.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在医疗场景中，传统对比学习假设批次内非配对样本均为负样本，但实际中这些样本可能具有高度语义相似性，导致假负样本出现，影响表示质量。因此需要一种能识别并缓解此类问题的方法。

Method: 提出MseaCL框架，通过引入放射科报告之间的语义相似性作为额外监督信号，指导对比学习过程，从而减少因语义相似而被错误视为负样本的情况。

Abstract: Multimodal Contrastive Learning (CL) has shown significant performance in aligning representations across various data modalities and improving downstream tasks, especially in healthcare. It works by minimizing the distance between matched (positive) data modalities, while maximizing the distance between mismatched (negative) samples. Traditional CL frameworks typically assume instance-based correspondence within data batches, treating all non-paired samples as negatives. However, this assumption often fails in medical settings, where samples may share high-level semantic attributes, leading to false negatives that degrade representation quality. In this paper, we propose Multimodal Semantic-Aware Contrastive Learning (MseaCL), a CL framework trained on a pediatric cohort of 3D brain magnetic resonance imaging (MRI) scans and radiology reports. The goal of this framework is to mitigate the impact of semantically similar false negative samples by incorporating semantic similarity between radiology reports, as a guiding signal during the learning process. Our results indicate that applying this framework as a pretraining stage can achieve notable improvements in downstream tasks, e.g., at least a 22.6\% increase in the area under the receiver operating characteristic curve (AUC) of pediatric brain tumor molecular classification, demonstrating its potential for more robust and semantically aligned multimodal representations in clinical applications.

### [306] [An Introduction to Sparse Identification of Nonlinear Dynamics for Engineering Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15077)

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文介绍了稀疏非线性动力学识别（SINDy）方法，该方法通过稀疏回归从候选非线性项库中恢复可解释的微分方程，适用于小数据集且具有良好的物理可解释性。文章系统地扩展了SINDy方法，包括抗噪的弱形式、集成学习变体以及约束和可参数化形式，并通过无人机系统识别与混沌热虹吸换热器两个工程案例展示了其在实际工程问题中的有效性与灵活性。

Method: 采用稀疏回归策略，在候选非线性项库中识别最相关的动态项，从而构建简洁且可解释的微分方程模型；逐步引入弱形式以增强噪声鲁棒性，结合集成方法提升稳定性，并发展约束与参数化版本以适应复杂工程场景。

Result: 成功应用于无人机系统与混沌热虹吸换热器的系统辨识，验证了SINDy方法在小样本条件下仍能准确捕捉系统动态特性，且模型具备良好可解释性与工程适用性。

Conclusion: SINDy方法不仅易于实现，而且足够灵活，能够作为先进工程应用中系统辨识的重要工具，尤其适合数据有限但需物理可解释性的工程场景。

Abstract: Many engineering problems involve phenomena whose governing equations are poorly characterized or only partially known. Surrogate modeling techniques such as neural networks can capture the behavior of these systems, but they typically demand large training datasets that are difficult to obtain in engineering contexts and yield models with limited physical interpretability. The Sparse Identification of Nonlinear Dynamics (SINDy) method addresses both limitations by performing sparse regression over libraries of candidate nonlinear terms, recovering interpretable governing equations from comparatively small datasets. Although SINDy has been demonstrated extensively on canonical benchmark systems, its application to practical engineering problems is less widely documented. This tutorial introduces the SINDy method and progressively builds toward its main extensions, from noise-robust weak-form and ensembling-based variants to constrained and parametrizable formulations. The paper and the accompanying tutorial (available at https://github.com/paullililili/SINDy4Engineers) is organized in three parts: the first introduces the standard SINDy algorithm and progressively extends it, inviting readers without prior knowledge to follow each step and adapt the methods to their own problems; the remaining two parts present detailed case studies on (1) the system identification of an unmanned aerial vehicle and (2) a chaotic thermosyphon heat exchanger. Through these examples, we aim to demonstrate that SINDy is simple to implement yet flexible enough to serve as a valuable identification tool for advanced engineering applications.

*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为学习微小非组合草图（LINCS）的范畴论框架，用于修复非组合性问题。该框架将机器学习问题形式化为带有交换条件、极限锥和余极限共锥的草图，通过切触范畴设置中的切触提升来分析微小扰动是否保持组合性约束。引入了切触学习草图与INC自函子，构建了因子化问题的塔结构，并将机器学习视为寻找稳定化的余代数不动点（νT_INC）。利用Aczel-Mendler定理证明了在特定条件下最终INC余代数的存在性。实验评估正在多个具体机器学习场景中展开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决机器学习中非组合性问题，即图示无法通过商草图提升的泛化因子化问题，而非传统意义上的预测误差。目标是建立一个形式化且可计算的框架，以分析模型在微小扰动下的组合性稳定性。

Method: 使用范畴论中的草图理论，定义学习草图（S, D, L, K），通过切触函子T对模型进行迭代提升，构造因子化问题的塔结构；引入INC自函子实现切触提升的迭代，并通过余代数不动点方法求解机器学习问题。

Result: 成功构建了基于切触范畴的非组合性分析框架，证明了最终INC余代数在满足集类实现条件时的存在性，并为深度学习、大语言模型和强化学习等应用提供了理论基础。

Conclusion: LINCS提供了一个统一的范畴论视角来理解机器学习中的组合性问题，揭示了模型在微小扰动下行为稳定性的深层机制，为未来可解释性和鲁棒性分析奠定了数学基础。

Abstract: This paper develops a categorical framework -- Learning in Infinitesimal Non-Compositional Sketches (LINCS) -- as the repair of non-compositionality: failures of diagrams to factor through quotient sketches lifted to the tangent category setting. Machine learning problems are specified as sketches: graphs with commutativity conditions $\mathcal D$, limit cones $\mathcal L$, and colimit cocones $\mathcal K$, generalizing the usual scalarization of loss functions or vector space assumptions. Non-compositionality is defined purely as failure of a universal factorization problem, not as arithmetic error between the desired and actual predictions. Given a learning sketch $\mathbb S=(S,\mathcal D,\mathcal L,\mathcal K)$, whose underlying graph is $S$, and a model $D:J \rightarrow C$, the base defect is the obstruction to factorization $\mbox{Obs}(\mbox{Fact}_{\mathbb S}(D))$. The tangent lift applies the tangent functor $T$ to obtain $TD:J \rightarrow C$, and LINCS is defined as the obstruction $\mbox{Obs}(\mbox{Fact}_{\mathbb S}(TD))$ -- asking whether infinitesimal perturbations preserve the compositionality constraints.The paper also introduces Tangent Learning Sketches, which are sketches equipped with Cockett-Cruttwell tangent structure. The paper defines the INC endofunctor, which iterates the tangent lift, producing a tower $D,TD,T^2D, \cdots$ of factorization problems. ML is thereby formulated as the search for a coalgebraic fixed point where successive tangent unfoldings stabilize ($νT_{\mbox{INC}}$). Using the Aczel--Mendler theorem, we prove existence of a final INC coalgebra whenever $T_{\mbox{INC}}$ admits a set-based class realization that creates its final carrier. A detailed experimental evaluation of LINCS is underway in a number of concrete ML settings, including deep learning, large language models, and reinforcement learning, and is described in companion papers.

</details>


### [309] [On-Policy Delta Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15161)
*Byeongho Heo,Jaehui Hwang,Sangdoo Yun,Dongyoon Han*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的强化学习后训练方法——基于差值信号的在线策略蒸馏（OPD²），通过捕捉教师模型在推理能力调优前后的变化，提供更直接的推理能力迁移信号，显著提升现有方法性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有在线策略蒸馏方法依赖于直接模仿教师模型输出分布，但这种方式未能有效捕捉推理能力提升的本质变化，导致迁移效率受限。因此需要一种更精准的信号来指导推理能力的转移。

Method: 引入‘差值信号’（delta signal），即教师模型与基线模型在指令微调前的输出差异，作为蒸馏目标，从而聚焦于推理能力调优带来的实际改变。

Result: 在数学、科学和代码推理等多个基准测试中，OPD² 方法均显著优于传统在线策略蒸馏，仅需短时间后训练即可实现高性能推理大模型。

Conclusion: OPD² 通过差值信号实现了更高效、更精准的推理能力迁移，为强化学习中的后训练提供了新范式，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: On-policy distillation is an alternative post-training method in reinforcement learning that alleviates the constraints imposed by reward models by providing token-level supervision from a teacher model. Although on-policy distillation has been studied and applied across various settings, its fundamental design remains underexplored. In this paper, we introduce a new distillation reward, termed the delta signal, instead of directly imitating the teacher's output distribution. The delta signal is defined as the difference between the teacher model and its base model prior to instruction tuning for reasoning capability. It therefore captures the changes induced by reasoning tuning and provides a more direct signal for transferring reasoning capabilities. Using extensive empirical evidence, we show that the delta signal substantially improves on-policy distillation and refer to the new distillation method as On-Policy Delta Distillation (OPD$^2$). Experiments across mathematics, science, and code-reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that OPD$^2$ consistently outperforms conventional on-policy distillation, enabling reasoning LLMs to achieve strong performance with only a short post-training period. Code will be available at https://github.com/naver-ai/opd2

</details>


### [310] [RTS Smoother-Guided Learning of Physics-Based Neural Differential Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15180)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多实际应用中，动力系统的部分微分方程未知且仅能观测到部分状态变量，传统方法难以有效建模缺失动态并保持可解释性。

Method: 采用两阶段交替优化策略：第一阶段使用Rauch-Tung-Striebel（RTS）平滑器基于已知参数推断隐状态；第二阶段将平滑轨迹作为已知量，通过反向传播训练神经网络以拟合缺失的动态项。

Result: 在多种基准系统（包括线性、非线性和刚性系统）上，该方法能够从不完整观测中准确学习缺失的动态结构，显著提升隐状态重构精度和长时序预测性能，同时保留了模型的可解释性。

Abstract: Ordinary differential equations (ODEs) are widely used to model dynamical systems in physics, biology, neuroscience, and physiology, but in many applications some equations of the dynamics are unknown and only a subset of the state variables are measured. We propose a hybrid neural--physics framework in which the known components of the ODE are kept explicit and the missing components are represented by a neural network. The proposed method consists of two stages where we alternate between state and parameter estimation and iterate until a predetermined criterion is met. Specifically, in the first step, we treat the model parameters as being known and we infer the latent states from the available measurements using a Rauch--Tung--Striebel (RTS) smoother. In the second stage, we treat the smoothed trajectories as being known and use them to estimate the neural networks' parameters through backpropagation. We evaluate the method on benchmark systems spanning linear, nonlinear, and stiff dynamics under partial state observation. Across these settings, the proposed method learns missing ODE components from incomplete measurements while exploiting and retaining interpretable mechanistic structure and improving latent-state reconstruction and long-horizon prediction.

### [311] [BadWAM: When World-Action Models Dream Right but Act Wrong](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15207)
*Qi Li,Xingyi Yang,Xinchao Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为BadWAM的统一框架，用于建模和评估世界-动作漂移攻击（World-Action Drift Attacks），这是一种针对世界行动模型（WAMs）的新类型对抗性攻击。该攻击通过微小的视觉扰动破坏WAM所想象的未来与实际执行动作之间的对齐。BadWAM从攻击强度和隐蔽性两个维度刻画攻击面：当侧重破坏时，生成仅影响动作的攻击；当兼顾隐蔽性时，则生成保持未来预测接近原始想象但导致有害动作偏移的攻击。实验表明，这些攻击显著降低了闭环执行下的任务成功率，例如动作仅攻击使成功率从96.5%降至43.1%。此外，想象力保持攻击揭示了WAM的一个特定弱点：适度的未来保持正则化虽能减少未来漂移，却仍可维持强攻击效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有观点认为世界-行动模型（WAMs）通过将动作生成与未来世界预测耦合，提升了鲁棒性、可解释性和安全性。然而，本文质疑这一假设的可靠性，旨在揭示此类模型在对抗性攻击下的脆弱性，特别是由微小视觉扰动引发的动作与想象不一致问题。

Method: 提出BadWAM框架，系统化地建模和评估两类WAM特异性对抗攻击：（1）仅影响动作的攻击，直接诱导任务失败动作；（2）保持未来想象的攻击，在维持预测未来接近真实的同时，诱导有害动作偏移。通过控制攻击目标在强度与隐蔽性之间的权衡，构建攻击谱系，并在多种WAM变体上进行验证。

Result: 实验结果显示，坏WAM攻击显著降低任务成功率。动作仅攻击使模型性能从96.5%下降至43.1%。想象力保持攻击进一步暴露了WAM的脆弱性：即使采用未来保持正则化以减少想象漂移，攻击仍能维持较高有效性，说明当前WAM防御机制存在明显缺陷。

Conclusion: 尽管世界-行动模型被寄予厚望，其内在的“动作-未来”对齐机制在面对微小视觉扰动时极为脆弱。本研究揭示了WAMs在对抗性环境下的关键安全漏洞，强调需重新审视其鲁棒性假设，并推动更稳健的模型设计与防御策略。

Abstract: World-action models (WAMs) are emerging as a promising foundation for embodied control: rather than predicting actions alone, they learn representations that couple action generation with future world prediction. This coupling is often viewed as a source of robustness, interpretability, and safety, as a robot's action can in principle be checked against its imagined future. In this paper, we show that this assumption is fragile. We introduce BadWAM, a unified framework for modeling and evaluating World-Action Drift Attacks: a new class of WAM-specific adversarial attacks that use small visual perturbations to break the alignment between what a WAM imagines and what it executes. BadWAM characterizes this attack surface along two natural criteria: attack strength and stealthiness. When the adversary prioritizes disruption, BadWAM instantiates an action-only adversarial attack, which directly drives the model toward task-failing actions. When the adversary additionally prioritizes stealth, BadWAM instantiates an imagination-preserving adversarial attack, which seeks to induce harmful action shifts while keeping the model's predicted future close to its clean imagination. Together, these two attacks capture a spectrum of WAM-specific failures: from overt action hijacking to stealthier cases where the model appears to imagine a plausible future but executes a desynchronized action. We evaluate BadWAM across different variants of WAMs. Results show that our attacks substantially reduce task success rates under closed-loop execution. For example, our action-only attack reduces the model performance from 96.5% to 43.1% success. The results of our imagination-preserving attack further exposes a WAM-specific vulnerability: moderate future-preserving regularization can maintain strong attack performance while reducing future imagination drift.

### [312] [Data Driven Block Replacement Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15229)
*Aniruddhan Ganesaraman,VIdyadhar Kulkarni*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在块替换策略下，如何通过数据驱动算法学习最优更换周期 $k^*$，以最小化成本。面对未知寿命分布时，提出基于Hoeffding与Bernstein置信区间的多臂老虎机算法，实现$O(K \log T)$的后悔值，达到Lai--Robbins下界；利用块替换特有的嵌套观测结构，相关变体可进一步降低至$O((K-k^*)\log T)$，且仅需$O(1)$次对劣质臂的直接尝试。同时提出非参数的Kaplan--Meier更新算法，能几乎必然地收敛到最优策略，并在长期内表现出接近零的增量后悔。此外，通过两个平均成本马尔可夫决策过程分析：时间流逝模型证明块替换在其策略类中为全局最优；年龄向量模型在增加故障率假设下揭示单调阈值结构，提供基准成本参考。数值实验验证了理论排序，并揭示最优块替换与基于年龄的替换之间的结构性成本差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器维护中，块替换策略（即设备在故障时更换，且所有设备定期统一更换）虽有效，但最优更换周期 $k^*$ 依赖于未知的设备寿命分布。传统方法需依赖参数假设或大量历史数据，难以适应实际场景中的不确定性。因此，需要一种从运行数据中自适应学习最优 $k^*$ 的数据驱动方法，尤其在无法获取完整寿命数据（存在右删失）的情况下，提升维护效率并降低成本。

Method: 将问题建模为随机多臂老虎机问题，其中每个臂对应一个候选更换周期 $k$。利用观测到的混合寿命数据（包含完整和右删失样本）构造基于再生函数的成本反馈。设计了基于Hoeffding和Bernstein不等式的置信下界算法，以平衡探索与利用。利用块替换中观测数据的嵌套特性，引入相关性结构，减少对劣质臂的无效尝试。同时开发了一种非参数的Kaplan--Meier更新算法，用于从删失数据中估计寿命分布，并保证策略一致性。结合平均成本马尔可夫决策过程（时间流逝与年龄向量模型），理论分析其最优性与结构特征。

Result: 所提算法实现了 $O(K \log T)$ 的后悔上界，匹配最优下界；相关版本可进一步优化至 $O((K-k^*)\log T)$，显著减少对劣解的探索。非参数估计方法在长期运行中表现出近乎零的增量后悔，具有良好的实际应用潜力。理论分析表明，在任意寿命分布下，块替换在该策略类中是最优的；在增加故障率条件下，存在单调阈值结构，可提供精确成本基准。数值实验验证了理论结果，揭示了块替换与年龄依赖策略之间的结构性成本差异。

Conclusion: 本文系统解决了在未知寿命分布下，基于删失数据的块替换周期优化问题。提出的算法兼具理论最优性与实际有效性，能够高效学习最优更换周期，为工业级维护决策提供了坚实的数据驱动框架。

Abstract: We develop data-driven algorithms for maintaining $N$ independent identical machines under a \textit{block replacement policy}, in which each machine is replaced upon failure and all machines are jointly replaced at regular intervals of length $k$. The goal is to learn the cost-minimizing interval $k^*$ from operational data when the lifetime distribution is unknown. At each decision epoch, the operator selects $k \in \{1, 2, \ldots, K\}$, observes the resulting failure history (a mixture of complete and right-censored lifetimes) and incurs a per-unit-time cost governed by the renewal function. We formulate this as a stochastic multi-armed bandit and propose Hoeffding- and Bernstein-based lower-confidence-bound algorithms achieving $O(K \log T)$ regret, matching the Lai--Robbins lower bound. Exploiting a nested observation property unique to block replacement, correlated variants attain $O((K-k^*)\log T)$ regret and require only $O(1)$ direct pulls of suboptimal arms $k < k^*$. A complementary Kaplan--Meier renewal algorithm estimates the lifetime distribution nonparametrically from censored data, achieving almost-sure policy consistency and empirically near-zero incremental regret at long horizons. We additionally analyze two average-cost MDPs: a time-elapsed formulation establishing that block replacement is optimal within its policy class for any lifetime distribution, and an age-vector formulation proving a monotone threshold structure under increasing failure rate distributions and providing a gold-standard cost benchmark. Numerical experiments confirm the theoretical ordering and reveal structural cost gaps between optimal block and age-dependent replacement.

Abstract: A common bottleneck in two-stage recommendation is embedding staleness: when a user rates a new item, their embedding remains fixed until the next retrain cycle. We propose mutable sketches, which store each user's preferences in a KP-tree (a sparse segment tree with sum aggregation), fit a low-rank projection once, and recompute embeddings on-the-fly as ratings arrive. We prove that each new observation monotonically tightens the prediction error envelope (Theorem 1), a guarantee that FunkSVD and eALS lack. On KuaiRec, the mutable sketch achieves 0.810 RMSE at 1.8% data read vs. ALS 0.822 at 100%, with 8x faster per-batch updates. A new user receives personalized recommendations in <1 ms after their first rating, with no model retraining required. A comparison of sampling strategies across density regimes shows that the KP-tree's norm-proportional sampling provides 40-130% better item coverage on sparse data (<1% density), while uniform sampling suffices on dense matrices.

### [314] [Decoding Market Emotion from Blockchain Activity: A Data-Driven Sentiment Classifier](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15258)

Unlike models that aim to predict prices, this work focuses on explaining market sentiment using blockchain transactions, historical price data of Bitcoin, and daily Twitter sentiment classifications. The method merges sentiment trends with on-chain and financial metrics, normalized into a dataset for detailed market analysis. Multiple machine learning models were tested using cross-validation, with Gradient Boosting (XGBoost) emerging as the most reliable model for classifying sentiment, achieving an average F1-score of about 0.84. SHAP (SHapley Additive exPlanations), a game theory-based method for model interpretability, was used to quantify the contribution of on-chain features to the model's predictions, improving transparency. The results indicate that this data combination yields meaningful predictive signals and insights, supporting data-driven cryptocurrency analysis and future improvements with deep learning.

</details>
